''' Component: usrForm
'================================================================================
' UserForm:     usrForm (code-behind)
' Purpose:      Provides a simple "console" text box for program output.
'               - ClearConsole resets text
'               - Prt / PrtLn append text (with optional leading space)
'
' Notes:        Keeps UI responsive when CPU!Step=1 (DoEvents on write).
' Source:       Stable snapshot (2026-02-12 18:38)
'================================================================================
Private Declare PtrSafe Function SendMessage Lib "user32" Alias "SendMessageA" (ByVal hwnd As LongPtr, ByVal wMsg As Long, ByVal wParam As LongPtr, lParam As Any) As LongPtr
    
Private Const WM_VSCROLL As Long = &H115
Private Const SB_BOTTOM As Long = 7
Private pSendText As Boolean

Public Sub ClearConsole()
    Me.tbConsole.Locked = False
    Me.tbConsole.text = vbNullString
    Me.tbConsole.Locked = True
    Me.tbConsole.SelStart = 0
    Range("consoleText") = ""
    
  ' NEW: authoritative buffer clear
    ConsoleBuffer_Clear

End Sub

Public Sub ConPrtLn(ByVal data As String, Optional ByVal prtSpace As Boolean = False)
    With Me.tbConsole
        .Locked = False
        ' Append text
        .value = .value & IIf(Len(.value) > 0 And prtSpace, " ", "") & data & vbCrLf
        
        ' Force Focus and Scroll
        .SetFocus
        .SelStart = Len(.value)
        SendMessage CreateObject("WScript.Shell").SendKeys("{PGDN}"), 0, 0, 0 ' Fallback helper
        
        ' The most reliable method for MSForms:
        .CurLine = .LineCount - 1
        
        .Locked = True
    End With
    
    ' Force the UserForm to process the visual change
    Me.Repaint
    If Sheets("CPU").Range("Step").value = 1 Then DoEvents
End Sub

Public Sub ConPrt(ByVal data As String, Optional ByVal prtSpace As Boolean = False)
    With Me.tbConsole
        .Locked = False
        .value = .value & IIf(Len(.value) > 0 And prtSpace, " ", "") & data
        
        .SetFocus
        .SelStart = Len(.value)
        
        If .LineCount > 0 Then .CurLine = .LineCount - 1
        
        .Locked = True
    End With
    
     Me.Repaint
    If Sheets("CPU").Range("Step").value = 1 Then DoEvents
        
End Sub

Public Function ConReadByte() As Byte
    Dim wsUnitTest As Worksheet
    Set wsUnitTest = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("Unit Tests")
    Dim outByte As Byte
    Dim power As Long
    outByte = 0
    
    If Me.tgl7.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 128
    End If
    If Me.tgl6.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 64
    End If
    If Me.tgl5.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 32
    End If
    If Me.tgl4.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 16
    End If
    If Me.tgl3.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 8
    End If
    If Me.tgl2.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 4
    End If
    If Me.tgl1.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 2
    End If
    If Me.tgl0.value Then
        outByte = outByte Or 1
    End If
    Me.txtLights.text = outByte
    Dim i As Integer
    Dim rangeName As String
    
    power = 1
    For i = 0 To 7
        rangeName = "SW_" & i
        If (outByte And power) = power Then
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 1
        Else
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 0
        End If
        power = power * 2
    Next i
        
        
    ConReadByte = outByte
End Function
Public Sub ConSetByte(ByVal inByte)
    Dim wsUnitTest As Worksheet
    Set wsUnitTest = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("Unit Tests")

    If (inByte And 1) = 1 Then
        Me.tgl0.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl0.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 2) = 2 Then
        Me.tgl1.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl1.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 4) = 4 Then
        Me.tgl2.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl2.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 8) = 8 Then
        Me.tgl3.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl3.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 16) = 16 Then
        Me.tgl4.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl4.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 32) = 32 Then
        Me.tgl5.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl5.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 64) = 64 Then
        Me.tgl6.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl6.value = False
    End If
    If (inByte And 128) = 128 Then
        Me.tgl7.value = True
    Else
        Me.tgl7.value = False
    End If
    
    Dim power As Long
    Dim i As Long
    Dim rangeName As String
    power = 1
    For i = 0 To 7
        rangeName = "SW_" & i
        If (inByte And power) = power Then
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 1
        Else
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 0
        End If
        power = power * 2
    Next i
    
    Me.Repaint

End Sub
Public Sub ConSetLights(ByVal inByte)
    Dim wsUnitTest As Worksheet
    Set wsUnitTest = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("Unit Tests")

    If (inByte And 1) = 1 Then
        Me.txt0.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt0.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 2) = 2 Then
        Me.txt1.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt1.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 4) = 4 Then
        Me.txt2.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt2.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 8) = 8 Then
        Me.txt3.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt3.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 16) = 16 Then
        Me.txt4.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt4.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 32) = 32 Then
        Me.txt5.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt5.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 64) = 64 Then
        Me.txt6.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt6.BackColor = 0
    End If
    If (inByte And 128) = 128 Then
        Me.txt7.BackColor = 65535
    Else
        Me.txt7.BackColor = 0
    End If
    
    Dim power As Long
    Dim i As Long
    Dim rangeName As String
    power = 1
    For i = 0 To 7
        rangeName = "LT_" & i
        If (inByte And power) = power Then
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 1
        Else
            wsUnitTest.Range(rangeName) = 0
        End If
        power = power * 2
    Next i
    
    Me.Repaint
End Sub

Public Sub ResetConsole()
    ConSetByte 0
    ConSetLights 0
    ClearConsole
End Sub

Public Sub ResetSendText()
    pSendText = False
End Sub

Public Sub SendText()
    pSendText = True
End Sub

Private Sub cmdBreak_Click()
    Dim wsCPU As Worksheet
    Set wsCPU = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU")
    wsCPU.Range("Stop") = 1
    DoEvents
End Sub

Private Sub cmdEnter_Click()
    pSendText = True
End Sub

''' Component: Exportcode
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Module:       Exportcode
' Purpose:      Exports all VBA components to a single timestamped .txt file and
'               saves a binary snapshot (.xlsm) to one or more output folders.
'
' Requirements:
'   - Reference: Microsoft Visual Basic for Applications Extensibility 5.3
'   - Trust Center: "Trust access to the VBA project object model" (temporarily)
'
' Notes:        Uses late binding for VBIDE objects to reduce hard dependency.
'               Documentation/formatting only. No functional changes.
' Source:       Stable snapshot (2026-02-12 18:38)
'================================================================================

Public Sub ExportAllVbaToSingleText()
    '==============================================================================
    ' Modified ExportAllVbaToSingleText
    ' Enhancements:
    '   - Logs exports to "Export Log" worksheet
    '   - Automatically increments VersionNumber by 0.01
    '   - All files exported in this run share the same version number
    '   - Adds version number to exported filenames
    '==============================================================================
    
    Dim vbProj As Object ' late bound VBIDE.VBProject
    Dim vbComp As Object
    Dim codeMod As Object
    Dim f, g As Integer
    Dim outputDir As Variant
    Dim baseName As String
    Dim timeStamp As String
    Dim finalFileName As String
    Dim outputPath As String
    Dim outputPathStndard As String
    Dim fullPathXlsm As String
    Dim lastLine As Long
    Dim fso As Object
    
    ' Version tracking variables
    Dim currentVersion As Double
    Dim newVersion As Double
    Dim versionStr As String
    Dim exportLogWs As Worksheet
    Dim nextLogRow As Long
    Dim lastLogRow As Long
    
    ' Initialization
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    Set exportLogWs = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Export Log")
    
    ' Find the last row with data in the Export Log (starting from row 3)
    lastLogRow = 2
    Do While exportLogWs.Cells(lastLogRow + 1, 1).value <> Empty
        lastLogRow = lastLogRow + 1
    Loop
    
    ' Get the version from the last log entry, or use 1.00 if table is empty
    If lastLogRow > 2 Then
        currentVersion = CDbl(exportLogWs.Cells(lastLogRow, 1).value)
    Else
        currentVersion = 1#
    End If
    
    ' Increment version for this run
    newVersion = currentVersion + 0.01
    newVersion = Application.Round(newVersion, 2) ' Ensure proper rounding
    versionStr = Format(newVersion, "0.00")
    
    ' 1) Timestamp
    timeStamp = Format(Now, "yyyy-mm-dd_HHmm")
    
    ' 2) Workbook name without extension
    baseName = ThisWorkbook.name
    If InStrRev(baseName, ".") > 0 Then
        baseName = Left(baseName, InStrRev(baseName, ".") - 1)
    End If
    
    ' Declare variables for export loop
    Dim base As Range, saveRow As Range
    Set base = Range("Exports")
    
    ' 3) Export to all selected output directories
    For Each saveRow In base.Rows
        If saveRow.Cells(1, 1) = 1 Then
            outputDir = saveRow.Cells(1, 2)
            
            ' Ensure trailing backslash
            If Right(outputDir, 1) <> "\" Then outputDir = outputDir & "\"
            
            ' Specific file paths - WITH VERSION NUMBER
            finalFileName = baseName & "_" & timeStamp & "_v" & versionStr
            outputPath = outputDir & finalFileName & ".txt"
            fullPathXlsm = outputDir & finalFileName & ".xlsm"
            outputPathStndard = outputDir & baseName & ".txt"
            
            ' Ensure folder exists
            On Error Resume Next
            If Not fso.FolderExists(outputDir) Then fso.CreateFolder outputDir
            On Error GoTo 0
            
            ' Open the text files
            f = FreeFile
            g = FreeFile
            Open outputPath For Output As #f
            
            g = FreeFile
            Open outputPathStndard For Output As #g
            
            Set vbProj = ThisWorkbook.VBProject
            Print #f, "=== VBA EXPORT: " & ThisWorkbook.name & " ==="
            Print #f, "Timestamp: " & Now
            Print #f, "Version: " & versionStr
            Print #f, String(80, "=")
            
            Print #g, "=== VBA EXPORT: " & ThisWorkbook.name & " ==="
            Print #g, "Timestamp: " & Now
            Print #g, "Version: " & versionStr
            Print #g, String(80, "=")
    
            For Each vbComp In vbProj.VBComponents
                Set codeMod = vbComp.CodeModule
                lastLine = codeMod.CountOfLines
    
                Print #f, vbCrLf & "''' Component: " & vbComp.name
                Print #g, vbCrLf & "''' Component: " & vbComp.name
                If lastLine > 0 Then
                    Print #f, codeMod.lines(1, lastLine)
                    Print #g, codeMod.lines(1, lastLine)
                Else
                    Print #f, "''' [No code]"
                    Print #g, "''' [No code]"
                End If
            Next vbComp
    
            Close #f
            Close #g
    
            ' Binary copy of workbook (with version in filename)
            ThisWorkbook.SaveCopyAs fullPathXlsm
            
            ' Find next empty row in Export Log and write one entry per file
            nextLogRow = 3
            Do While exportLogWs.Cells(nextLogRow, 1).value <> Empty Or _
                     exportLogWs.Cells(nextLogRow, 2).value <> Empty Or _
                     exportLogWs.Cells(nextLogRow, 3).value <> Empty
                nextLogRow = nextLogRow + 1
            Loop
            
            ' Write entry for .txt file (full path)
            With exportLogWs
                .Cells(nextLogRow, 1).value = newVersion
                .Cells(nextLogRow, 2).value = Now
                .Cells(nextLogRow, 3).value = outputPath
            End With
            
            ' Write entry for .xlsm file (full path, next row)
            With exportLogWs
                .Cells(nextLogRow + 1, 1).value = newVersion
                .Cells(nextLogRow + 1, 2).value = Now
                .Cells(nextLogRow + 1, 3).value = fullPathXlsm
            End With
        End If
    Next saveRow
    
    ' Notify user
    MsgBox "Export completed!" & vbCrLf & _
           "Version " & versionStr & " - " & Format(Now, "yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss") & vbCrLf & _
           "Log entries written to Export Log sheet", _
           vbInformation, "VBA Export Complete"
    
End Sub
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' ComponentTypeName (helper used by earlier versions — preserved for reference)
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Function ComponentTypeName(typeId As VBIDE.vbext_ComponentType) As String
    Select Case typeId
        Case vbext_ct_StdModule:   ComponentTypeName = "Module"
        Case vbext_ct_ClassModule: ComponentTypeName = "Class"
        Case vbext_ct_MSForm:      ComponentTypeName = "UserForm"
        Case vbext_ct_Document:    ComponentTypeName = "Document (Sheet/Workbook)"
        Case Else:                 ComponentTypeName = CStr(typeId)
    End Select
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' CleanFileName
' Removes extension and replaces spaces with underscores.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function CleanFileName(ByVal fileName As String) As String
    Dim dotPosition As Integer

    dotPosition = InStrRev(fileName, ".")
    If dotPosition > 0 Then
        fileName = Left(fileName, dotPosition - 1)
    End If

    CleanFileName = Replace(fileName, " ", "_")
End Function


''' Component: clsDecCPU
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsDecCPU
' Purpose:      CPU core for the Excel/VBA Intel 8080 emulator.
'               - Register & flag storage
'               - Stack & label helpers (clsStack/clsLabels)
'               - Implemented 8080 subset (CALL, RET, LXI, MOV, MVI, INR, DCR,
'                 ORA, JMP + conditions, HLT, PUSH/POP incl. PSW)
'               - UI deferral to reduce paint during headless runs
'               - Console print shims (PRTN/PRTNS/PRTCRLF/PRTCRLFS)
'
' Notes:        Documentation/formatting only. No functional changes.
' Source:       Stable snapshot (2026-02-12 18:38)  ? Export reference.
'================================================================================

'--- State ---
Private pRegs As Object            ' Dictionary: registers A,B,C,D,E,H,L,PC,SP (hex strings)
Private pFlags As Object           ' Dictionary: Carry, Parity, AC, Zero, Sign, Flag (ints)
Private pStack As New clsDecStack
Private pLabels As New clsLabels
Private pPC_dec As Long            ' Internal PC in decimal
Private pNodeRec As clsAddrRecord
Private pAddressList As clsAddrList
Private pMemory As clsMemory

'--- UI deferral (headless runs) ---
Private mUIRegsDirty As Boolean
Private mUIFlagsDirty As Boolean
Private mUIStackDirty As Boolean

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' BeginDeferUI / EndDeferUI / FlushUI
' Aggregates UI writes to reduce overhead when "Step"=0.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Class_Initialize
' Initializes registers and flags to known defaults.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub Class_Initialize()
    Set pRegs = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    pRegs.ADD "A", 0
    pRegs.ADD "B", 0
    pRegs.ADD "C", 0
    pRegs.ADD "D", 0
    pRegs.ADD "E", 0
    pRegs.ADD "H", 0
    pRegs.ADD "L", 0
    pRegs.ADD "PC", 0
    pRegs.ADD "SP", &HFF

' --- NEW: Z80 Flag (F) Register---
    pRegs.ADD "F", 0

' --- NEW: Z80 Shadow Registers (The "Prime" set) ---
    pRegs.ADD "Ap", 0: pRegs.ADD "Fp", 0
    pRegs.ADD "Bp", 0: pRegs.ADD "Cp", 0
    pRegs.ADD "Dp", 0: pRegs.ADD "Ep", 0
    pRegs.ADD "Hp", 0: pRegs.ADD "Lp", 0

    ' --- NEW: Z80 Index & Special Registers ---
    pRegs.ADD "IX", 0: pRegs.ADD "IY", 0
    pRegs.ADD "I", 0:  pRegs.ADD "R", 0
    
    Set pFlags = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    pFlags.ADD "Carry", 0
    pFlags.ADD "Parity", 0
    pFlags.ADD "AC", 0
    pFlags.ADD "Zero", 0
    pFlags.ADD "Sign", 0
    pFlags.ADD "Flag", 1

' NEW: Z80 specific flags
    pFlags.ADD "N", 0 ' Add/Subtract flag for DAA
    
    Set pAddressList = gAddressList
    Set pMemory = gMemory
    
End Sub
' --- Class_Initialize ---

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' RunOpcode
' Routes a normalized opcode to its clsCPU implementation.
' Parameters:
'   myCpu  - CPU instance
'   opcode - already UCase/Trim by Execute (kept redundant for safety)
'   op1/op2 - operands (normalized by Execute)
'   curRow  - the line's Range for context (EQU label lookup)
' Returns:
'   0 on success; negative / nonzero error codes for fault/END
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function RunOpcode(ByVal opcode As String, _
    ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String, _
    Optional ByVal label As String = "") As Long

    Dim result As Long
    result = 0

    'opcode = Trim$(UCase$(opcode))
    Select Case opcode
        ' In Z80 machine code, CB is a prefix. In your row-based model,
        ' we treat the next row or the op1/op2 as the bit instruction.
        Case "CB": result = Me.CB(op1)
        Case "ADD": result = Me.ADD(op1)      ' 120xx
        Case "ADI": result = Me.ADI(op1)      ' 130xx
        Case "ANA": result = Me.ANA(op1)      ' 140xx
        Case "ANI": result = Me.ANI(op1)      ' 150xx
        Case "CMP": result = Me.CMP(op1)      ' 190xx
        Case "CPI": result = Me.CPI(op1)      ' 200xx
        Case "CALL": result = Me.CALL_(op1, op2)         ' 160xx error base inside
        Case "DB":   result = 0                              ' data pseudo-op
        Case "EQU":  result = Me.EQU(op1, label)
        Case "END":  result = ERR_EXEC_END                ' soft termination
        Case "DCR":  result = Me.DCR(op1)                 ' 230xx
        Case "HLT":  result = Me.HLT()                    ' -100
        Case "IN":   result = Me.IN_(op1)                 ' 270xx
        Case "INR":  result = Me.INR(op1)                 ' 280xx
        Case "JC":   result = Me.JC(op1)
        Case "JM":   result = Me.JM(op1)
        Case "JMP":  result = Me.JMP(op1)                 ' 300xx
        Case "JNC":  result = Me.JNC(op1)
        Case "JNZ":  result = Me.JNZ(op1)
        Case "JP":   result = Me.JP(op1, op2)              'redefined z80 operation
        Case "JPE":  result = Me.JPE(op1)
        Case "JPO":  result = Me.JPO(op1)
        Case "JZ":   result = Me.JZ(op1)
        Case "LXI":  result = Me.LXI(op1, op2)            ' 340xx
        Case "MOV":  result = Me.MOV(op1, op2)            ' 350xx
        Case "MVI":  result = Me.MVI(op1, op2)            ' 360xx
        Case "NOP":  result = Me.NOP()
        Case "ORA", "OR":  result = Me.ORA(op1)            ' 380xx
        Case "ORG":  result = Me.NOP()
        Case "ORI":  result = Me.ORI(op1)                 ' 390xx
        Case "OUT":  result = Me.OUT_(op1)                ' 400xx
        Case "POP":  result = Me.POP(op1)                 ' 420xx
        Case "PUSH": result = Me.PUSH(op1)                ' 430xx
        Case "RET":  result = Me.RET()                    ' 460xx
        
        ' --- Arithmetic with carry/borrow ---
        Case "ADC": result = Me.ADC(op1)
        Case "ACI": result = Me.ACI(op1)
        Case "SUB": result = Me.SUB_(op1)
        Case "SUI": result = Me.SUI(op1)
        Case "SBB": result = Me.SBB(op1)
        Case "SBI": result = Me.SBI(op1)
        
        ' --- Logical XOR ---
        Case "XRA": result = Me.XRA(op1)
        Case "XRI": result = Me.XRI(op1)
        
        ' --- Rotates / carry ops / complement / NOP ---
        Case "RLC": result = Me.RLC()
        Case "RRC": result = Me.RRC()
        Case "RAL": result = Me.RAL()
        Case "RAR": result = Me.RAR()
        Case "STC": result = Me.STC()
        Case "CMC": result = Me.CMC()
        Case "CMA": result = Me.CMA()
        
        ' --- 16-bit register-pair ops ---
        Case "INX": result = Me.INX(op1)
        Case "DCX": result = Me.DCX(op1)
        Case "DAD": result = Me.DAD(op1)
        Case "DAA": result = Me.DAA()
        
        ' --- Register pair exchanges / flow helpers ---
        Case "XCHG": result = Me.XCHG()
        Case "SPHL": result = Me.SPHL()
        Case "PCHL": result = Me.PCHL()
        
        ' --- Conditional CALL ---
        Case "CZ":  result = Me.CCOND("Z", op1)
        Case "CNZ": result = Me.CCOND("NZ", op1)
        Case "CC":  result = Me.CCOND("C", op1)
        Case "CNC": result = Me.CCOND("NC", op1)
        Case "CM":  result = Me.CCOND("M", op1)
        Case "CPE": result = Me.CCOND("PE", op1)
        Case "CPO": result = Me.CCOND("PO", op1)
        
        ' --- Conditional RET ---
        Case "RZ":  result = Me.RCOND("Z")
        Case "RNZ": result = Me.RCOND("NZ")
        Case "RC":  result = Me.RCOND("C")
        Case "RNC": result = Me.RCOND("NC")
        Case "RP":  result = Me.RCOND("P")
        Case "RM":  result = Me.RCOND("M")
        Case "RPE": result = Me.RCOND("PE")
        Case "RPO": result = Me.RCOND("PO")
        
        ' --- address routines from
        Case "LDA":  result = Me.LDA(op1)
        Case "STA":  result = Me.STA(op1)
        Case "LHLD": result = Me.LHLD(op1)
        Case "SHLD": result = Me.SHLD(op1)
        Case "LDAX": result = Me.LDAX(op1)
        Case "STAX": result = Me.STAX(op1)
        Case "XTHL": result = Me.XTHL()
        ' --- IO ops (non standard 8080) ---
        Case "PRI": result = Me.PRI(op1)
        Case "PRT": result = Me.PRT()
        ' --- New Z80 Exchanges ---
        Case "EX": result = Me.EX(op1, op2)
        Case "EXX": result = Me.EXX
        Case "SRL": result = SRL(op1)
        
        ' --- Unified Z80 LD Logic ---
        Case "LD": result = LD(op1, op2)
        Case "CP": result = Me.cp(op1, op2)
        
        ' --- Bit Operations ---
        Case "BIT": result = Me.BIT(op1, op2)
        Case "SET": result = Me.SET_BIT(op1, op2)
        Case "RES": result = Me.RES_BIT(op1, op2)
        Case Else
            result = -9999                                   ' unrecognized opcode
    End Select

    RunOpcode = result
End Function
' ---  ---
' End RunOpcode

'==============================================================================
'                       Instruction Implementations
'==============================================================================

' ==============================================================================
' ACI (Add Immediate with Carry to A)
' Usage: ACI data
' Opcode:   11001110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A + immediate + CY
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = 1 if sum > 255 (overflow)
'   P  = 1 if result has even parity
'   AC = 1 if carry from bit 3
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   N  = 0 (Z80 only; indicates ADD, not SUB)
'
' Examples:
'   ACI 0x10        - Add 0x10 + carry to A
'   ACI 0xFF        - Add 0xFF + carry to A
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Multi-byte addition (add high byte with carry from low byte)
'   - Arithmetic with carry propagation
'
' Error Codes (base 100):
'   100: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   101: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ACI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 100
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "ACI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then ACI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Addition CLng(imm8), True  ' ? WITH carry included!
    ACI = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End ACI

' ==============================================================================
' ADC (Add Register with Carry to A)
' Usage: ADC source
' Opcode:   10001ss (ss = 0-7 for B,C,D,E,H,L,M,A)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A + source + CY
' Flags Affected: Same as ADD (CY, P, AC, Z, S, N)
'
' Examples:
'   ADC B           - Add B + carry to A
'   ADC M           - Add memory at (HL) + carry to A
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Multi-byte addition
'   - 16-bit: First ADD low bytes, then ADC high bytes
'
' Error Codes (base 110):
'   110: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   111: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ADC(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 110
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "ADC")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then ADC = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Addition CLng(src), True  ' True = include carry
    ADC = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End ADC

' ==============================================================================
' ADD (Add Register to A)
' Usage: ADD source
' Opcode:   10000ss (ss = 0-7 for B,C,D,E,H,L,M,A)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A + source
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = 1 if sum > 255 (overflow)
'   P  = 1 if result has even parity
'   AC = 1 if carry from bit 3
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set (result is "negative")
'   N  = 0 (Z80 only; indicates ADD, not SUB)
'
' Examples:
'   ADD A           - Double A (A = A + A)
'   ADD M           - Add memory at (HL) to A
'   ADD B           - Add B to A
'
' Error Codes (base 120):
'   120: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   121: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ADD(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 120
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "ADD")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then ADD = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Addition CLng(src), False  ' False = no carry
    ADD = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End ADD

' ==============================================================================
' ADI (Add Immediate to A)
' Usage: ADI data
' Opcode:   11000110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A + immediate
' Flags:       Same as ADD (CY, P, AC, Z, S, N)
'
' Examples:
'   ADI 10h         - Add 0x10 to A (opcode: C6h 10h)
'
' Error Codes (base 130):
'   130: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   131: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or label resolves to invalid/out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ADI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 130
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "ADI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then ADI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Addition CLng(imm8), False  ' ? No carry included
    ADI = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End ADI

' ==============================================================================
' ANA (AND Register with A)
' Usage: ANA source
' Opcode:   10100ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A AND source (bitwise AND)
' Flags Affected:
'   All flags set based on result (Z, S, P)
'   CY = 0 (always cleared)
'   AC = 1 (always set, Z80 behavior)
'
' Examples:
'   ANA A           - Logical AND of A with itself (result = A, flags set)
'   ANA B           - Mask A by AND-ing with B
'   ANA M           - AND A with memory at (HL)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Bit masking
'   - Testing bit patterns
'   - Clearing high nibble: ANA 0Fh
'
' Error Codes (base 140):
'   140: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   141: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ANA(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 140
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "ANA")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then ANA = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_AND CLng(src)
    ANA = 0
End Function
' ---  ANA ---


' ==============================================================================
' ANI (AND Immediate with A)
' Usage: ANI data
' Opcode:   11100110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A AND immediate
' Flags:       Same as ANA (Z, S, P; CY = 0, AC = 1)
'
' Examples:
'   ANI 0x0F        - Clear high nibble of A (mask with 0x0F)
'   ANI 0x80        - Test bit 7 (result 0 if not set)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Bit pattern testing
'   - Clearing specific bit groups
'   - Extract low/high nibble
'
' Error Codes (base 150):
'   150: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   151: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ANI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 150
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "ANI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then ANI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_AND CLng(imm8)
    ANI = 0
End Function
' ---  ANI ---

' ==============================================================================
' CALL (Call Subroutine)
' Usage: CALL address
' Opcode:   11001101 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 17 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 17 cycles
'
' Operation:   SP ? SP - 2
'              Memory[SP] ? next_instruction_address
'              PC ? address
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   CALL 0x1000     - Call subroutine at 0x1000
'   CALL 0x2000     - Call subroutine at 0x2000
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Call subroutines
'   - Function calls
'   - Modular code organization
'   - Reusable code blocks
'
' Error Codes (base 430):
'   430: Missing operand
'   431: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function CALL_(ByVal op1 As String, Optional ByVal op2 As String = "") As Long
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord, currentPC As Long, retAddr As Long
    Dim strAddr As String, sp_dec As Long, proc As Boolean
    Dim line0Address As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 160
    Dim decAddr As Long
    Dim addrRec As clsAddrRecord

    If op1 = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, "CALL: Missing Operand: " & op1
        CALL_ = errorBase: Exit Function
    End If

    proc = pLabels.IsProc(op1)
    If proc Then
        CALL_ = CallByName(Me, op1, VbMethod, op2)
        Exit Function
    End If

    Set record = pLabels.GetLabel(op1)
    If Not record Is Nothing Then
        decAddr = record.clsAddress
    Else
        If Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
            SetError errorBase + 1, "CALL: Invalid Address op1: " & op1
            CALL_ = errorBase + 1
            Exit Function
        End If
        decAddr = usrHexToDec(op1)
    End If

    currentPC = pPC_dec
    sp_dec = pRegs("SP")
    Set addrRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(currentPC)
    retAddr = addrRec.clsAddressNext

    strAddr = Right$("0000" & usrDecToHexString(retAddr), 4)

    sp_dec = sp_dec - 1
    pStack.clsPUSH sp_dec, usrHexToDec(Left$(strAddr, 2)), "CALL " & op1
    sp_dec = sp_dec - 1
    pStack.clsPUSH sp_dec, usrHexToDec(Right$(strAddr, 2)), "CALL " & op1
    
    SetReg "SP", sp_dec
    mUIStackDirty = True
    
    
    Set addrRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(decAddr)
    pPC_dec = addrRec.clsAddressLast
    SetPC pPC_dec
    
    CALL_ = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End CALL

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' CLS (console clear)
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function CLS(Optional ByVal op1 = "", Optional ByVal op2 = "") As Long
    usrForm.ClearConsole
    CLS = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End CLS

' ==============================================================================
' CMA (Complement A)
' Usage: CMA
' Opcode:   00101111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? NOT A (one's complement, bitwise NOT)
'
' Example:
'   Before:  A = 01010101
'   After:   A = 10101010
'
' Flags Affected: NONE (all flags remain unchanged)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Bitwise negation
'   - Inverting all bits in A
'   - Two's complement (CMA followed by INR A)
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function CMA() As Long
    Dim a As Long
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    SetReg "A", ((a Xor &HFF) And 255)
    ' Flags unaffected
    CMA = 0
End Function
' --- CMA ---

' ==============================================================================
' CMC (Complement Carry)
' Usage: CMC
' Opcode:   00111111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   CY ? NOT CY
'
' Example:
'   Before:  CY = 1
'   After:   CY = 0
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = flipped
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Toggle carry flag
'   - Prepare for conditional operations
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function CMC() As Long
    HlpFlagCalcCarry (1 - (pFlags("Carry") And 1))
    CMC = 0
End Function
' --- CMC ---


' ==============================================================================
' CMP (Compare Register with A)
' Usage: CMP source
' Opcode:   10111ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A - source (perform subtraction, discard result, set flags)
' Flags Affected:
'   Z  = 1 if A == source
'   S  = 1 if result is negative
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   CY = 1 if A < source (borrow)
'   AC = 1 if borrow from bit 3
'
' Notes:
'   - Does NOT modify A; only sets flags
'   - Useful for conditional jumps after comparison
'
' Examples:
'   MVI A, 0x50     - Load A with 0x50
'   CMP B           - Compare A with B (don't modify A)
'   JZ  EQUAL       - Jump if equal (Z flag set)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Testing equality: CMP reg, then JZ
'   - Testing less-than: CMP reg, then JC
'
' Error Codes (base 190):
'   190: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   191: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function CMP(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 190
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "CMP")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then CMP = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Compare CLng(src)
    CMP = 0
End Function
' --- CMP ---

' ==============================================================================
' CP (Integrated CP Opcode)
' Z80 redefined this opcode for clarity
' 8080: Call if Plus: CP Word
' Z80:  Compare Option with Register A:  CP A (option)
'       Native Z80 Operation is CALL P WORD
' Usage: CP data

Public Function cp(ByVal op1 As String, op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 185
    Dim result As Long
    '8080 CP: execute conditional CP
    If op2 = "" And op1 <> "A" Then
        cp = Me.CCOND("P", op1)
        Exit Function
    End If
    'Z80:  this is z80 compare and not 8080 call if plus
    If op1 = "A" Then
        'Standard register to A comparisons - resuse existing 8080 compare
        If usrIsRegister08Bit(op2) Then
            cp = Me.CMP(op2)
            Exit Function
        End If
        'CP A, BYTE which is equivalent to CPI BYTE in 8080
        If usrValIsHexString(op2) Then
            cp = Me.CPI(op2)
            Exit Function
        End If
        'still need to implement other z80 CP ops such as CP A,(HL) and CP A, (IX+OFFSET)
    End If
    SetError errorBase, "CP: Invalid Operation: " & op1 & " " & op2
    cp = errorBase
End Function

' ==============================================================================
' Redefined in Z80
' Z80: New Compare and increment Block Operation
' 8080: CPI (Compare Immediate with A)
' Usage: CPI data
' Opcode:   11111110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A - immediate (perform subtraction, discard result, set flags)
' Flags:       Same as CMP
'
' Notes:
'   - Immediate version of CMP
'   - Does NOT modify A
'
' Examples:
'   CPI 0x50        - Compare A with 0x50
'   JZ  FOUND       - Jump if A was 0x50
'
' Error Codes (base 200):
'   200: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   201: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function CPI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 200
    Dim imm8 As Variant
    
    'Assume this is a Z80 CPI and not a 8080 CPI
    If op1 = "" Then
        CPI = CPI_Z80
        Exit Function
    End If

    '8080 Version of CPI: CPI BYTE
    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "CPI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then CPI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Compare CLng(imm8)
    CPI = 0
End Function
' --- CPI ---
Public Function CPI_Z80() As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 205
    SetError errorBase, "CPI: Z80 Invalid Operation"
    CPI_Z80 = errorBase
End Function

' ==============================================================================
' DAA (Decimal Adjust Accumulator)
' Usage: DAA
' Opcode:   00100111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   Adjust A for Binary-Coded Decimal (BCD) after ADD/ADC
'
' Logic (8080):
'   If (A & 0x0F) > 9 or AC = 1: A ? A + 0x06
'   If (A >> 4) > 9 or CY = 1: A ? A + 0x60
'
' Notes:
'   - Used after ADD/ADC when operands are BCD digits (0-9)
'   - Corrects result into valid BCD format
'   - Example: 0x09 + 0x01 = 0x0A, DAA converts to 0x10 (BCD 10)
'
' Flags Affected:
'   Z, S, P updated for new value
'   CY may be set if high nibble overflow
'   AC preserved from original operation
'
' Common Uses:
'   - BCD arithmetic
'   - Decimal calculations
'   - Converting binary to BCD
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function DAA() As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 210
    Dim a As Long, ADD As Long
    Dim cyIn As Long, cyOut As Long
    Dim lowAdj As Boolean
    Dim result As Long

    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    cyIn = pFlags("Carry") And 1

    ADD = 0
    lowAdj = False

    If ((a And &HF) > 9) Or (pFlags("AC") = 1) Then
        ADD = ADD + &H6
        lowAdj = True
    End If

    If (a > &H99) Or (cyIn = 1) Then
        ADD = ADD + &H60
    End If

    result = a + ADD

    cyOut = IIf((result > 255) Or (a > &H99) Or (cyIn = 1 And (ADD And &H60) <> 0), 1, 0)
    HlpFlagCalcCarry cyOut
    HlpFlagCalcAC IIf(lowAdj, 1, 0)

    result = result And 255
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcSign result: HlpFlagCalcZero result: HlpFlagCalcParity result

    DAA = 0
End Function
' ---  DAA ---


' ==============================================================================
' DAD (Add Register Pair to HL)
' Usage: DAD regpair
' Opcode:   00pp1001 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, SP)
' 8080:     1 byte, 10 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 11 cycles
'
' Operation:   HL ? HL + regpair
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = 1 if result > 65535 (overflow), else 0
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Examples:
'   DAD B           - HL ? HL + BC
'   DAD D           - HL ? HL + DE
'   DAD HL          - HL ? HL + HL (double HL)
'   DAD SP          - HL ? HL + SP
'
' Common Uses:
'   - 16-bit addition
'   - Address arithmetic
'   - Pointer adjustment
'   - Doubling values (DAD HL)
'
' Error Codes (base 400):
'   400: Missing operand
'   401: Invalid register pair
' ==============================================================================
Public Function DAD(ByVal rp As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 220
    Dim hl As Long, addv As Variant, sum As Long

    
    addv = HlpResolveRegPair(rp, errorBase, "DAD")
    If IsEmpty(addv) Then DAD = errorBase: Exit Function

    hl = ((pRegs("H") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("L") And 255)
    sum = hl + CLng(addv)

    HlpFlagCalcCarry IIf(sum > &HFFFF&, 1, 0)
    sum = sum And &HFFFF&

    SetReg "H", (sum \ 256&) And 255
    SetReg "L", sum And 255
    DAD = 0
End Function
' --- DAD ---


' ==============================================================================
' DCR (Decrement Register or Memory)
' Usage: DCR register
' Opcode:   00ddd101 (ddd = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles (10 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (11 if M)
'
' Operation:   register ? register - 1
' Flags Affected:
'   Z, S, P, AC set based on result
'   CY unaffected
'
' Examples:
'   DCR A           - Decrement A
'   DCR M           - Decrement memory at (HL)
'   DCR B           - Decrement B
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Loop counters (decrement and jump if not zero)
'   - Counting down
'
' Error Codes (base 250):
'   250: Missing operand
'   251: Invalid register
' ==============================================================================
Public Function DCR(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 230
    Dim cur As Variant, result As Long, ac As Long

    cur = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "DCR")
    If IsEmpty(cur) Then DCR = errorBase: Exit Function

    result = (CLng(cur) - 1) And 255
    ac = IIf((CLng(cur) And &HF) = 0, 1, 0)

    HlpFlagCalcAC ac
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result

    If Not HlpStoreReg08(op1, result, errorBase + 1, "DCR") Then DCR = errorBase + 1: Exit Function
    DCR = 0
End Function
' --- DCR ---


' ==============================================================================
' DCX (Decrement Register Pair)
' Usage: DCX regpair
' Opcode:   00pp1011 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, SP)
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 6 cycles
'
' Operation:   register_pair ? register_pair - 1
' Flags Affected: NONE (16-bit operation)
'
' Examples:
'   DCX B           - Decrement BC
'   DCX HL          - Decrement HL
'   DCX SP          - Decrement stack pointer
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Decrementing address pointers
'   - Stack pointer adjustments
'   - 16-bit loop counters
'
' Error Codes (base 280):
'   280: Missing operand
'   281: Invalid register pair
' ==============================================================================
Public Function DCX(ByVal rp As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 240
    Dim v As Variant
    v = HlpResolveRegPair(rp, errorBase, "DCX")
    If IsEmpty(v) Then DCX = errorBase: Exit Function
    SetPairValue rp, (CLng(v) - 1) And &HFFFF&
    DCX = 0
End Function
' --- DCX ---

' ==============================================================================
' EQU (Equate / Define Symbol)
' Usage: EQU value [label_name]
' Purpose: Define a symbolic constant or label
'
' Operation:   Create symbol mapping to value
'              label_name ? value (usually hex address)
'
' Examples:
'   BUFFER EQU 0x1000      - Define BUFFER as 0x1000
'   COUNT EQU 10            - Define COUNT as 10
'   START EQU 0x0000        - Define START as start address
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Define symbolic names for addresses
'   - Create named constants
'   - Improve code readability
'   - Make code more maintainable
'
' Error Codes (base 440):
'   440: Missing value
'   441: Invalid hex value format
'   442: Duplicate symbol definition
' ==============================================================================
Public Function EQU(ByVal op1 As String, label As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 300
    Dim res As Long
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord

    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "EQU: Missing Operand: " & op1: EQU = errorBase: Exit Function
    If label = "" Then SetError errorBase + 1, "EQU: Missing Label: " & label: EQU = errorBase + 1: Exit Function

    Set record = pLabels.GetLabel(label)
    If record Is Nothing Then SetError errorBase + 2, "EQU: Missing label: " & label: EQU = errorBase + 2: Exit Function

    If Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then SetError errorBase + 3, "EQU: Invalid Valid: " & op1: EQU = errorBase + 3: Exit Function
    EQU = 0
End Function
' --- EQU ---

' ==============================================================================
' HLT (Halt)
' Usage: HLT
' Opcode:   01110110
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (+ CPU stopped)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (+ CPU stopped)
'
' Operation:   Stop execution (wait for interrupt)
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - CPU stops executing further instructions
'   - Program ends
'   - Can be resumed by interrupt (if enabled)
'
' Examples:
'   HLT             - End program
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Program termination
'   - End of main routine
'   - Idle state
'
' Return Value: -100 (normal termination code)
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function HLT() As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = -100
    SetError errorBase, "Program Halted:"
    HLT = errorBase
End Function
' --- HLT  ---


' ==============================================================================
' IN (Input from Port)
' Usage: IN port
' Opcode:   11011011 (next byte is port number)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 10 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 11 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? Port[port]
' Flags Affected: NONE (typically)
'
' Examples:
'   IN 0x00         - Read from port 0 into A
'   IN 0x01         - Read from port 1 into A
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Read input ports
'   - Serial communication
'   - Reading hardware state
'   - Reading switches/sensors
'
' Error Codes (base 410):
'   410: Missing operand
'   411: Invalid port number
' ==============================================================================
Public Function IN_(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 270
    Dim portVal As Long
    Dim dec_port As Long

    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "IN: Missing Port op1": IN_ = errorBase: Exit Function

    If Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, "IN: Invalid Hex: " & op1
        IN_ = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
        
    dec_port = CLng(usrHexToDec(op1))
    If dec_port < 0 Or dec_port > 255 Then
        SetError errorBase + 2, "IN: Invalid Port " & op1
        IN_ = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    Select Case dec_port
        Case 255: 'FF
            portVal = usrForm.ConReadByte
            SetReg "A", portVal
        Case 254: 'FE
            If Not GetInput(errorBase + 3) Then
                IN_ = errorBase + 3
            End If
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 4, "IN: Unconfigured Port: " & op1
            IN_ = errorBase + 4
            Exit Function
     End Select
     DoEvents
     IN_ = 0
End Function
' --- IN_ ---


' ==============================================================================
' INR (Increment Register or Memory)
' Usage: INR register
' Opcode:   00ddd100 (ddd = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles (10 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (11 if M)
'
' Operation:   register ? register + 1
' Flags Affected:
'   Z, S, P, AC set based on result
'   CY unaffected
'
' Examples:
'   INR A           - Increment A
'   INR M           - Increment memory at (HL)
'   INR B           - Increment B
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Loop counters
'   - Incrementing pointers
'   - Counting up
'
' Error Codes (base 260):
'   260: Missing operand
'   261: Invalid register
' ==============================================================================
Public Function INR(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 280
    Dim cur As Variant, result As Long, ac As Long

    cur = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "INR")
    If IsEmpty(cur) Then INR = errorBase: Exit Function

    result = (CLng(cur) + 1) And 255
    ac = IIf((CLng(cur) And &HF) = &HF, 1, 0)

    HlpFlagCalcAC ac
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result

    If Not HlpStoreReg08(op1, result, errorBase + 1, "INR") Then INR = errorBase + 1: Exit Function
    INR = 0
End Function
' --- INR ---


' ==============================================================================
' INX (Increment Register Pair)
' Usage: INX regpair
' Opcode:   00pp0011 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, SP)
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 6 cycles
'
' Operation:   register_pair ? register_pair + 1
' Flags Affected: NONE (16-bit operation, no flags set)
'
' Examples:
'   INX B           - Increment BC (B:C) by 1
'   INX HL          - Increment HL by 1
'   INX SP          - Increment stack pointer
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Address pointer increments
'   - Stack pointer management
'   - 16-bit counters
'
' Error Codes (base 270):
'   270: Missing operand
'   271: Invalid register pair (not BC, DE, HL, SP)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function INX(ByVal rp As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 290
    Dim v As Variant
    v = HlpResolveRegPair(rp, errorBase, "INX")
    If IsEmpty(v) Then INX = errorBase: Exit Function
    SetPairValue rp, (CLng(v) + 1) And &HFFFF&
    INX = 0
End Function
' --- INX ---


' ==============================================================================
' JMP (Unconditional Jump)
' Usage: JMP address
' Opcode:   11000011 (next 2 bytes are target address, LSB first)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles
'
' Operation:   PC ? address (jump unconditionally)
' Flags:       None affected
'
' Examples:
'   JMP 1000h       - Jump to address 0x1000 (opcode: C3h 00h 10h)
'
' Error Codes (base 310):
'   310: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   311: Label not found (referenced label does not exist)
'   312: Label resolves to invalid hex (address cannot be converted to hex)
'   313: Out-of-range address (address is beyond memory size)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JMP(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 300
    Dim memEnd_dec As Long, op_dec As Long
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord
    Dim line0Address As Long
    Dim addRec As clsAddrRecord
    
    Dim cur As Variant, result As Long, ac As Long

    cur = HlpResolveAddr16(op1, errorBase, "JMP")
    If IsEmpty(cur) Then JMP = errorBase: Exit Function
    memEnd_dec = Range("MemEnd").offset(0, 1).value
    op_dec = CLng(cur)
    If op_dec < 0 Or op_dec > memEnd_dec Then SetError errorBase + 3, "JMP: Invalid Address: " & op1: JMP = errorBase + 3: Exit Function

    Set addRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(op_dec)
    SetPC addRec.clsAddressLast

    JMP = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End JMP
Public Function JMP_o(op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 300
    Dim memEnd_dec As Long, op_dec As Long
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord
    Dim line0Address As Long
    Dim addRec As clsAddrRecord

    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "JMP: Missing Operand: " & op1: JMP_o = errorBase: Exit Function

    Set record = pLabels.GetLabel(op1)
    If record Is Nothing Then SetError errorBase + 1, "JMP: Missing Label: " & op1: JMP_o = errorBase + 1: Exit Function

    op1 = record.clsAddressHex
    If Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then SetError errorBase + 2, "JMP: Invalid Operand: " & op1: JMP_o = errorBase + 2: Exit Function

    memEnd_dec = Range("MemEnd").offset(0, 1).value
    op_dec = usrHexToDec(op1)
    If op_dec < 0 Or op_dec > memEnd_dec Then SetError errorBase + 3, "JMP: Invalid Address: " & op1: JMP_o = errorBase + 3: Exit Function

    Set addRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(op_dec)
    SetPC addRec.clsAddressLast

    JMP_o = 0
End Function
' ---  ---
' End JMP

' ==============================================================================
' JC / JNC / JZ / JNZ / JP / JM / JPE / JPO (Conditional Jumps)
' Conditional Jump Instructions
'
' Mnemonic | Opcode | Jump If...           | Flag Test
' ---------|--------|----------------------|-------------
' JC       | DA     | Carry = 1            | Jump if carry flag is SET
' JNC      | D2     | Carry = 0            | Jump if NO carry
' JZ       | CA     | Zero = 1             | Jump if result was ZERO
' JNZ      | C2     | Zero = 0             | Jump if NOT zero
' JP       | F2     | Sign = 0             | Jump if POSITIVE (sign bit clear)
' JM       | FA     | Sign = 1             | Jump if MINUS/NEGATIVE
' JPE      | EA     | Parity = 1           | Jump if EVEN parity
' JPO      | E2     | Parity = 0           | Jump if ODD parity
'
' 8080:     3 bytes each, 10 cycles if jump taken, 7 if not
' Z80:      3 bytes each, 10 cycles if jump taken, 7 if not
'
' Operation:   If condition true: PC ? address; else: PC ? PC + 3
' Flags:       None affected (test done before jump)
'
' Examples:
'   JC  1000h       - Jump to 0x1000 if carry flag is set
'   JNZ LOOP        - Jump back to LOOP label if NOT zero (continue loop)
'   JP  POSITIVE    - Jump if result was positive (high bit clear)
' ==============================================================================

' ==============================================================================
' JZ (Jump if Zero)
' Usage: JZ address
' Opcode:   11001010 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If Z = 1, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
' Flags:       No flags affected
'
' Condition:   Jump if last result was zero
'
' Examples:
'   JZ LOOP         - Jump to LOOP if last operation result was 0
'   JZ 0x1000       - Jump to address 0x1000 if Z flag set
'
' Error Codes (base 150):
'   150: Missing operand
'   151: Invalid address (not valid hex)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JZ(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    If HlpEvaluateCondition("JZ") Then
        JZ = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JZ = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JZ ---


' ==============================================================================
' JNZ (Jump if Not Zero)
' Usage: JNZ address
' Opcode:   11000010
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If Z = 0, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
' Flags:       No flags affected
'
' Condition:   Jump if last result was NOT zero
'
' Examples:
'   JNZ LOOP        - Jump if result is not zero (loop)
'   JNZ 0x2000      - Jump to 0x2000 if non-zero
'
' Error Codes (base 160):
'   160: Missing operand
'   161: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JNZ(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    If HlpEvaluateCondition("JNZ") Then
        JNZ = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JNZ = 0
    End If
End Function
' ---  JNZ ---


' ==============================================================================
' JC (Jump if Carry)
' Usage: JC address
' Opcode:   11011010
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If CY = 1, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
'
' Condition:   Jump if carry flag is set
'   - Overflow in ADD operations
'   - Borrow in CMP/SUB operations (CY=1 means A < operand)
'
' Examples:
'   JC ERROR        - Jump if overflow occurred
'   JC CHECK_LOW    - Jump if compare showed A < operand
'
' Error Codes (base 170):
'   170: Missing operand
'   171: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JC(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    If HlpEvaluateCondition("JC") Then
        JC = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JC = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JC ---

' ==============================================================================
' JNC (Jump if No Carry)
' Usage: JNC address
' Opcode:   11010010
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If CY = 0, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
'
' Condition:   Jump if carry flag is clear
'   - No overflow in ADD
'   - No borrow in CMP/SUB (CY=0 means A >= operand)
'
' Examples:
'   JNC SUCCESS     - Jump if no overflow
'   JNC GREATER     - Jump if A >= operand
'
' Error Codes (base 180):
'   180: Missing operand
'   181: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JNC(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    If HlpEvaluateCondition("JNC") Then
        JNC = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JNC = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JNC ---

' ==============================================================================
' JM (Jump if Minus)
' Usage: JM address
' Opcode:   11111010
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If S = 1, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
'
' Condition:   Jump if sign flag set (bit 7 = 1, negative number)
'
' Examples:
'   JM NEGATIVE     - Jump if result is negative
'   JM ERROR_NEG    - Jump for negative value check
'
' Error Codes (base 210):
'   210: Missing operand
'   211: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JM(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    If HlpEvaluateCondition("JM") Then
        JM = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JM = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JM ---


' ==============================================================================
' Z80 Redefined: JP (all jump conditions)
' 808: JP (Jump if Plus)
' Usage: JP address
' Opcode:   11110010
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles (5 if no jump)
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles (7 if no jump)
'
' Operation:   If S = 0, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
'
' Condition:   Jump if sign flag clear (bit 7 = 0, positive number)
'
' Examples:
'   JP POSITIVE     - Jump if result is positive
'   JP CONTINUE     - Jump for non-negative values
'
' Error Codes (base 220):
'   220: Missing operand
'   221: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function JP(ByVal op1 As String, Optional ByVal op2 As String = "") As Long
    '8080 instruction for jump if plus
    Dim condition As String: condition = "JP"
    'Z80 instruction for general jump conditions based on op1
    If op2 <> "" Then
       
        ' direct jump
        If op1 = "" Then
            JP = JMP(op2)
            Exit Function
        End If
        
        ' indrect jump from (HL)
        If op1 = "(HL)" Or op1 = "(IX)" Or op1 = "(IY)" Then
            JP = PCHL(op1)
            Exit Function
        End If
        
        If op1 = "C" Then condition = "JC"
        If op1 = "M" Then condition = "JM"
        If op1 = "NC" Then condition = "JNC"
        If op1 = "NZ" Then condition = "JNZ"
        If op1 = "P" Then condition = "JP"
        If op1 = "PE" Then condition = "JPE"
        If op1 = "PO" Then condition = "JPO"
        If op1 = "Z" Then condition = "JZ"
        op1 = op2
    End If
    
    If HlpEvaluateCondition(condition) Then
        JP = JMP(op1)
    Else
        JP = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JP ---
Public Function JP_indirect(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 305
    If op1 = "(HL)" Then
        JP_indirect = PCHL()
    End If
    

End Function

' ==============================================================================

'   JPE CHECK_CRC   - Jump for parity validation

' Error Codes (base 230):

Public Function JPE(ByVal op1 As String) As Long

        JPE = 0
    End If
End Function
' --- JPE ---

' Operation:   If P = 0, PC ? address; else PC ? PC + 3
'
' Condition:   Jump if parity flag clear (odd number of 1-bits)
'

'   JPO ERROR       - Jump for odd parity error detection
