    End If
End Function
' --- JPO ---
' ==============================================================================
' LDA (Load A Direct)
' Usage: LDA address
' Opcode:   00111010 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 13 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 13 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? Memory[address]
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   LDA 0x1000      - Load A from address 0x1000
'   LDA 0x2000      - Load A from address 0x2000
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Load data from direct memory addresses
'   - Reading from fixed memory locations
'
' Error Codes (base 320):
'   320: Missing operand
'   321: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function LDA(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 310
    Dim addr As Variant
    addr = HlpResolveAddr16(op1, errorBase, "LDA")
    If IsEmpty(addr) Then LDA = errorBase: Exit Function

    SetReg "A", CLng(pMemory.addr(CLng(addr))) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("LDA", CLng(addr), errorBase + 1) Then
        LDA = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    LDA = 0
End Function
' --- LDA ---
' ==============================================================================
' LHLD (Load H and L Direct)
' Usage: LHLD address
' Opcode:   00101010 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 16 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 16 cycles
'
' Operation:   L ? Memory[address], H ? Memory[address+1]
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Loads 16-bit value into HL from memory
'   - Little-endian: low byte at address, high byte at address+1
'
' Examples:
'   LHLD 0x1000     - Load HL from addresses 0x1000-0x1001
'   LHLD 0x2000     - Load HL from addresses 0x2000-0x2001
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Load 16-bit pointers
'   - Load 16-bit addresses
'   - Restoring HL from memory
'
' Error Codes (base 360):
'   360: Missing operand
'   361: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function LHLD(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 330
    Dim addr As Variant, a As Long
    addr = HlpResolveAddr16(op1, errorBase, "LHLD")
    If IsEmpty(addr) Then LHLD = errorBase: Exit Function

    a = CLng(addr)
    SetReg "L", pMemory.addr(a) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("LHLD", a, errorBase + 1) Then
        LHLD = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    SetReg "H", pMemory.addr(a + 1) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("LHLD", a + 1, errorBase + 2) Then
        LHLD = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    LHLD = 0
End Function
' --- LHLD ---

' ==============================================================================
' LDAX (Load A Indirect)
' Usage: LDAX regpair
' Opcode:   00rp1010 (rp = 0,1 for BC or DE)
' 8080:     1 byte, 7 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? Memory[regpair]
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Only BC and DE register pairs supported
'   - Address is stored in register pair
'
' Examples:
'   LDAX B          - A ? Memory[BC]
'   LDAX D          - A ? Memory[DE]
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Indirect memory access
'   - Array/buffer reading
'   - Pointer dereferencing
'
' Error Codes (base 340):
'   340: Missing operand
'   341: Invalid register pair (must be BC or DE)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function LDAX(ByVal rp As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 320
    Dim addr As Long

    rp = UCase$(Trim$(rp))
    Select Case rp
        Case "B"
            addr = ((pRegs("B") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("C") And 255)
        Case "D"
            addr = ((pRegs("D") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("E") And 255)
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 1, "LDAX: Invalid register pair: " & rp
            LDAX = errorBase + 1
            Exit Function
    End Select

    SetReg "A", pMemory.addr(addr) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("LDAX", addr, errorBase) Then
        LDAX = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    LDAX = 0
End Function
' --- LDAX ---


' ==============================================================================
' LXI (Load Register Pair Immediate)
' Usage: LXI regpair, address
' Opcode:   00pp0001 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, SP)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 10 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 10 cycles
'
' Operation:   register_pair ? address (16-bit value)
'   reg_high ? address_high, reg_low ? address_low
'
' Examples:
'   LXI B, 0x1000   - Load BC with 0x1000 (B=0x10, C=0x00)
'   LXI HL, 0x2000  - Load HL with 0x2000
'   LXI SP, 0x3000  - Load stack pointer with 0x3000
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Initialize register pairs
'   - Set up stack pointer
'   - Initialize address pointers
'   - Load constants into register pairs
'
' Error Codes (base 290):
'   290: Missing register pair
'   291: Invalid register pair
'   292: Missing address
'   293: Invalid address format
' ==============================================================================
Public Function LXI(ByVal op1 As String, op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 340
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord
    Dim useLabel As Boolean
    Dim address As String
    Dim regLow As String, regHigh As String
    Dim decLow As Long, decHigh As Long
    Dim sp As Long, memStart As Long

    If op1 = "" Or op2 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "LXI: Missing Operands: " & op1 & " " & op2: LXI = errorBase: Exit Function
    If op1 <> "B" And op1 <> "D" And op1 <> "H" And op1 <> "SP" Then SetError errorBase + 1, "LXI: Invalid Register: " & op1: LXI = errorBase + 1: Exit Function

    Set record = pLabels.GetLabel(op2)
    useLabel = Not record Is Nothing
    If useLabel Then op2 = record.clsAddressHex

    If Not usrValIsHexString(op2) Then SetError errorBase + 2, "LXI: Invalid Address: " & op2: LXI = errorBase + 2: Exit Function

    address = Right$("0000" & op2, 4)
    regHigh = Left$(address, 2)
    regLow = Right$(address, 2)
    decLow = usrHexToDec(regLow)
    decHigh = usrHexToDec(regHigh)

    Select Case op1
        Case "B": SetReg "B", decHigh: SetReg "C", decLow
        Case "D": SetReg "D", decHigh: SetReg "E", decLow
        Case "H": SetReg "H", decHigh: SetReg "L", decLow
        Case "SP"
            Me.SetReg "SP", usrHexToDec(address)
            mUIStackDirty = True

    End Select
    
    LXI = 0
End Function
' --- LXI ---

' ==============================================================================
' MOV (Move Data Register to Register)
' Usage: MOV dest, source
' Opcode:   01dddss (ddd = dest, sss = source)
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles (7 if M involved)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M involved)
'
' Operation:   dest ? source
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Transfers data from source to destination
'   - M represents memory at address (HL)
'   - All register combinations supported (A, B, C, D, E, H, L, M)
'
' Examples:
'   MOV A, B        - A ? B
'   MOV B, A        - B ? A
'   MOV M, A        - Memory at (HL) ? A
'   MOV A, M        - A ? Memory at (HL)
'   MOV H, L        - H ? L
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Register copy operations
'   - Loading from memory
'   - Storing to memory
'   - Register shuffling
'
' Error Codes (base 300):
'   300: Missing operands
'   301: Invalid destination register
'   302: Invalid source register
' ==============================================================================
Public Function MOV(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 350
    Dim v As Variant

    v = HlpResolveReg08(op2, errorBase, "MOV")
    If IsEmpty(v) Then MOV = errorBase: Exit Function

    If Not HlpStoreReg08(op1, CLng(v), errorBase + 1, "MOV") Then MOV = errorBase + 1: Exit Function

    MOV = 0
End Function
' --- MOV ---

' ==============================================================================
' MVI (Move Immediate Data to Register)
' Usage: MVI dest, data
' Opcode:   00ddd110 (ddd = destination register)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles (10 if M)
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles (10 if M)
'
' Operation:   dest ? immediate_value
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   MVI A, 0x50     - A ? 0x50
'   MVI B, 0xFF     - B ? 0xFF
'   MVI M, 0x00     - Memory at (HL) ? 0x00
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Initialize registers
'   - Load constants
'   - Clear memory locations
'   - Set up values before operations
'
' Error Codes (base 310):
'   310: Missing operands
'   311: Invalid hex value
'   312: Invalid destination register
' ==============================================================================
Public Function MVI(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 360
    Dim imm As Variant

    imm = HlpResolveImm08(op2, errorBase, "MVI")
    If IsEmpty(imm) Then MVI = errorBase: Exit Function

    If Not HlpStoreReg08(op1, CLng(imm), errorBase, "MVI") Then MVI = errorBase: Exit Function

    MVI = 0
End Function
' --- MVI ---

' ==============================================================================
' NOP (No Operation)
' Usage: NOP
' Opcode:   00000000
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   None (CPU does nothing for 4 cycles)
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   NOP             - Do nothing
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Timing delays
'   - Placeholder in code
'   - Alignment padding
'   - Debugging
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function NOP() As Long
    NOP = 0
End Function
' --- NOP ---

' ==============================================================================
' OUT (Output to Port)
' Usage: OUT port
' Opcode:   11010011 (next byte is port number)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 10 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 11 cycles
'
' Operation:   Port[port] ? A
' Flags Affected: NONE (typically)
'
' Examples:
'   OUT 0x00        - Write A to port 0
'   OUT 0x01        - Write A to port 1
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Write output ports
'   - Serial communication
'   - Controlling hardware
'   - Writing to LEDs/displays
'
' Error Codes (base 420):
'   420: Missing operand
'   421: Invalid port number
'
' op1:
'   FF / 255 - Set Lights with Reg A
'   FE / 254 - Set switches with Reg A
'   FD / 253 - Open Console
'   FC / 252 - Clear Console
'   FB / 251 - Repaint Console
'   FA / 250 - delay reg A in 1/100 seconds
' =============================================================================='
Public Function OUT_(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 400
    Dim portVal As Long
    Dim dec_port As Long

    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "OUT: Missing Port op1": OUT_ = errorBase: Exit Function

    If Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, "OUT: Invalid Hex: " & op1
        OUT_ = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
        
    dec_port = CLng(usrHexToDec(op1))
    If dec_port < 0 Or dec_port > 255 Then
        SetError errorBase + 2, "OUT: Invalid Port " & op1
        OUT_ = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    Select Case dec_port
        Case 255: 'FF - Set Lights
            usrForm.ConSetLights (pRegs("A"))
            DoEvents
        Case 254: 'FE - Set Switches
            usrForm.ConSetByte (pRegs("A"))
            DoEvents
        Case 253: 'FD - Open console
            ShowConsole
            DoEvents
        Case 252: 'FC - Clear Console
            ResetConsole
            DoEvents
        Case 251: 'FB - Repaint Console
            usrForm.Repaint
        Case 250: 'FA - Execute Time Delay
            portVal = pRegs("A")
            SmartDelay (portVal)
            
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 3, "OUT: Unconfigured Port: " & op1
            OUT_ = errorBase + 3
            Exit Function
     End Select
     
     OUT_ = 0
End Function
' --- OUT_ ---


' ==============================================================================
' ORA (OR Register with A)
' Usage: ORA source
' Opcode:   10110ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A OR source (bitwise OR)
' Flags Affected:
'   Z, S, P set based on result
'   CY = 0 (always cleared)
'   AC = 0 (always cleared)
'
' Examples:
'   ORA B           - OR A with B
'   ORA A           - Sets flags on A, CY cleared
'   ORA M           - OR A with memory at (HL)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Combining bit patterns
'   - Setting specific bits: ORA 80h (set bit 7)
'
' Error Codes (base 380):
'   380: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ORA(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 380
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "ORA")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then ORA = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_OR CLng(src)
    ORA = 0
End Function
' ---  ORA ---

' ==============================================================================
' ORI (OR Immediate with A)
' Usage: ORI data
' Opcode:   11110110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A OR immediate
' Flags:       Z, S, P set; CY = 0, AC = 0
'
' Examples:
'   ORI 0x80        - Set bit 7 of A (A = A | 0x80)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Setting specific bit groups in A
'   - Combining bitmasks
'
' Error Codes (base 390):
'   390: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   391: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function ORI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 390
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "ORI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then ORI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_OR CLng(imm8)
    ORI = 0
End Function
' ---  ORI ---

' ==============================================================================
' Z80 Extension: indirect jump to HL, IX, IY
' PCHL (Jump to Address in HL)
' Usage: PCHL
' Opcode:   11101001
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   PC ? HL (unconditional jump to address in HL)
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   PCHL            - Jump to address in HL
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Indirect jump via register
'   - Jump table implementation
'   - Dynamic jumps based on computed addresses
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function PCHL(Optional ByVal registerPair As String = "(HL)") As Long
    Dim hl As Long
    Dim addRec As clsAddrRecord
    Select Case registerPair
        Case "(HL)"
            hl = ((pRegs("H") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("L") And 255)
        Case "(IX)"
            hl = pRegs("IX")
        Case "(IY)"
            hl = pRegs("IY")
    End Select
    Set addRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(hl)
    SetPC addRec.clsAddressLast
    PCHL = 0
End Function
' ---  PCHL ---

' ==============================================================================
' POP (Pop Register Pair from Stack)
' Usage: POP regpair
' Opcode:   11pp0001 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, PSW)
' 8080:     1 byte, 10 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 10 cycles
'
' Operation:   reg_low ? Memory[SP], reg_high ? Memory[SP+1]
'              SP ? SP + 2
' Flags Affected: None (unless PSW, then all flags restored)
'
' Examples:
'   POP B           - Pop BC from stack
'   POP H           - Pop HL from stack
'   POP PSW         - Pop A and Flags from stack
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Restore register pairs from stack
'   - Return from function calls
'   - Restore saved state
'
' Error Codes (base 390):
'   390: Missing operand
'   391: Invalid register pair
'   392: Stack underflow (if applicable)
' ==============================================================================
Friend Function POP(ByVal op1) As Long
    Dim res As Long, sp As Long
    Dim registerRecH As clsDecRegisterState, registerRecL As clsDecRegisterState
    Dim decLow As Long, decHigh As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 420
    Dim flagByte As Byte

    res = 0
    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "POP: Missing Operand: " & op1: POP = errorBase: Exit Function

    sp = pRegs("SP")
    Set registerRecL = pStack.clsPOP: sp = sp + 1
    Set registerRecH = pStack.clsPOP: sp = sp + 1
    decLow = registerRecL.value
    decHigh = registerRecH.value

    Select Case op1
        Case "B": SetReg "B", decHigh: SetReg "C", decLow
        Case "D": SetReg "D", decHigh: SetReg "E", decLow
        Case "H": SetReg "H", decHigh: SetReg "L", decLow
        Case "PSW"
            SetReg "A", decHigh
            flagByte = decLow And 255
            pFlags("Sign") = IIf((flagByte And 128) <> 0, 1, 0)
            pFlags("Zero") = IIf((flagByte And 64) <> 0, 1, 0)
            pFlags("AC") = IIf((flagByte And 16) <> 0, 1, 0)
            pFlags("Parity") = IIf((flagByte And 4) <> 0, 1, 0)
            pFlags("Flag") = 1
            pFlags("Carry") = IIf((flagByte And 1) <> 0, 1, 0)
            mUIFlagsDirty = True
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 1, "POP: Invalid Register: " & op1: POP = errorBase + 1: Exit Function
    End Select

    SetReg "SP", sp
    
    POP = res
End Function
' --- POP ---

' ==============================================================================
' PUSH (Push Register Pair onto Stack)
' Usage: PUSH regpair
' Opcode:   11pp0101 (pp = 0-3 for BC, DE, HL, PSW)
' 8080:     1 byte, 11 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 11 cycles
'
' Operation:   SP ? SP - 2
'              Memory[SP+1] ? reg_high, Memory[SP] ? reg_low
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   PUSH B          - Push BC onto stack
'   PUSH H          - Push HL onto stack
'   PUSH PSW        - Push A and Flags onto stack
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Save register pairs on stack
'   - Preserve values during function calls
'   - Create temporary storage
'
' Note:
'   - PSW = A and Flags register together
'   - Decrements SP by 2
'
' Error Codes (base 380):
'   380: Missing operand
'   381: Invalid register pair
'   382: Stack overflow (if applicable)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function PUSH(ByVal op1) As Long
    Dim sp As Long
    Dim sp_high As String, sp_low As String
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 430
    Dim flagByte As Byte

    If op1 = "" Then SetError errorBase, "PUSH: Missing Operand: " & op1: PUSH = errorBase: Exit Function

    sp = pRegs("SP")
    sp_high = sp - 1
    sp = sp - 1
    sp_low = sp
    
    Select Case op1
        Case "B": pStack.clsPUSH sp_high, pRegs("B"), "B": pStack.clsPUSH sp_low, pRegs("C"), "C"
        Case "D": pStack.clsPUSH sp_high, pRegs("D"), "D": pStack.clsPUSH sp_low, pRegs("E"), "E"
        Case "H": pStack.clsPUSH sp_high, pRegs("H"), "H": pStack.clsPUSH sp_low, pRegs("L"), "L"
        Case "PSW"
            pStack.clsPUSH sp, pRegs("A"), "A"
            sp = sp - 1
            flagByte = 0
            If pFlags("Sign") = 1 Then flagByte = flagByte + 128
            If pFlags("Zero") = 1 Then flagByte = flagByte + 64
            If pFlags("AC") = 1 Then flagByte = flagByte + 16
            If pFlags("Parity") = 1 Then flagByte = flagByte + 4
            flagByte = flagByte + 2     ' reserved bit set
            If pFlags("Carry") = 1 Then flagByte = flagByte + 1
            
            pStack.clsPUSH sp, flagByte, "Flags"
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 1, "PUSH: Invalid Register: " & op1: PUSH = errorBase + 1: Exit Function
    End Select

    SetReg "SP", sp
    mUIStackDirty = True
    
    PUSH = 0
End Function
' --- PUSH ---

' ==============================================================================
' RAL (Rotate A Left Through Carry)
' Usage: RAL
' Opcode:   00010111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? (A << 1) | CY_old, bit 7 ? CY
'
' Example:
'   Before:  A = 10110010, CY = 1
'   After:   A = 01100101, CY = 1  (bit 7 = 1)
'
' Notes:
'   - Rotate left; CY enters bit 0
'   - Old bit 7 goes to CY
'   - Effectively: A = (A * 2) | CY, with CY = (A >> 7)
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = old bit 7
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function RAL() As Long
    Dim a As Long, msb As Long, cy As Long, result As Long
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    cy = pFlags("Carry") And 1
    msb = IIf((a And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
    result = ((a * 2) And 255) Or cy
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcCarry msb
    RAL = 0
End Function
' --- RAL ---

' ==============================================================================
' RAR (Rotate A Right Through Carry)
' Usage: RAR
' Opcode:   00011111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? (A >> 1) | (CY_old << 7), bit 0 ? CY
'
' Example:
'   Before:  A = 10110011, CY = 1
'   After:   A = 11011001, CY = 1  (bit 0 = 1)
'
' Notes:
'   - Rotate right; CY enters bit 7
'   - Old bit 0 goes to CY
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = old bit 0
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function RAR() As Long
    Dim a As Long, lsb As Long, cy As Long, result As Long
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    cy = pFlags("Carry") And 1
    lsb = a And 1
    result = ((a \ 2) And 127) Or (cy * 128)
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcCarry lsb
    RAR = 0
End Function
' --- RAR ---

' ==============================================================================
' RET (Return from Subroutine)
' Usage: RET
' Opcode:   11001001
' 8080:     1 byte, 10 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 10 cycles
'
' Operation:   PC ? Memory[SP], SP ? SP + 2 (pop return address)
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Pops return address from stack
'   - Continues execution from return address
'   - Complements CALL instruction
'
' Examples:
'   RET             - Return to caller
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Exit from subroutines
'   - Return from function calls
'   - Standard function return
'
' Error Codes:
'   None (hardware manages stack)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function RET() As Long
    Dim stackRec As clsDecRegisterState
    Dim Count As Long, newPC As Long, sp_dec As Long
    Dim retAddress As String, retAddress_dec As Long
    Dim line0Address As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 460
    Dim addressRec As clsAddrRecord

    Count = pStack.Count
    If Count = 0 Then SetError errorBase, "RET: No Address on Stack": RET = errorBase: Exit Function

    Set stackRec = pStack.clsPeek
    If Left$(stackRec.RegisterName, 4) <> "CALL" Then SetError errorBase + 1, "RET: Invalid Address on Stack: " & stackRec.RegisterName: RET = errorBase + 1: Exit Function

    sp_dec = pRegs("SP")
    Set stackRec = pStack.clsPOP
    sp_dec = sp_dec + 1
    retAddress_dec = stackRec.value
    retAddress = usrDecToHexString(retAddress_dec)
    
    Set stackRec = pStack.clsPOP
    sp_dec = sp_dec + 1
    retAddress = usrDecToHexString(stackRec.value) & retAddress

    Me.SetReg "SP", sp_dec
    mUIStackDirty = True

    Set addressRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(usrHexToDec(retAddress))
    newPC = addressRec.clsAddressLast
    SetPC newPC

    RET = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

' --- RLC/RRC/RAL/RAR (only CY affected, other flags unchanged) ---
Public Function RLC() As Long
    Dim a As Long, msb As Long, result As Long
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    msb = IIf((a And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
    result = ((a * 2) And 255) Or msb
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcCarry msb
    RLC = 0
End Function
' ==============================================================================
' RRC (Rotate A Right Circular)
' Usage: RRC
' Opcode:   00001111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A >> 1, bit 0 ? CY, CY ? bit 7
'
' Example:
'   Before:  A = 10110011, CY = 0
'   After:   A = 01011001, CY = 1  (bit 0 was 1)
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = old bit 0
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Rotating bits right
'   - Extracting LSB
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function RRC() As Long
    Dim a As Long, lsb As Long, result As Long
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    lsb = a And 1
    result = ((a \ 2) And 127) Or (lsb * 128)
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcCarry lsb
    RRC = 0
End Function
' --- RRC ---

' ==============================================================================
' SBB (Subtract Register with Borrow from A)
' Usage: SBB source
' Opcode:   10011ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A - source - CY
' Flags:       Same as SUB
'
' Notes:
'   - CY flag contains borrow from previous operation
'   - Used for multi-byte subtraction
'
' Examples:
'   SBB B           - Subtract B and borrow from A
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Multi-byte subtraction (SBB high bytes after SUB low bytes)
'
' Error Codes (base 570):
'   570: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   571: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SBB(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 570
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "SBB")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then SBB = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Subtraction CLng(src), True   ' ? WITH borrow included!
    SBB = 0
End Function
' --- SBB ---

' ==============================================================================
' SBI (Subtract Immediate with Borrow from A)
' Usage: SBI data
' Opcode:   11011110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A - immediate - CY
' Flags:       Same as SUB
'
' Examples:
'   SBI 0x10        - Subtract 0x10 + borrow from A
'
' Error Codes (base 560):
'   560: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   561: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SBI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 560
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "SBI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then SBI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Subtraction CLng(imm8), True  ' ? WITH borrow included!
    SBI = 0
End Function
' --- SBI ---

' ==============================================================================
' SHLD (Store H and L Direct)
' Usage: SHLD address
' Opcode:   00100010 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 16 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 16 cycles
'
' Operation:   Memory[address] ? L, Memory[address+1] ? H
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Stores 16-bit HL to memory
'   - Little-endian: L at address, H at address+1
'
' Examples:
'   SHLD 0x1000     - Store HL to addresses 0x1000-0x1001
'   SHLD 0x2000     - Store HL to addresses 0x2000-0x2001
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Save HL pair to memory
'   - Store 16-bit pointers
'   - Saving address registers
'
' Error Codes (base 370):
'   370: Missing operand
'   371: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SHLD(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 520
    Dim addr As Variant, a As Long
    addr = HlpResolveAddr16(op1, errorBase, "SHLD")
    If IsEmpty(addr) Then SHLD = errorBase: Exit Function

    a = CLng(addr)
    pMemory.addr(a) = CByte(pRegs("L") And 255)
    If HlpMemCheckError("SHLD", a, errorBase + 1) Then
        SHLD = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    pMemory.addr(a + 1) = CByte(pRegs("H") And 255)
    If HlpMemCheckError("SHLD", a + 1, errorBase + 2) Then
        SHLD = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    SHLD = 0
End Function
' --- SHLD ---

' ==============================================================================
' SPHL (Load Stack Pointer from HL)
' Usage: SPHL
' Opcode:   11111001
' 8080:     1 byte, 5 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 6 cycles
'
' Operation:   SP ? HL
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   SPHL            - Set stack pointer to HL value
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Switch stack contexts
'   - Initialize stack pointer dynamically
'   - Restore stack pointer from HL
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SPHL() As Long
    Dim hl As Long
    hl = ((pRegs("H") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("L") And 255)
    SetReg "SP", hl And &HFFFF&
    mUIStackDirty = True
    SPHL = 0
End Function
' --- SPHL ---

' ==============================================================================
' STA (Store A Direct)
' Usage: STA address
' Opcode:   00110010 (address follows as 16-bit word)
' 8080:     3 bytes, 13 cycles
' Z80:      3 bytes, 13 cycles
'
' Operation:   Memory[address] ? A
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   STA 0x1000      - Store A to address 0x1000
'   STA 0x2000      - Store A to address 0x2000
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Store accumulator to direct memory
'   - Writing to fixed memory locations
'   - Saving results
'
' Error Codes (base 330):
'   330: Missing operand
'   331: Invalid address
' ==============================================================================
Public Function STA(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 550
    Dim addr As Variant
    addr = HlpResolveAddr16(op1, errorBase, "STA")
    If IsEmpty(addr) Then STA = errorBase: Exit Function

    pMemory.addr(CLng(addr)) = CByte(pRegs("A") And 255)
    If HlpMemCheckError("STA", CLng(addr), errorBase + 1) Then
        STA = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    STA = 0
End Function
' --- STA ---

' ==============================================================================
' STAX (Store A Indirect)
' Usage: STAX regpair
' Opcode:   00rp0010 (rp = 0,1 for BC or DE)
' 8080:     1 byte, 7 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   Memory[regpair] ? A
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Notes:
'   - Only BC and DE register pairs supported
'   - Complements LDAX instruction
'
' Examples:
'   STAX B          - Memory[BC] ? A
'   STAX D          - Memory[DE] ? A
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Indirect memory storage
'   - Array/buffer writing
'   - Pointer-based storage
'
' Error Codes (base 350):
'   350: Missing operand
'   351: Invalid register pair (must be BC or DE)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function STAX(ByVal rp As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 560
    Dim addr As Long

    rp = UCase$(Trim$(rp))
    Select Case rp
        Case "B"
            addr = ((pRegs("B") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("C") And 255)
        Case "D"
            addr = ((pRegs("D") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("E") And 255)
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 1, "STAX: Invalid register pair: " & rp
            STAX = errorBase + 1
            Exit Function
    End Select

    pMemory.addr(addr) = CByte(pRegs("A") And 255)
    If HlpMemCheckError("STAX", addr, errorBase) Then
        STAX = errorBase + 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    STAX = 0
End Function
' --- STAX ---

' ==============================================================================
' STC (Set Carry)
' Usage: STC
' Opcode:   00110111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   CY ? 1
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = 1
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Initialize carry flag before operations
'   - Set up for conditional logic
'   - Prepare for SBB operations
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function STC() As Long
    HlpFlagCalcCarry 1
    STC = 0
End Function
' --- STC ---

' ==============================================================================
' SUB (Subtract Register from A)
' Usage: SUB_ source
' Opcode:   10010ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A - source
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = 1 if A < source (borrow)
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   AC = 1 if borrow from bit 3
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if result is negative (bit 7 set)
'   N  = 1 (Z80 only; indicates SUB, not ADD)
'
' Examples:
'   SUB B           - Subtract B from A
'   SUB M           - Subtract memory at (HL) from A
'
' Error Codes (base 580):
'   580: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   581: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SUB_(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 580
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "SUB")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then SUB_ = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Subtraction CLng(src), False  ' False = no borrow
    SUB_ = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

' ==============================================================================
' SUI (Subtract Immediate from A)
' Usage: SUI data
' Opcode:   11010110 (next byte is immediate)
' 8080:     2 bytes, 7 cycles
' Z80:      2 bytes, 7 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A - immediate
' Flags:       Same as SUB (CY, AC, Z, S, P, N)
'
' Examples:
'   SUI 0x10        - Subtract 0x10 from A
'   SUI 0x01        - Decrement A by 1
'
' Error Codes (base 590):
'   590: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   591: Invalid hex immediate (not valid hex or out-of-range)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SUI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 590
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "SUI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then SUI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_Subtraction CLng(imm8), False  ' ? No borrow included
    SUI = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

' ==============================================================================
' XRA (XOR Register with A)
' Usage: XRA source
' Opcode:   10101ss (ss = 0-7)
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles (7 if M)
'
' Operation:   A ? A XOR source (exclusive OR)
' Flags:       Z, S, P set; CY = 0, AC = 0
'
' Examples:
'   XRA A           - XOR A with itself (result = 0, all flags updated)
'   XRA B           - XOR A with B (toggle bits where B has 1s)
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Clear register: XRA A (faster than MVI A, 0)
'   - Toggle bits selectively
'   - Checksum/parity computation
'
' Error Codes (base 400):
'   400: Missing operand (op1 is empty)
'   401: Invalid register (op1 register name not recognized)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function XRA(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 400
    Dim src As Variant

    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "XRA")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then XRA = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_XOR CLng(src)
    XRA = 0
End Function
' ---  XRA ---


' --- XRI data (A = A XOR imm) ; clears CY and AC; sets S/Z/P ---
Public Function XRI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 410
    Dim imm8 As Variant

    imm8 = HlpResolveImm08(op1, errorBase, "XRI")
    If IsEmpty(imm8) Then XRI = errorBase: Exit Function

    HlpALU_XOR CLng(imm8)
    XRI = 0
End Function
' --- XRI ---

' ==============================================================================
' XCHG (Exchange HL and DE)
' Usage: XCHG
' Opcode:   11101011
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   HL ? DE (swap register pairs)
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   XCHG            - Swap HL and DE
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Swap addresses
'   - Exchange pointer values
'   - Temporary storage swap
'
' Error Codes: None (no operands)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function XCHG() As Long
    Dim d As Long, e As Long, h As Long, l As Long
    d = pRegs("D"): e = pRegs("E")
    h = pRegs("H"): l = pRegs("L")
    SetReg "D", h: SetReg "E", l
    SetReg "H", d: SetReg "L", e
    XCHG = 0
End Function
' --- XCHG ---
' ==============================================================================
' XTHL (Exchange HL with Memory at Stack)
' Usage: XTHL
' Opcode:   11100011
' 8080:     1 byte, 18 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 19 cycles
'
' Operation:   HL ? Memory[SP]
'   temp_L ? L, L ? Memory[SP], Memory[SP] ? temp_L
'   temp_H ? H, H ? Memory[SP+1], Memory[SP+1] ? temp_H
'
' Flags Affected: NONE
'
' Examples:
'   XTHL            - Swap HL with top of stack
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Exchange HL with stack value
'   - Temporary swap with stack
'
' Error Codes: None
' ==============================================================================
Public Function XTHL() As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 630
    Dim sp As Long
    Dim tmp As Long

    sp = pRegs("SP") And &HFFFF&

    ' swap L <-> (SP)
    tmp = pMemory.addr(sp) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("XTHL", sp, errorBase) Then
        XTHL = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    pMemory.addr(sp) = CByte(pRegs("L") And 255)
    SetReg "L", tmp

    ' swap H <-> (SP+1)
    tmp = pMemory.addr(sp + 1) And 255
    If HlpMemCheckError("XTHL", sp + 1, errorBase + 1) Then
        XTHL = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    pMemory.addr(sp + 1) = CByte(pRegs("H") And 255)
    SetReg "H", tmp

    mUIStackDirty = True
    XTHL = 0
End Function
' --- XTHL ---

'================================================================================
' Z80 Additions
'================================================================================
' ==============================================================================
' EX (Exchange Register Pairs)
' Usage: EX dest, source
' Variants:
'   EX DE, HL       - Swap DE with HL (opcode: EBh)
'   EX AF, AF'      - Swap A and F with shadows (opcode: 08h)
'   EX (SP), HL     - Swap (SP) with HL (1-byte stack operation)
'
' 8080:     Limited support (varies)
' Z80:      Full support (1-2 bytes, 4-19 cycles)
'
' Operation:
'   Exchanges values of two registers
'
' Examples:
'   EX DE, HL       - Swap DE and HL values
'   EX (SP), HL     - Pop HL from stack, push original HL to stack
' ==============================================================================
Public Function EX(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2000
    ' Case 1: EX AF, AF' (Swaps main Accumulator/Flags with Shadows)
    If op1 = "AF" Then
        Me.EX_AF_AF_PRIME
        
    ' Case 2: EX DE, HL (Swaps DE and HL register pairs)
    ElseIf op1 = "DE" And op2 = "HL" Then
        Dim tDE As Long: tDE = Me.RegGet16("DE")
        Me.SetReg16 "DE", Me.RegGet16("HL")
        Me.SetReg16 "HL", tDE
        
    ' Case 3: EX (SP), HL (Swaps HL with the top of the Stack)
    ElseIf op1 = "(SP)" And op2 = "HL" Then
        Dim tSP As Long, tHL As Long
        tHL = Me.RegGet16("HL")
        ' Read 16-bit value from stack
        tSP = pMemory.addr(Me.RegGet16("SP")) + (CLng(pMemory.addr(Me.RegGet16("SP") + 1)) * 256)
        If HlpMemCheckError("EX", Me.RegGet16("SP"), errorBase) Then
            EX = errorBase
            Exit Function
        End If
        
        ' Swap them
        Me.SetReg16 "HL", tSP
        ' Write original HL back to stack
        pMemory.addr(Me.RegGet16("SP")) = tHL And &HFF
        pMemory.addr(Me.RegGet16("SP") + 1) = (tHL \ 256) And &HFF
    Else
        SetError errorBase + 1, "EX: Invalid register pair: " & op1 & " - " & op2
        EX = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    EX = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

Public Function EX_AF_AF_PRIME() As Long
    Dim tempA As Variant, tempF As Variant
    
    ' Swap A
    tempA = pRegs("A")
    pRegs("A") = pRegs("Ap")
    pRegs("Ap") = tempA
    
    ' Swap Flags (Internal dictionary to Shadow and back)
    ' This requires a helper to pack/unpack the flags into a byte
    tempF = HlpFlagPack()
    HlpFlagUnpack pRegs("Fp")
    pRegs("Fp") = tempF
    
    mUIRegsDirty = True
    EX_AF_AF_PRIME = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

' ==============================================================================
' EXX (Exchange Primary and Shadow Registers)
' Usage: EXX
' Opcode:   11011001 (single byte)
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:
'   Swap (B,C) ? ? (B',C')
'   Swap (D,E) ? ? (D',E')
'   Swap (H,L) ? ? (H',L')
'   Note: A and F are NOT swapped; use separate EX AF, AF' for that
'
' Flags:       None affected (flags not swapped unless using EX AF, AF')
'
' Usage:
'   EXX             - Quickly swap register set for interrupt handler
'   EX AF, AF'      - Swap A and F with shadow versions
'
' Example:
'   Original:    B=0x42, C=0x99, B'=0x11, C'=0x22
'   After EXX:   B=0x11, C=0x22, B'=0x42, C'=0x99
' ==============================================================================
Public Function EXX() As Long
    Dim temp As Variant
    Dim pairs As Variant, p As Variant
    pairs = Array("B", "C", "D", "E", "H", "L")
    
    For Each p In pairs
        temp = pRegs(p)
        pRegs(p) = pRegs(p & "p")
        pRegs(p & "p") = temp
    Next p
    mUIRegsDirty = True
    EXX = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

Public Function SRL(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2010
    Dim src As Variant
    Dim result As Boolean
    src = HlpResolveReg08(op1, errorBase, "SRL")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then SRL = errorBase: Exit Function
    Dim subCode As Byte
    subCode = &H38 + HlpRegGetCode(op1) ' Helper to get 0-7 for B,C,D,E,H,L,(HL),A
    result = HlpHandleCBShifts(subCode, "SRL", errorBase)
    If Not result Then
        SRL = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    mUIRegsDirty = True
    SRL = 0
End Function
' ---  ---

' End z80 additions

' --- Conditional CALL / RET (no memory beyond stack) ---
Public Function CCOND(ByVal cond As String, ByVal target As String) As Long
    If HlpTestCondition(cond) Then
        CCOND = CALL_(target)
    Else
        CCOND = 0
    End If
End Function
' ---  ---

Public Function RCOND(ByVal cond As String) As Long
    If HlpTestCondition(cond) Then
        RCOND = RET()
    Else
        RCOND = 0
    End If
End Function
' ---  ---

'==============================================================================
'                         Helper Utilities
'==============================================================================

' Evaluates jump conditions against flags
Private Function HlpEvaluateCondition(ByVal opcode As String) As Boolean
    Select Case opcode
        Case "JZ":  HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Zero") = 1)
        Case "JNZ": HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Zero") = 0)
        Case "JC":  HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Carry") = 1)
        Case "JNC": HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Carry") = 0)
        Case "JM":  HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Sign") = 1)
        Case "JP":  HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Sign") = 0)
        Case "JPE": HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Parity") = 1)
        Case "JPO": HlpEvaluateCondition = (pFlags("Parity") = 0)
    End Select
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Function HlpTestCondition(ByVal cond As String) As Boolean
    Select Case cond
        Case "Z":  HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Zero") = 1)
        Case "NZ": HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Zero") = 0)
        Case "C":  HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Carry") = 1)
        Case "NC": HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Carry") = 0)
        Case "M":  HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Sign") = 1)
        Case "P":  HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Sign") = 0)
        Case "PE": HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Parity") = 1)
        Case "PO": HlpTestCondition = (pFlags("Parity") = 0)
    End Select
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Function HlpResolveImm08(ByVal token As String, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Variant
    Dim lbl As clsLabelRecord

    If token = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, opname & ": Missing Operand"
        HlpResolveImm08 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    Set lbl = pLabels.GetLabel(token)
    If Not lbl Is Nothing Then token = lbl.clsAddressHex

    If Not usrValIsHexString(token) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, opname & ": Invalid Hex Immediate: " & token
        HlpResolveImm08 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    HlpResolveImm08 = (usrHexToDec(token) And 255)
End Function
' --- HlpResolveImm08  ---
Private Function HlpResolveImm16(ByVal token As String, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Variant
    Dim lbl As clsLabelRecord

    If token = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, opname & ": Missing Operand"
        HlpResolveImm16 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    Set lbl = pLabels.GetLabel(token)
    If Not lbl Is Nothing Then token = lbl.clsAddressHex

    If Not usrValIsHexString(token) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, opname & ": Invalid Hex Immediate: " & token
        HlpResolveImm16 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    HlpResolveImm16 = (usrHexToDec(token) And 255 * 255)
End Function
' --- HlpResolveImm16  ---

Private Function HlpResolveRegPair(ByVal rp As String, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Variant
    Dim v As Long
    Select Case rp
        Case "B": v = ((pRegs("B") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("C") And 255)
        Case "D": v = ((pRegs("D") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("E") And 255)
        Case "H": v = ((pRegs("H") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("L") And 255)
        Case "SP": v = (pRegs("SP") And &HFFFF&)
        Case Else
            SetError errorBase + 1, opname & ": Invalid Register Pair: " & rp
            HlpResolveRegPair = Empty
            Exit Function
    End Select
    HlpResolveRegPair = (v And &HFFFF&)
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Sub SetPairValue(ByVal rp As String, ByVal v As Long)
    v = v And &HFFFF&
    Select Case rp
        Case "B"
            SetReg "B", (v \ 256&) And 255
            SetReg "C", v And 255
        Case "D"
            SetReg "D", (v \ 256&) And 255
            SetReg "E", v And 255
        Case "H"
            SetReg "H", (v \ 256&) And 255
            SetReg "L", v And 255
        Case "SP"
            SetReg "SP", v
            mUIStackDirty = True
    End Select
End Sub
' ---  ---

' Centralized error setter (writes Error / errMessage on sheet)
Private Sub SetError(ByVal errcode As Long, ByVal errString As String)
    Dim errMessage As String
    If errString Like "*Halt*" Then errMessage = errString Else errMessage = "Error: " & errcode & " - " & errString
    errMessage = errMessage & " at line " & Reg("PC")
    Range("Error").value = errcode
    Range("errMessage") = errMessage
End Sub
' ---  ---

' Increment PC and update sheet (unless deferred)
Public Function IncPC() As Long
    Dim addrRec As clsAddrRecord
    Set addrRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(pPC_dec)
    pPC_dec = addrRec.clsAddressNext
    pRegs("PC") = pPC_dec
    IncPC = pPC_dec
End Function
' ---  ---

' Set PC to absolute decimal address and update sheet (unless deferred)
Public Function SetPC(ByVal address As Long)
    pPC_dec = address
    pRegs("PC") = pPC_dec
    mUIRegsDirty = True
    SetPC = pPC_dec
End Function
' ---  ---

Public Function GetCurrentIdx() As Long
    Set pNodeRec = pAddressList.GetAddr(pPC_dec)
    If pNodeRec Is Nothing Then
        GetCurrentIdx = -1
    Else
        GetCurrentIdx = pNodeRec.clsIndex
    End If
End Function
' ---  ---

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpFlagCalcParity (fast via LUT): sets Parity=1 for even parity as on 8080
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Function HlpFlagCalcParity(ByVal bits As Byte) As Long
    Static parity(0 To 255) As Byte
    Static init As Boolean
    Dim i As Long, b As Long, c As Long
    If Not init Then
        For i = 0 To 255
            b = i: c = 0
            Do While b
                c = c Xor (b And 1)
                b = b \ 2
            Loop
            ' 8080 parity flag: 1 for even parity
            parity(i) = IIf(c = 0, 1, 0)
        Next
        init = True
    End If
    pFlags("Parity") = parity(bits)
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcParity = pFlags("Parity")
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Function HlpFlagCalcSign(bits As Long) As Long
    Dim sign As Long
    sign = IIf((bits And 128) > 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("Sign") = sign
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcSign = sign
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Function HlpFlagCalcAC(bits As Long) As Long
    pFlags("AC") = bits And 1
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcAC = bits
End Function
' ---  ---

Private Function HlpFlagCalcCarry(bits As Long) As Long
    pFlags("Carry") = bits And 1
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcCarry = bits
End Function
' ---  ---

Public Function HlpFlagCalcZero(result As Long) As Long
    pFlags("Zero") = IIf(result = 0, 1, 0)
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcZero = pFlags("Zero")
End Function
' ---  ---

' New Z80 N Subtract Flag
Public Function HlpFlagCalcZeroAndSign(result As Long) As Long
    pFlags("N") = IIf(result = 0, 1, 0)
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    HlpFlagCalcZeroAndSign = pFlags("N")
End Function
' ---  ---

' SetReg always updates internal state; paints UI only if not deferred.
Public Function SetReg(ByVal register As String, ByVal value As Long)
    If pRegs.Exists(register) Then
        pRegs(register) = value
        mUIRegsDirty = True
        SetReg = value
    Else
        SetReg = -1
    End If
End Function
Public Function SetFlag(ByVal Flag As String, ByVal value As Long)
    If pFlags.Exists(Flag) Then
        pFlags(Flag) = value
        mUIFlagsDirty = True
        SetFlag = value
    Else
        SetFlag = -1
    End If
End Function
' PRI
' Print Immediate op1 value in either Hex or Ascii depending on A Register value
' op2 used to indicate whether to:
'   "X0": just print the byte
'   "X1": add space before after
'   "X2": add crlf after
'   "X3": add space before and crlf after
'   "0X": print ascii character
'   "1X": print hex character
Public Function PRI(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 425
    Dim options As Long
    Dim prtSpace As Boolean, prtCrLf As Boolean, prtHex As Boolean
    Dim out As String
    Dim dec_op1 As Long
    Dim lbl As clsLabelRecord
    
    ' 1) Operand required
    If op1 = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, "PRI: Missing Operand"
        PRI = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If

    ' 2) Allow EQU labels as immediate (like your MVI does)
    Set lbl = pLabels.GetLabel(op1)
    If Not lbl Is Nothing Then
        op1 = lbl.clsAddressHex  ' use the label's hex value/address
    End If

    Dim op2 As Long
    op2 = pRegs("A")
    
    options = usrHexToDec(op2) And 255
    prtSpace = options And 1
    prtCrLf = options And 2
    prtHex = options And 16

    ' 3) Validate immediate (8-bit)
    If prtHex And Not usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, "PRI: Invalid Hex Immediate: " & op1
        PRI = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    If prtHex Then
        out = usrHexToAscii(op1)
    Else
        out = op1
    End If
    
    ConsolePrint out, prtCrLf, prtSpace
    PRI = 0
End Function

' PRT
' Prints literal string located at M (HL address pointer).  String is delimted by 0h end of line
' Reg A used to indicate whether to:
'   "X0": just print the byte
'   "X1": add space before after
'   "X2": add crlf after
'   "X3": add space before and crlf after
' prints its clsData. Optional CR/LF and space prefix handled by flags.
Public Function PRT() As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 428
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord
    Dim address As String
    Dim address_high As String
    Dim address_low As String
    Dim dec_addr As Long
    Dim options As Long
    Dim prtSpace As Boolean, prtCrLf As Boolean
    Dim out As String
    Const MAX_STRING As Long = 1024   ' Maximum string length
    Dim outLen As Long: outLen = 0
    Dim outChar As Long
    
    options = pRegs("A") And 255
    prtSpace = options And 1
    prtCrLf = options And 2
    
    ' Resolve address in HL
    address_high = Right("00" & usrDecToHexString(pRegs("H")), 2)
    address_low = Right("00" & usrDecToHexString(pRegs("L")), 2)
    address = address_high & address_low
    
    out = ""
    dec_addr = usrHexToDec(address)
    outChar = pMemory.addr(dec_addr)
    If HlpMemCheckError("PRTN", dec_addr, errorBase) Then
        PRT = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    Do While outChar <> 0 And outLen < MAX_STRING
        out = out & Chr(outChar)
        dec_addr = dec_addr + 1
        outChar = pMemory.addr(dec_addr)
        If HlpMemCheckError("PRTN", dec_addr, errorBase) Then
            PRT = errorBase
            Exit Function
        End If
        outLen = outLen + 1
    Loop
    
    ConsolePrint out, prtCrLf, prtSpace
    PRT = 0
End Function


' PRTN
' If op2 provided, prints literal; otherwise resolves HL to a data label and
' prints its clsData. Optional CR/LF and space prefix handled by flags.
Public Function PRTN(Optional ByVal op2 As String, _
                     Optional ByVal crlf As Boolean = False, _
                     Optional ByVal prtSpace As Boolean = False) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 425
    Dim record As clsLabelRecord
    Dim address As String
    Dim address_high As String
    Dim address_low As String

    If Len(op2) > 0 Then
        ConsolePrint op2, crlf, prtSpace
        PRTN = 0
        Exit Function
    End If

    ' Resolve address in HL
    address_high = Right("00" & usrDecToHexString(pRegs("H")), 2)
    address_low = Right("00" & usrDecToHexString(pRegs("L")), 2)
    address = address_high & address_low
    Set record = pLabels.GetByXref(address)
    If record Is Nothing Then
        SetError errorBase, "PRTN: Missing Label for Address: " & address
        PRTN = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If

    ConsolePrint record.clsData, crlf, prtSpace
    PRTN = 0
End Function

Public Function PRTNS(Optional ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    ' space + text (no newline)
    PRTNS = PRTN(op2, False, True)
End Function

Public Function prtCrLf(Optional ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    ' newline, no leading space
    prtCrLf = PRTN(op2, True, False)
End Function

Public Function PRTCRLFS(Optional ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    ' newline + leading space
    PRTCRLFS = PRTN(op2, True, True)
End Function

    RefreshStack = pStack.ShowStack(refresh)
