Public Function GetInput(ByVal errorBase As Long) As Boolean
    Dim inputStr As String
    Dim addr As Long
    Dim addr_high As Long, addr_low As Long
    Dim i As Long
    'inputStr = InputBox("Enter Text:", "Console Input")
    inputStr = usrForm.tbInput.value
    If inputStr <> "" Then
        addr_high = pRegs("H")
        addr_low = pRegs("L")
        addr = addr_high * 256 + addr_low - 1
        For i = 1 To Len(inputStr)
            pMemory.addr(addr + i) = Asc(Mid(inputStr, i, 1))
            If HlpMemCheckError("IN", addr + i, errorBase) Then
                GetInput = False
                Exit Function
            End If
        Next i
        pMemory.addr(addr + Len(inputStr) + 1) = 0
        If HlpMemCheckError("IN", addr + Len(inputStr) + 1, errorBase) Then
            GetInput = False
            Exit Function
        End If
    End If
    GetInput = True
End Function

' ==========================
' Memory / Operand helpers
' ==========================
Private Function HlpMemAddrFromHL() As Long
    HlpMemAddrFromHL = ((pRegs("H") And 255) * 256&) + (pRegs("L") And 255)
End Function

Private Function HlpResolveReg08(ByVal operand As String, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Variant
    operand = UCase$(Trim$(operand))
    If operand = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, opname & ": Missing operand"
        HlpResolveReg08 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    If operand = "M" Then
        HlpResolveReg08 = CLng(pMemory.addr(HlpMemAddrFromHL())) And 255
        If HlpMemCheckError(opname, HlpMemAddrFromHL(), errorBase) Then
            HlpResolveReg08 = Empty
        End If
        Exit Function
    End If

    If pRegs.Exists(operand) Then
        HlpResolveReg08 = CLng(pRegs(operand)) And 255
        Exit Function
    End If

    SetError errorBase, opname & ": Invalid operand: " & operand
    HlpResolveReg08 = Empty
End Function

Private Function HlpStoreReg08(ByVal dest As String, ByVal value As Long, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Boolean
    dest = UCase$(Trim$(dest))
    value = value And 255

    If dest = "M" Then
        pMemory.addr(HlpMemAddrFromHL()) = CByte(value)
        If HlpMemCheckError(opname, HlpMemAddrFromHL(), errorBase) Then
            HlpStoreReg08 = False
        Else
            HlpStoreReg08 = True
        End If
        Exit Function
    End If

    If pRegs.Exists(dest) Then
        SetReg dest, value
        HlpStoreReg08 = True
        Exit Function
    End If

    SetError errorBase, opname & ": Invalid destination: " & dest
    HlpStoreReg08 = False
End Function

Private Function HlpResolveAddr16(ByVal token As String, ByVal errorBase As Long, ByVal opname As String) As Variant
    Dim lbl As clsLabelRecord
    token = UCase$(Trim$(token))

    If token = "" Then
        SetError errorBase, opname & ": Missing address"
        HlpResolveAddr16 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    Set lbl = pLabels.GetLabel(token)
    If Not lbl Is Nothing Then token = lbl.clsAddressHex

    If Not usrValIsHexString(token) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, opname & ": Invalid address: " & token
        HlpResolveAddr16 = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If

    HlpResolveAddr16 = usrHexToDec(token) And &HFFFF&
End Function
Private Function HlpFlagPack() As Byte
    Dim f As Byte
    If pFlags("Sign") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H80
    If pFlags("Zero") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H40
    If pFlags("AC") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H10
    If pFlags("Parity") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H4
    If pFlags("N") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H2
    If pFlags("Carry") <> 0 Then f = f Or &H1
    HlpFlagPack = f
End Function

Private Sub HlpFlagUnpack(ByVal f As Byte)
    HlpFlagCalcSign IIf((f And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
    HlpFlagCalcZero IIf((f And &H40) <> 0, 1, 0)
    HlpFlagCalcAC IIf((f And &H10) <> 0, 1, 0)
    HlpFlagCalcParity IIf((f And &H4) <> 0, 1, 0)
    HlpFlagCalcCarry IIf((f And &H1) <> 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("N") = IIf((f And &H2) <> 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("Carry") = IIf((f And &H1) <> 0, 1, 0)
End Sub
' ==============================================================================
' BIT (Test Bit)
' Usage: BIT bit_pos, source
' Opcode:   CB 01bbsss (bb = bit 0-7, sss = source register)
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (12 if memory)
'
' Operation:   Test bit in source; set Zero flag if bit is 0
' Flags Affected:
'   Z = 1 if bit is 0 (bit not set)
'   Z = 0 if bit is 1 (bit is set)
'   S, P affected per result
'
' Examples:
'   BIT 0, A        - Test bit 0 of A (check if LSB is set)
'   BIT 7, B        - Test bit 7 of B (check sign bit)
'   BIT 3, M        - Test bit 3 of memory at (HL)
'
' Common Use:
'   BIT 0, A
'   JZ IS_EVEN      - Jump if bit 0 clear (even number)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function BIT(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2020
    Dim src As Variant
    Dim bitNum As Long
    
    If Not IsNumeric(op1) Or val(op1) < 0 Or val(op1) > 7 Then
        SetError errorBase, "BIT: Invalid BIT " & op1
    End If
    
    bitNum = CLng(val(op1))
    src = HlpResolveReg08(op2, errorBase, "BIT")
    If IsEmpty(src) Then BIT = errorBase: Exit Function
    
    ' Set Zero flag if bit is 0
    pFlags("Zero") = IIf((src And (2 ^ bitNum)) = 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("N") = 0        ' Z80 BIT resets N flag
    pFlags("AC") = 1       ' Z80 BIT sets Half-Carry flag
    mUIFlagsDirty = True
    BIT = 0
End Function
' ==============================================================================
' SET (Set Bit)
' SET_BIT bit_pos, dest
' Opcode:   CB 11bbddd (bb = bit 0-7, ddd = dest register)
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (15 if memory)
'
' Operation:   Set specified bit to 1 in destination
' Flags:       None affected
'
' Examples:
'   SET 7, A        - Set bit 7 of A (0x80 | A)
'   SET 0, C        - Set bit 0 of C
'   SET 4, M        - Set bit 4 of memory at (HL)
' ==============================================================================
Public Function SET_BIT(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim bitNum As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2050
    
    If Not IsNumeric(op1) Or val(op1) < 0 Or val(op1) > 7 Then
        SetError errorBase, "SET_BIT: Invalid BIT " & op1
        SET_BIT = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    bitNum = CLng(val(op1))
    If Not pRegs.Exists(op2) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, "SET_BIT: Invalid Register" & op2
        SET_BIT = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    pRegs(op2) = pRegs(op2) Or (2 ^ bitNum)
    mUIRegsDirty = True
    SET_BIT = 0
End Function
' ==============================================================================
' RES (Reset Bit)
' Usage: RES_BIT bit_pos, dest
' Opcode:   CB 10bbddd (bb = bit 0-7, ddd = dest register)
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (15 if memory)
'
' Operation:   Clear specified bit to 0 in destination
' Flags:       None affected
'
' Examples:
'   RES 7, A        - Clear bit 7 of A (A & 0x7F)
'   RES 0, H        - Clear bit 0 of H
' ==============================================================================
Public Function RES_BIT(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim bitNum As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2050
    
    If Not IsNumeric(op1) Or val(op1) < 0 Or val(op1) > 7 Then
        SetError errorBase, "RES_BIT: Invalid BIT " & op1
        RES_BIT = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    bitNum = CLng(val(op1))
    If Not pRegs.Exists(op2) Then
        SetError errorBase + 1, "RES_BIT: Invalid Register" & op2
        RES_BIT = errorBase + 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    pRegs(op2) = pRegs(op2) And (Not (2 ^ bitNum))
    RES_BIT = 0
End Function
Public Function CB(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2030
    Dim result As Boolean
    ' Extract the sub-opcode from your op1 column
    Dim subOp As Byte
    subOp = CByte(usrHexToDec(CStr(op1)))
    ' Call the handler - passing the CPU object so it can modify registers
    result = HlpHandleCBPrefix(subOp, errorBase)
    If Not result Then
        CB = errorBase
        Exit Function
    End If
    CB = 0
End Function

' Helper to calculate (IX+d) or (IY+d)
Private Function HlpMemGetIndexedAddr(ByVal regName As String, ByVal displacement As Variant) As Long
    Dim baseAddr As Long
    Dim d As Integer
    
    baseAddr = pRegs(regName)
    
    ' Convert hex displacement to signed integer
    d = CInt(usrHexToDec(CStr(displacement)))
    If d > 127 Then d = d - 256 ' Handle signed 8-bit wrap
    
    HlpMemGetIndexedAddr = (baseAddr + d) And &HFFFF&
End Function
Public Function HlpHandleCBPrefix(ByVal subOp As Byte, ByVal errorBase As Long) As Long
    ' subOp is the byte that follows the CB prefix
    Dim result As Boolean
    Select Case subOp
        ' 00h - 3Fh are all Shifts/Rotates
        Case &H0 To &H3F
            HlpHandleCBPrefix = HlpHandleCBShifts(subOp, "CB", errorBase)
            Exit Function
        ' 40h - 7Fh are BIT b, r
        Case &H40 To &H7F
            ' Logic for BIT...
            
        ' 80h - BFh are RES b, r
        Case &H80 To &HBF
            ' Logic for RES...
            
        ' C0h - FFh are SET b, r
        Case &HC0 To &HFF
            ' Logic for SET...
    End Select
    HlpHandleCBPrefix = 0
End Function
' ==============================================================================
' RLC (Rotate A Left Circular)
' Usage: RLC
' Opcode:   00000111
' 8080:     1 byte, 4 cycles
' Z80:      1 byte, 4 cycles
'
' Operation:   A ? A << 1, bit 7 ? CY, CY ? bit 0
'
' Example:
'   Before:  A = 10110010, CY = 0
'   After:   A = 01100101, CY = 1  (bit 7 was 1)
'
' Flags Affected:
'   CY = old bit 7
'   All other flags unchanged
'
' Common Uses:
'   - Rotating bits left
'   - Extracting MSB
'   - Bit pattern manipulation
'
' Error Codes: None (no operands)
' ==============================================================================
' ==============================================================================
' SLA dest
' Opcode:   CB 00100ddd
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (15 if memory)
'
' Operation:
'   Shift left; bit 0 becomes 0; bit 7 moves to Carry
'   Before:  [bit7][bit6]...[bit1][bit0]
'   After:   [bit6]...[bit1][bit0][0] <- Carry gets old bit7
'
' Flags:       CY = old bit 7, Z,S,P per result
'
' Notes:
'   - Equivalent to multiply by 2
'   - Sign bit preserved implicitly (next SLA will rotate it out)
' ==============================================================================
' ==============================================================================
' SRL dest
' Opcode:   CB 00111ddd
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (15 if memory)
'
' Operation:
'   Shift right; bit 7 becomes 0; bit 0 moves to Carry
'   Before:  [bit7][bit6]...[bit1][bit0]
'   After:   [0][bit7]...[bit2][bit1] <- Carry gets old bit0
'
' Flags:       CY = old bit 0, Z,S,P per result
'
' Notes:
'   - Equivalent to unsigned divide by 2
' ==============================================================================
' ==============================================================================
' SRA dest
' Opcode:   CB 00101ddd
' 8080:     NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:      2 bytes, 8 cycles (15 if memory)
'
' Operation:
'   Shift right; bit 7 preserved (sign-extending); bit 0 to Carry
'   Before:  [bit7][bit6]...[bit1][bit0]
'   After:   [bit7][bit7]...[bit2][bit1] <- Carry gets old bit0
'
' Flags:       CY = old bit 0, Z,S,P per result
'
' Notes:
'   - Preserves sign (arithmetic right shift)
'   - Equivalent to signed divide by 2
'   - Negative numbers shift in with 1s (preserved sign)
' ==============================================================================
Private Function HlpHandleCBShifts(ByVal op As Byte, ByVal opcode As String, ByVal errorBase As Long) As Boolean
    Dim regCode As Integer, opCodeType As Integer
    Dim regName As String
    Dim val As Byte, oldCarry As Byte, carryOut As Byte
    Dim res As Long ' Long to prevent overflow during bit shifts
    
    ' 1. Identify Register and Operation
    regCode = op And &H7          ' Bits 0-2: Register
    opCodeType = (op \ 8) And &H7 ' Bits 3-5: Operation
    
    ' 2. Get the value (Register or (HL))
    If regCode = 6 Then
        val = pMemory.addr(RegGet16("HL"))
        If HlpMemCheckError(opcode, Me.RegGet16("HL"), errorBase) Then
            HlpHandleCBShifts = False
            Exit Function
        End If
    Else
        regName = HlpRegGetName(regCode)
        val = pRegs(regName)
    End If
    
    oldCarry = pFlags("Carry")
    
    ' 3. Perform Operation
    Select Case opCodeType
        Case 0 ' RLC (Rotate Left Circular)
            carryOut = IIf((val And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
            res = ((val * 2) Or carryOut) And &HFF
            
        Case 1 ' RRC (Rotate Right Circular)
            carryOut = val And &H1
            res = (val \ 2) Or (carryOut * 128)
            
        Case 2 ' RL (Rotate Left through Carry)
            carryOut = IIf((val And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
            res = ((val * 2) Or oldCarry) And &HFF
            
        Case 3 ' RR (Rotate Right through Carry)
            carryOut = val And &H1
            res = (val \ 2) Or (oldCarry * 128)
            
        Case 4 ' SLA (Shift Left Arithmetic - Bit 0 becomes 0)
            carryOut = IIf((val And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
            res = (val * 2) And &HFF
            
        Case 5 ' SRA (Shift Right Arithmetic - Bit 7 is preserved)
            carryOut = val And &H1
            res = (val \ 2) Or (val And &H80)
            
        Case 6 ' SLL (Shift Left Logical - Bit 0 becomes 1, technically undocumented)
            carryOut = IIf((val And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
            res = ((val * 2) Or 1) And &HFF
            
        Case 7 ' SRL (Shift Right Logical - Bit 7 becomes 0)
            carryOut = val And &H1
            res = val \ 2
    End Select
    
    ' 4. Update Result
    If regCode = 6 Then
        pMemory.addr(RegGet16("HL")) = CByte(res)
    Else
        pRegs(regName) = CByte(res)
    End If
    
    ' 5. Update Z80 Flags
    pFlags("Carry") = carryOut
    pFlags("Zero") = IIf(res = 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("Sign") = IIf((res And &H80) <> 0, 1, 0)
    pFlags("Parity") = HlpFlagCalcParity(CByte(res)) ' P/V stores parity for shifts
    pFlags("AC") = 0 ' Half-carry is always reset
    pFlags("N") = 0  ' Add/Subtract is always reset
    HlpHandleCBShifts = True
End Function
Private Function HlpRegGetName(ByVal code As Integer) As String
    Select Case code
        Case 0: HlpRegGetName = "B"
        Case 1: HlpRegGetName = "C"
        Case 2: HlpRegGetName = "D"
        Case 3: HlpRegGetName = "E"
        Case 4: HlpRegGetName = "H"
        Case 5: HlpRegGetName = "L"
        Case 7: HlpRegGetName = "A"
        Case Else: HlpRegGetName = "" ' 6 is (HL), handled separately
    End Select
End Function
Private Function HlpRegGetCode(ByVal Reg As String) As Byte
    ' Standard Z80/8080 Register Mapping:
    ' B=000, C=001, D=010, E=011, H=100, L=101, (HL)=110, A=111
    
    Select Case UCase(Trim(Reg))
        Case "B": HlpRegGetCode = 0
        Case "C": HlpRegGetCode = 1
        Case "D": HlpRegGetCode = 2
        Case "E": HlpRegGetCode = 3
        Case "H": HlpRegGetCode = 4
        Case "L": HlpRegGetCode = 5
        Case "(HL)", "M": HlpRegGetCode = 6 ' "M" is the 8080 name for (HL)
        Case "A": HlpRegGetCode = 7
        Case Else
            ' If the register isn't standard (like IX), we return 255 to flag an error
            HlpRegGetCode = 255
    End Select
End Function
Public Function RegGet16(ByVal regPair As String) As Long
    Dim result As Long
    
    ' Standardize input: remove spaces and handle different prime notations
    Dim key As String
    key = UCase(Trim(regPair))
    key = Replace(key, "PRIME", "'") ' Handle "BCPRIME" -> "BC'"
    
    Select Case key
        ' --- Standard Main Register Pairs ---
        Case "BC"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("B")) * 256) + pRegs("C")
        Case "DE"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("D")) * 256) + pRegs("E")
        Case "HL"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("H")) * 256) + pRegs("L")
        Case "AF"
            ' Uses your HlpFlagPack() to convert dictionary flags to a byte
            result = (CLng(pRegs("A")) * 256) + HlpFlagPack()

        ' --- Z80 Shadow (Prime) Pairs ---
        Case "BC'", "BC1"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("Bp")) * 256) + pRegs("C'")
        Case "DE'", "DE1"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("Dp")) * 256) + pRegs("E'")
        Case "HL'", "HL1"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("Hp")) * 256) + pRegs("L'")
        Case "AF'", "AF1"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("Ap")) * 256) + pRegs("F'")

        ' --- Index and Special Registers ---
        Case "IX"
            result = CLng(pRegs("IX"))
        Case "IY"
            result = CLng(pRegs("IY"))
        Case "SP"
            result = CLng(pRegs("SP"))
        Case "PC"
            result = CLng(pRegs("PC"))
            
        ' --- Special 8-bit combinations (I and R) ---
        Case "IR"
            result = (CLng(pRegs("I")) * 256) + pRegs("R")

        Case Else
            Debug.Print "Warning: RegGet16 unknown register: " & regPair
            result = 0
    End Select
    
    ' Apply the 16-bit mask to ensure no overflow and force positive Long
    RegGet16 = result And &HFFFF&
End Function
Public Sub SetReg16(ByVal regPair As String, ByVal value As Long)
    Dim val As Long
    val = value And &HFFFF& ' Safety mask
    
    Select Case UCase(Trim(regPair))
        Case "BC": pRegs("B") = (val \ 256): pRegs("C") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "DE": pRegs("D") = (val \ 256): pRegs("E") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "HL": pRegs("H") = (val \ 256): pRegs("L") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "AF"
            pRegs("A") = (val \ 256)
            HlpFlagUnpack CByte(val And &HFF) ' Updates pFlags dictionary
            
        Case "BC'": pRegs("Bp") = (val \ 256): pRegs("Cp") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "DE'": pRegs("Dp") = (val \ 256): pRegs("Ep") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "HL'": pRegs("Hp") = (val \ 256): pRegs("Lp") = (val And &HFF)
        Case "AF'": pRegs("Ap") = (val \ 256): pRegs("Fp") = (val And &HFF)
            
        Case "IX": pRegs("IX") = val
        Case "IY": pRegs("IY") = val
        Case "SP": pRegs("SP") = val
        Case "PC": pRegs("PC") = val
    End Select
    mUIRegsDirty = True
End Sub
' ==============================================================================
' Indexed Addressing: (IX+d) and (IY+d)
'
' Purpose:    Access memory at (Index Register + signed displacement)
' Example:    LD A, (IX+5)     - Load A from memory at IX + 5
'             LD (IY-2), B     - Store B to memory at IY - 2
'
' Operand (d) is a signed 8-bit value (-128 to +127)
'
' 8080:       NOT AVAILABLE
' Z80:        Available with DD or FD prefix
'   DD = IX prefix
'   FD = IY prefix
'
' Execution:  address = Index_Reg + sign_extend(d)
'             Then perform operation at [address]
'
' Cycles:     Generally +4 cycles vs non-indexed variant
'             Example: LD A, (HL) = 7 cycles
'                      LD A, (IX+0) = 15 cycles (DD+opcode+displacement)
'
' Notes:
'   - Displacement is signed; allows negative offsets
'   - Essential for Z80 array/structure access
'   - Requires 2-byte opcode: DD/FD, then regular opcode
' ==============================================================================
Private Function LD(ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Long
    Dim errorBase As Long: errorBase = 2040
    On Error Resume Next
    Dim addr As Long
    ' 1. Indexed Target: LD (IX+5), A
    If InStr(op1, "(") > 0 And (InStr(op1, "IX") > 0 Or InStr(op1, "IY") > 0) Then
        addr = HlpMemParseIndexAddr(op1)
        pMemory.addr(addr) = HlpGetOperandValue(op2)
        If HlpMemCheckError("LD", addr, errorBase) Then
            LD = errorBase
            Exit Function
        End If
    ' 2. Indexed Source: LD A, (IX-1)
    ElseIf InStr(op2, "(") > 0 And (InStr(op2, "IX") > 0 Or InStr(op2, "IY") > 0) Then
        addr = HlpMemParseIndexAddr(op2)
        pRegs(op1) = pMemory.addr(addr)
        If HlpMemCheckError("LD", addr, errorBase + 1) Then
            LD = errorBase + 1
            Exit Function
        End If
    ' 3. 16-Bit Register: LD HL, 1234H
    ElseIf usrIsRegister16Bit(op1) Then
        SetReg16 op1, usrHexToDec(CStr(op2))
    ' 4. Standard 8-bit: LD A, B
    Else
        SetReg op1, HlpGetOperandValue(op2)
    End If
    LD = 0
End Function
' Helper: Determines if the operand is a register or a hex literal
Private Function HlpGetOperandValue(ByVal op As String) As Byte
    op = Trim(UCase(op))
    If pRegs.Exists(op) Then
        ' It's a register (A, B, C, etc.)
        HlpGetOperandValue = CByte(pRegs(op) And &HFF)
    Else
        ' It's a hex value (e.g., 55H or 0xFF)
        HlpGetOperandValue = CByte(usrHexToDec(CStr(op)) And &HFF)
    End If
End Function

Private Function HlpMemParseIndexAddr(ByVal s As String) As Long
    ' Purpose: Converts strings like "(IX+05H)" or "(IY-1H)" into a 16-bit address
    ' s: The operand string from the Excel sheet
    
    On Error GoTo ParseError
    
    Dim cleanS As String
    cleanS = UCase(Replace(Replace(s, "(", ""), ")", "")) ' Remove parentheses
    
    Dim regPart As String
    Dim offsetPart As String
    Dim baseAddr As Long
    Dim offsetValue As Long
    
    ' Determine if we are using IX or IY
    regPart = Left(cleanS, 2) ' Should be IX or IY
    baseAddr = RegGet16(regPart)
    
    ' Check if there is an offset (+ or -)
    If InStr(cleanS, "+") > 0 Then
        offsetPart = Mid(cleanS, InStr(cleanS, "+") + 1)
        offsetValue = usrHexToDec(offsetPart)
    ElseIf InStr(cleanS, "-") > 0 Then
        offsetPart = Mid(cleanS, InStr(cleanS, "-") + 1)
        ' Ensure the offset is subtracted
        offsetValue = -usrHexToDec(offsetPart)
    Else
        ' No offset provided, e.g., "(IX)"
        offsetValue = 0
    End If
    
    ' Z80 addresses are 16-bit, so we use And &HFFFF& to wrap around
    HlpMemParseIndexAddr = (baseAddr + offsetValue) And &HFFFF&
    Exit Function

ParseError:
    Debug.Print "Error parsing Indexed Address: " & s
    HlpMemParseIndexAddr = 0
End Function

Private Function HlpMemCheckError(ByVal opcode As String, ByVal addr As Long, ByVal errorBase As Long) As Boolean
    If pMemory.MemError Then
        SetError errorBase, opcode & ": Invalid Memory Address: " & addr
        HlpMemCheckError = True
    Else
        HlpMemCheckError = False
    End If
End Function
'==============================================================================
' INTERNAL ALU HELPER FUNCTIONS
' These consolidate flag calculation logic for arithmetic and logical operations
'==============================================================================

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_Addition
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit addition with automatic flag calculation
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to add to A
'               includeCarry - If True, add carry flag to result
' Side Effects: Updates A, CY, AC, Z, S, P flags
'
' Flag Logic:
'   CY = 1 if sum > 255 (overflow)
'   AC = 1 if carry from bit 3 (nibble overflow)
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   N  = 0 (addition, not subtraction)
'
' Used by: ADD, ADI, ADC, ACI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_Addition(ByVal operandValue As Long, Optional ByVal includeCarry As Boolean = False)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, sum As Long, result As Long
    Dim ac As Long, cy As Long
    
    ' Get current A register
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    
    ' Add carry if requested (ADC/ACI instructions)
    If includeCarry Then
        b = b + pFlags("Carry")
    End If
    
    ' Perform addition
    sum = a + b
    result = sum And 255
    
    ' Calculate flags
    cy = IIf(sum > 255, 1, 0)                           ' Carry from bit 7
    ac = IIf(((a And &HF) + (b And &HF)) > &HF, 1, 0)  ' Carry from bit 3
    
    ' Set flags
    pFlags("Carry") = cy
    HlpFlagCalcAC ac
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result
    ' N flag = 0 (addition)
    If pFlags.Exists("N") Then pFlags("N") = 0
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_Subtraction
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit subtraction with automatic flag calculation
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to subtract from A
'               includeBorrow - If True, subtract borrow flag from result
' Side Effects: Updates A, CY, AC, Z, S, P, N flags
'
' Flag Logic:
'   CY = 1 if A < operand (borrow)
'   AC = 1 if borrow from bit 3
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   N  = 1 (subtraction operation, used for DAA)
'
' Used by: SUB, SUI, SBB, SBI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_Subtraction(ByVal operandValue As Long, Optional ByVal includeBorrow As Boolean = False)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, diff As Long, result As Long
    Dim borrow As Long, acBorrow As Long
    
    ' Get current A register
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    
    ' Subtract borrow if requested (SBB/SBI instructions)
    If includeBorrow Then
        b = b + pFlags("Carry")
    End If
    
    ' Calculate borrow before subtraction
    borrow = IIf(a < b, 1, 0)                        ' Borrow needed from bit 7
    acBorrow = IIf((a And &HF) < (b And &HF), 1, 0) ' Borrow from bit 3
    
    ' Perform subtraction (wrap-around for borrow)
    diff = a - b
    result = diff And 255  ' Mask to 8-bit (handles wrap-around)
    
    ' Set flags
    pFlags("Carry") = borrow           ' CY = 1 indicates borrow
    HlpFlagCalcAC acBorrow
    SetReg "A", result
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result
    ' N flag = 1 (subtraction)
    If pFlags.Exists("N") Then pFlags("N") = 1
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_AND
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit logical AND with automatic flag calculation
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to AND with A
' Side Effects: Updates A, Z, S, P flags
'               CY = 0, AC = 1 (Z80 behavior)
'
' Flag Logic:
'   A  = A AND operand
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   CY = 0 (always cleared)
'   AC = 1 (always set, Z80 behavior)
'
' Used by: ANA, ANI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_AND(ByVal operandValue As Long)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, result As Long
    
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    result = a And b
    
    ' Set result and flags
    SetReg "A", result
    pFlags("Carry") = 0      ' CY = 0 (always)
    pFlags("AC") = 1         ' AC = 1 (Z80 behavior)
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_OR
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit logical OR with automatic flag calculation
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to OR with A
' Side Effects: Updates A, Z, S, P flags
'               CY = 0, AC = 0
'
' Flag Logic:
'   A  = A OR operand
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   CY = 0 (always cleared)
'   AC = 0 (always cleared)
'
' Used by: ORA, ORI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_OR(ByVal operandValue As Long)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, result As Long
    
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    result = a Or b
    
    ' Set result and flags
    SetReg "A", result
    pFlags("Carry") = 0
    pFlags("AC") = 0
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_XOR
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit logical XOR with automatic flag calculation
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to XOR with A
' Side Effects: Updates A, Z, S, P flags
'               CY = 0, AC = 0
'
' Flag Logic:
'   A  = A XOR operand
'   Z  = 1 if result is 0
'   S  = 1 if bit 7 is set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   CY = 0 (always cleared)
'   AC = 0 (always cleared)
'
' Used by: XRA, XRI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_XOR(ByVal operandValue As Long)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, result As Long
    
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    result = a Xor b
    
    ' Set result and flags
    SetReg "A", result
    pFlags("Carry") = 0
    pFlags("AC") = 0
    HlpFlagCalcSign result
    HlpFlagCalcZero result
    HlpFlagCalcParity result
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' HlpALU_Compare
' Purpose:      Perform 8-bit subtraction for comparison (discard result)
' Input:        operandValue - 8-bit value to compare with A
' Side Effects: Updates Z, S, P, CY, AC flags (A register unchanged)
'
' Flag Logic: Same as subtraction, but A is not modified
'   Z  = 1 if A == operand
'   S  = 1 if (A - operand) has bit 7 set
'   P  = 1 if even parity
'   CY = 1 if A < operand (borrow)
'   AC = 1 if borrow from bit 3
'
' Used by: CMP, CPI
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Private Sub HlpALU_Compare(ByVal operandValue As Long)
    Dim a As Long, b As Long, diff As Long
    Dim borrow As Long, acBorrow As Long
    
    a = pRegs("A") And 255
    b = operandValue And 255
    
    ' Calculate borrow before subtraction
    borrow = IIf(a < b, 1, 0)
    acBorrow = IIf((a And &HF) < (b And &HF), 1, 0)
    
    ' Perform subtraction (but don't save result to A)
    diff = a - b
    diff = diff And 255  ' Mask to 8-bit
    
    ' Set flags based on result (A unchanged)
    pFlags("Carry") = borrow
    HlpFlagCalcAC acBorrow
    HlpFlagCalcSign diff     ' Sign of result
    HlpFlagCalcZero diff     ' Zero flag from result
    HlpFlagCalcParity diff   ' Parity of result
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' CPUMode
' Reads the named range "CPUMode" from the CPU sheet.
' Returns "8080" as the safe default if the range is missing or blank.
'
' SETUP: add a cell to the CPU sheet, name it "CPUMode", give it a dropdown:
'   Data Validation > List > source:  8080,Z80,6510
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function cpuMode() As String
    On Error Resume Next
    Dim v As String
    v = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU").Range("CPUMode").value)))
    If Err.Number <> 0 Or v = "" Then v = "8080"
    On Error GoTo 0
    cpuMode = v
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' IsCPU6510  —  convenience wrapper
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function IsCPU6510() As Boolean
    IsCPU6510 = (cpuMode() = "6510")
End Function

Public Sub ResetAddressList()
    Set pAddressList = Nothing
End Sub
Public Sub InitHexTable()
    Dim i As Long ' Use Long to avoid overflow during loop
    For i = 0 To 255
        ' IMPORTANT: Use the built-in Hex$ function here, NOT usrDecToHexString
        HexTable(i) = Right$("0" & Hex$(i), 2)
    Next i
    mIHexIintialized = True
End Sub
Public Function usrDecToHexString(ByVal value As Long) As String
    If Not mIHexIintialized Then InitHexTable
    
    ' Handle values as 16-bit if they exceed 255
    ' This covers PC, SP, and address operands automatically
    If value > 255 Then
        usrDecToHexString = HexTable(value \ 256) & HexTable(value Mod 256)
    ElseIf value < 0 Then
        ' Handle potential negative overflows if any
        usrDecToHexString = "0000"
    Else
        ' Standard 8-bit register (A, B, C, etc.)
        usrDecToHexString = HexTable(value)
    End If
End Function
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' usrValIsHexString
' Purpose:      Validate hex string input (with multiple format tolerances)
' Input:        hexValue - String to validate (may have leading/trailing space,
'                          trailing "H" suffix, or padding)
' Returns:      True if valid hex (1-4 digits, 0-9 A-F), False otherwise
' Examples:
'   usrValIsHexString("FF")      ? True
'   usrValIsHexString("0xFF")    ? True
'   usrValIsHexString(" FF ")    ? True
'   usrValIsHexString("FFH")     ? True
'   usrValIsHexString("F")       ? True (padded to 0F)
'   usrValIsHexString("FFFF")    ? True
'   usrValIsHexString("GG")      ? False (invalid hex digits)
'   usrValIsHexString("FFFFFF")  ? False (too long)
'
' Note: This consolidates usrIsValidHex() and the older validation logic
'       with better error handling and more flexible input tolerance.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function usrValIsHexString(ByVal hexValue As String) As Boolean
    Dim length As Long
    
    ' Step 1: Normalize input
    hexValue = Trim$(hexValue)                      ' Remove leading/trailing spaces
    hexValue = UCase$(hexValue)                     ' Convert to uppercase
    hexValue = Replace(hexValue, "H", "")           ' Remove trailing "H" if present
    
    ' Step 2: Check length
    length = Len(hexValue)
    
    ' Pad single or triple-digit hex to even length (2 or 4)
    If length = 1 Or length = 3 Then
        hexValue = "0" & hexValue
        length = length + 1
    End If
    
    ' Step 3: Validate length (must be 2 or 4 after padding)
    If length <> 2 And length <> 4 Then
        usrValIsHexString = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Step 4: Validate hex digits (0-9, A-F only)
    ' Pattern: "*[!0-9a-fA-F]*" matches any character that is NOT hex
    If hexValue Like "*[!0-9A-F]*" Then
        usrValIsHexString = False
    Else
        usrValIsHexString = True
    End If
End Function
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Console utilities (modeless)
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Sub ConsolePrint(ByVal text As String, _
                        Optional ByVal crlf As Boolean = True, _
                        Optional ByVal prtSpace As Boolean = False)
    ' 1) Always update the authoritative buffer synchronously
    ConsoleBuffer_Append text, crlf, prtSpace

    ' 2) Optionally update the UI (unchanged behavior)
    'If Not mConsoleOpen Then ShowConsole
    If crlf Then
        usrForm.ConPrtLn text, prtSpace
    Else
        usrForm.ConPrt text, prtSpace
    End If
End Sub

Public Sub ClearConsole()
    usrForm.ClearConsole
End Sub

Public Sub ShowConsole()
    usrForm.Show vbModeless
    mConsoleOpen = True
End Sub
Public Sub ResetConsole()
    usrForm.ResetConsole
End Sub
Public Sub ConsoleBuffer_Clear()
    gConsoleBuffer = vbNullString
End Sub

Public Sub ConsoleBuffer_Append(ByVal s As String, Optional ByVal addCrlf As Boolean = False, Optional ByVal addLeadingSpace As Boolean = False)
    If addLeadingSpace And Len(gConsoleBuffer) > 0 Then gConsoleBuffer = gConsoleBuffer & " "
    gConsoleBuffer = gConsoleBuffer & s
    If addCrlf Then gConsoleBuffer = gConsoleBuffer & vbCrLf
End Sub

Public Function ConsoleBuffer_Text() As String
    ConsoleBuffer_Text = gConsoleBuffer
End Function

Public Sub SelectEngine()
    Select Case cpuMode()
        Case "6510": Execute6510   ' in decExecute6510
        Case Else:   Execute8080   ' in decExecute8080 (renamed from decAssemble)
    End Select
End Sub
Public Sub AssembleForCPUMode()
    Select Case cpuMode()
        Case "6510": Assemble6510_ToMachine
        Case Else:   Assemble8080_ToMachine
    End Select
End Sub

Public Function usrIOReadSwitch(ByVal switch As Long) As Long
    Dim switchStat As Boolean
    Select Case switch
        Case 0:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl0.value
        Case 1:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl1.value
        Case 2:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl2.value
        Case 3:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl3.value
        Case 4:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl4.value
        Case 5:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl5.value
        Case 6:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl6.value
        Case 7:
            switchStat = usrForm.tgl7.value
        Case Else:
            switchStat = False
    End Select
    
    If switchStat Then
        usrIOReadSwitch = 1
    Else
        usrIOReadSwitch = 0
    End If
End Function

Public Sub AutoCalc()
     Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
     Application.Calculate
End Sub
Public Function SmartDelay(ByVal centiSeconds As Long)
    Dim endTime As Double
    endTime = Timer + centiSeconds / 100
    Do While Timer < endTime
        DoEvents
    Loop
    SmartDelay = 0
End Function
Public Function HasUnitTest(instring As String) As Boolean
    Dim ws As Worksheet, r As Range
    Set ws = Sheets("Unit Tests")
    For Each r In ws.Range("A:A")
        If r.value Like "Unit_*" Then
            If InStr(1, CStr(ws.Cells(r.row, "E").value), instring, vbTextCompare) > 0 Then
                HasUnitTest = True
                Exit Function
            End If
        End If
    Next
    HasUnitTest = False
End Function
' z80 additions
' Helper: Simple check to see if we are dealing with 16-bit register logic
Public Function usrIsRegister16Bit(ByVal r As String) As Boolean
    Select Case UCase(Trim(r))
        Case "BC", "DE", "HL", "IX", "IY", "SP", "AF", "BC'", "DE'", "HL'", "AF'": usrIsRegister16Bit = True
        Case Else: usrIsRegister16Bit = False
    End Select
End Function
'================================================================================
' HlpGetInstructionSize  (drop-in replacement for the existing function)
'
' HOW TO APPLY:
'   In modGlobals, select the entire existing HlpGetInstructionSize function
'   from "Public Function HlpGetInstructionSize" to its "End Function" and
'   replace it with this block.
'
' WHAT CHANGED:
'   Added an early CPUMode()="6510" branch at the top of the Select Case.
'   All 6510 mnemonics are handled there and Exit Function immediately,
'   so they never fall through to the 8080/Z80 cases below.
'   The 8080/Z80 section is unchanged.
'================================================================================
Public Function HlpGetInstructionSize( _
    ByVal mnem As String, _
    Optional ByVal op1 As String = "", _
    Optional ByVal op2 As String = "", _
    Optional ByVal cpuModeParam As String = "" _
) As Long

    mnem = UCase$(Trim$(mnem))
    op1 = UCase$(Trim$(op1))
    op2 = UCase$(Trim$(op2))
    Dim setCpuMode As String
    If cpuModeParam = "" Then
        setCpuMode = cpuMode()
    Else
        setCpuMode = UCase$(Trim$(cpuModeParam))
    End If

    Dim size As Long
    size = 1

    '===========================================================================
    ' 6510 PATH
    '===========================================================================
    If setCpuMode = "6510" Then
        Select Case mnem

            Case "", "EQU", "ORG"
                size = 0

            Case "END", "HLT", "STP"
                size = 1

            Case "DB"
                Dim szDB As Long: szDB = 0
                Dim pDB  As Long: pDB = 1
                Dim sDB  As String: sDB = Trim$(op1)
                Do While pDB <= Len(sDB)
                    Do While pDB <= Len(sDB) And _
                            (Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1) = "," Or Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1) = " ")
                        pDB = pDB + 1
                    Loop
                    If pDB > Len(sDB) Then Exit Do
                    If Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1) = Chr$(34) Or Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1) = "'" Then
                        Dim qqDB As String: qqDB = Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1)
                        pDB = pDB + 1
                        Do While pDB <= Len(sDB) And Mid$(sDB, pDB, 1) <> qqDB
                            szDB = szDB + 1
                            pDB = pDB + 1
                        Loop
                        pDB = pDB + 1
                    Else
                        szDB = szDB + 1
                        Dim cpDB As Long: cpDB = InStr(pDB, sDB, ",")
                        If cpDB > 0 Then
                            pDB = cpDB + 1
                        Else
                            Exit Do
                        End If
                    End If
                Loop
                size = IIf(szDB = 0, 1, szDB)

            Case "DS"
                If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
                    size = usrHexToDec(op1)
                ElseIf IsNumeric(op1) Then
                    size = CLng(op1)
                Else
                    size = 0
                End If

            Case "ADC", "AND", "ASL", "BIT", "CMP", "CPX", "CPY", _
                 "DEC", "EOR", "INC", "LDA", "LDX", "LDY", _
                 "LSR", "ORA", "ROL", "ROR", "SBC", "STA", "STX", "STY"
                size = Hlp6510InstrSize(op1)

            Case "BCC", "BCS", "BEQ", "BMI", "BNE", "BPL", "BVC", "BVS"
                size = 2

            Case "JSR", "JMP"
                size = 3

            Case "BRK", "CLC", "CLD", "CLI", "CLV", "DEX", "DEY", _
                 "INX", "INY", "NOP", "PHA", "PHP", "PLA", "PLP", _
                 "RTI", "RTS", "SEC", "SED", "SEI", _
                 "TAX", "TAY", "TSX", "TXA", "TXS", "TYA"
                size = 1

            Case Else
                size = 1

        End Select

        HlpGetInstructionSize = size
        Exit Function

    End If

    '===========================================================================
    ' 8080 / Z80 PATH  (unchanged)
    '===========================================================================
    Select Case mnem

        Case "", "EQU"
            size = 0

        Case "DB"
            size = Len(op1)

        Case "LXI", "JMP", "JC", "JNC", "JZ", "JNZ", _
             "JM", "JPE", "JPO", "CALL", "LDA", "STA", _
             "LHLD", "SHLD"
            size = 3

        Case "CC", "CM", "CNC", "CNZ", "CPE", "CPO", "CZ"
            size = 3

        Case "MVI", "ADI", "ACI", "ANI", "ORI", "XRI", _
             "CPI", "SUI", "SBI", "IN", "OUT", "PRI"
            size = 2

        Case "JR", "DJNZ"
            size = 2

        Case "BIT", "SET", "RES"
            size = 2

        Case "LD"
            size = HlpSizeLD(op1, op2)

        Case "AND"
            size = HlpSizeZ80Enhanced(mnem, op1, op2)

        Case "CPD", "CPDR", "CPIR", "IND", "INDR", "INI", "INIR", _
             "LDD", "LDDR", "LDI", "LDIR", "OTDR", "OTIR", "OUTD", "OUTI"
            size = 2

        Case "NEG", "RETI", "RETN", "RL", "RLD", "RR", "RRD", _
             "SLA", "SLR", "SRA", "SRL"
            size = 2

        Case "IM"
            size = 2

        Case "OR"
            If usrIsRegister08Bit(op1) And (op2 = "(HL)" Or usrIsRegister08Bit(op2)) Then
                size = 1
            ElseIf op2 = "BYTE" Then
                size = 2
            Else
                size = 4
            End If

        Case "CPI"
            size = 2

        Case "ADC", "ADD", "DEC", "INC", "SBC", "SUB", "XOR"
            size = HlpSizeZ80Enhanced(mnem, op1, op2)

        Case "CP"
            If op1 <> "A" And op2 = "" Then
                size = 3
            Else
                size = HlpSizeZ80Enhanced(mnem, op1, op2)
            End If

        Case "JP"
            If op1 = "(HL)" Then
                size = 1
            ElseIf op1 = "(IX)" Or op1 = "(IY)" Then
                size = 2
            Else
                size = 3
            End If

        Case "POP", "PUSH"
            If op1 = "IX" Or op1 = "IY" Then
                size = 2
            Else
                size = 1
            End If

        Case "RLC", "RRC"
            If op1 = "" Then
                size = 1
            Else
                size = 2
            End If

        Case Else
            size = 1

    End Select

    HlpGetInstructionSize = size

End Function
' --- Required Helpers ---
Private Function HlpSizeZ80Enhanced(opcode As String, op1 As String, op2 As String) As Long
    Dim size As Long: size = 0
    Dim ixy As Boolean
    ixy = Left(op1, 2) = "(I" Or Left(op1, 2) = "IX" Or Left(op1, 2) = "IY"
    
    'ADC a, (IX + offset)
    If Left(op2, 2) = "(I" Then
        size = 4 '3 + prefix
        GoTo Finished
    End If
    If Left(op1, 2) = "(I" And (opcode = "DEC" Or opcode = "INC") Then
        size = 4 '3 + prefix
        GoTo Finished
    End If
    If usrIsRegister16Bit(op1) Or usrIsRegister16Bit(op2) Then
        If (opcode = "ADD" Or opcode = "DEC" Or opcode = "INC") And Not ixy Then
            size = 1 'use native 8080
        Else
            size = 2 '1 + prefix
        End If
        GoTo Finished
    End If
    'ADC A, BYTE
    If op2 = "BYTE" Then
        size = 2
    'ADC B
    Else
        size = 1
    End If
Finished:
    HlpSizeZ80Enhanced = size
End Function

Private Function HlpSizeLD(op1 As String, op2 As String) As Long
    Dim op1Offset As Boolean
    Dim op2Offset As Boolean
    Dim op1IsHex As Boolean
    Dim op2IsHex As Boolean
    Dim op1IsRegister08Bit As Boolean
    Dim op2IsRegister08Bit As Boolean
    Dim op1IsRegister16Bit As Boolean
    Dim op2IsRegister16Bit As Boolean
    
    
    op1Offset = InStr(1, op1, "OFFSET", vbTextCompare) Or (Left(op1, 1) = "(" And (InStr(1, op1, "+", vbTextCompare) Or InStr(1, op1, "-", vbTextCompare)))
    op2Offset = InStr(1, op1, "OFFSET", vbTextCompare) Or (Left(op2, 1) = "(" And (InStr(1, op2, "+", vbTextCompare) Or InStr(1, op2, "-", vbTextCompare)))
    op1IsHex = usrValIsHexString(op1)
    op2IsHex = usrValIsHexString(op2)
    op1IsRegister08Bit = usrIsRegister08Bit(op1)
    op2IsRegister08Bit = usrIsRegister08Bit(op2)
    op1IsRegister16Bit = usrIsRegister16Bit(op1)
    op2IsRegister16Bit = usrIsRegister16Bit(op2)
    
    
    ' 16-bit with offset move of byte to IX or IY
    If op1Offset And (op2 = "BYTE" Or op2IsHex And Not op2IsRegister08Bit) Then
        HlpSizeLD = 5 'prefix + opcode + offset + byte
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Indexed addressing: (IX+d), (IY+d)
    If InStr(op1, "(IX") > 0 Or InStr(op1, "(IY") > 0 _
    Or InStr(op2, "(IX") > 0 Or InStr(op2, "(IY") > 0 Then
        HlpSizeLD = 4   ' prefix + opcode + displacement
        Exit Function
    End If

    ' 8-bit register swaps
    If op1IsRegister08Bit And op2IsRegister08Bit Then
        HlpSizeLD = 1
        Exit Function
    End If

    ' 16-bit register swaps
    If op1 = "SP" Then
        'LD SP, HL- equivalent of 8080 SPHL
        If op2 = "HL" Then
            HlpSizeLD = 1
            Exit Function
        End If
        If op2 = "IX" Or op2 = "IY" Then
            HlpSizeLD = 2
            Exit Function
        End If
    End If
    
    ' 16-bit store address to register
    ' LD BC, WORD
    ' LD BC, (WORD)
    If (op1IsRegister16Bit Or op1 = "A") And (op2 = "WORD" Or op2 = "(WORD)" Or op2IsHex) Then
        Select Case op1
            Case "IX", "IY"
                HlpSizeLD = 4 ' prefix + opcode + WORD
            Case "BC", "DE", "SP"
                If op2 = "WORD" Or op2IsHex Then
                    HlpSizeLD = 3 ' Map to 8080 operations
                Else
                    HlpSizeLD = 4 ' prefix + opcode + WORD
                End If
            Case Else
                HlpSizeLD = 3 ' Map to 8080 operations
            End Select
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 16-bit register store to address
    ' LD WORD, BC
    ' LD WORD, A
    If (op1 = "WORD" Or op1IsHex) And (op2 = "A" Or op2IsRegister16Bit) Then
        If op2 = "HL" Then
            HlpSizeLD = 3 ' 8080 SHLD operation equivalent
        ElseIf op2 = "A" Then
            HlpSizeLD = 3 ' 8080 STA operation equivalent
        Else
            HlpSizeLD = 4 ' prefix + opcode + WORD
        End If
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 16-bit store register to address
    ' LD (WORD), BC
    If Len(op1) > 0 Then
        Dim lp As Long, rp As Long
        lp = InStr(1, op1, "(")
        rp = InStr(1, op1, ")")
        If usrValIsHexString(Mid(op1, lp + 1, rp - lp - 1)) Then
            HlpSizeLD = 4 ' prefix + opcode + WORD
            Exit Function
        End If
    End If
        
    
    If op1 = "(WORD)" And op2IsRegister16Bit Then
        HlpSizeLD = 4 ' prefix + opcode + WORD
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    
    ' 16-bit immediate to IX and IY
    If (op1 = "IX" Or op1 = "IY") And (op2 = "WORD" Or op2IsHex) Then
        HlpSizeLD = 4
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 16-bit immediate
    If op1 = "BC" Or op1 = "DE" Or op1 = "HL" _
    Or op1 = "SP" Or op1 = "IX" Or op1 = "IY" Then
        HlpSizeLD = 3
        Exit Function
    End If
    

    ' 16-bit 8080 LDA ADDR equivalent
    If op1 = "A" And (op2 = "WORD" Or op2IsHex) Then
        HlpSizeLD = 3
        Exit Function
    End If

    ' 16 bit Register to Register Pair moves
    ' LD (BC), A
    If Left(op1, 1) = "(" And op2IsRegister08Bit Then
        HlpSizeLD = 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 8-bit register swaps to new Z80 registers I and R
    If op1 = "I" Or op2 = "I" Or op1 = "R" Or op2 = "R" Then
        HlpSizeLD = 2 ' prefix + op
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 8-bit immediate
    If op2 <> "" And Not InStr(op2, "(") > 0 _
       And (op2 = "BYTE" Or op2IsHex) Then
        HlpSizeLD = 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    

    ' Everything else
    HlpSizeLD = 1

End Function
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Hlp6510InstrSize
' Returns byte count for a 6510 instruction based on the addressing mode
' encoded in op1 as typed by the user.
'   #nn        -> 2  (immediate)
'   nn         -> 2  (zero page)
'   nn,X/Y     -> 2  (zero page indexed)
'   nnnn       -> 3  (absolute)
'   nnnn,X/Y   -> 3  (absolute indexed)
'   (nn,X)     -> 2  (indexed indirect)
'   (nn),Y     -> 2  (indirect indexed)
'   (nnnn)     -> 3  (indirect, JMP only)
'   A or ""    -> 1  (accumulator/implied)
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function Hlp6510InstrSize(ByVal op1 As String) As Long
    op1 = Trim$(UCase$(op1))
    
    ' Implied / accumulator
    If op1 = "" Or op1 = "A" Then
        Hlp6510InstrSize = 1
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Immediate
    If Left$(op1, 1) = "#" Then
        Hlp6510InstrSize = 2
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Indirect modes - all 2 bytes except (nnnn) JMP indirect = 3
    If Left$(op1, 1) = "(" Then
        If InStr(op1, ",X)") > 0 Or Right$(op1, 2) = "),Y" Then
            Hlp6510InstrSize = 2  ' (zp,X) or (zp),Y
        Else
            Hlp6510InstrSize = 3  ' (nnnn) absolute indirect
        End If
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Strip index suffix to check base address length
    Dim base As String
    Dim commaPos As Long: commaPos = InStr(op1, ",")
    If commaPos > 0 Then
        base = Left$(op1, commaPos - 1)
    Else
        base = op1
    End If
    
    ' Strip trailing H if present
    If Right$(base, 1) = "H" Then base = Left$(base, Len(base) - 1)
    
    ' Zero page (1-2 hex digits, value <= FF) = 2 bytes
    ' Absolute (3-4 hex digits, value > FF) = 3 bytes
    ' Labels: default to 3 (absolute) — conservative
    If usrValIsHexString(base) Then
        If usrHexToDec(base) <= &HFF& Then
            Hlp6510InstrSize = 2
        Else
            Hlp6510InstrSize = 3
        End If
    Else
        Hlp6510InstrSize = 3  ' unresolved label = assume absolute
    End If
End Function
Public Function usrIsRegister08Bit(ByVal s As String) As Boolean
    Select Case UCase(Trim(s))
        Case "A", "B", "C", "D", "E", "H", "L", "M": usrIsRegister08Bit = True
        Case Else: usrIsRegister08Bit = False
    End Select
End Function
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' usrHexToDec
' Purpose:      Convert hex string to decimal value
' Input:        hexStr - Hex string (may have leading/trailing space, trailing "H")
'               Examples: "FF", "0xFF", " FF ", "FFH"
' Returns:      Long decimal value equivalent to hex input
' Errors:       Returns 0 if input is not valid hex (or uses On Error GoTo)
' Examples:
'   usrHexToDec("FF")       ? 255
'   usrHexToDec("0xFF")     ? 255
'   usrHexToDec(" FF ")     ? 255
'   usrHexToDec("FFH")      ? 255
'   usrHexToDec("1234")     ? 4660
'   usrHexToDec("ABCD")     ? 43981
'
' Note: Consolidates pusrHexToDec() with better error handling
'       and broader input tolerance.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function usrHexToDec(ByVal hexStr As String) As Long
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    ' Step 1: Normalize input
    hexStr = Trim$(hexStr)                      ' Remove leading/trailing spaces
    hexStr = UCase$(hexStr)                     ' Convert to uppercase
    hexStr = Replace(hexStr, "H", "")           ' Remove trailing "H" if present
    
    ' Step 2: Convert hex string to decimal
    ' Val() with "&H" prefix tells VBA to interpret as hex
    usrHexToDec = val("&H" & hexStr)
    
    Exit Function
    
ErrorHandler:
    ' Return 0 on any error (invalid hex, empty string, etc.)
    usrHexToDec = 0
End Function
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' usrHexToAscii
' Returns '.' for non-printables and '?' for invalid hex.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function usrHexToAscii(ByVal hexRange As Variant) As String
    Dim hexVal As String
    Dim decVal As Integer

    If IsEmpty(hexRange) Or hexRange = "" Then
        usrHexToAscii = ""
        Exit Function
    End If

    hexVal = CStr(hexRange)
    On Error Resume Next
    decVal = Application.WorksheetFunction.Hex2Dec(hexVal)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then
        usrHexToAscii = "?"
        Exit Function
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0

    If decVal >= 32 And decVal <= 126 Then
        usrHexToAscii = Chr(decVal)
    Else
        usrHexToAscii = "."
    End If
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' usrAsciiToHex
' Safe Ascii byte to Hex  string -> long (uses &H prefix trick)
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function usrAsciiToHex(ByVal op1 As String) As String
    If op1 = "" Then
        usrAsciiToHex = "00"
        Exit Function
    End If
    Dim dec_char As Long
    dec_char = Asc(Left(op1, 1))
    usrAsciiToHex = usrDecToHexString(dec_char)
End Function

' Compiler Common functions

Public Function cmpResolveValue16(ByVal lbls As clsLabels, ByVal token As String) As Long
    token = UCase$(Trim$(token))
    If token = "" Then cmpResolveValue16 = 0: Exit Function

    Dim rec As clsLabelRecord
    Set rec = lbls.GetLabel(token)
    If Not rec Is Nothing Then
        cmpResolveValue16 = (rec.clsAddress And &HFFFF&)
        Exit Function
    End If

    If usrValIsHexString(token) Then
        cmpResolveValue16 = usrHexToDec(token) And &HFFFF&
    ElseIf IsNumeric(token) Then
        cmpResolveValue16 = CLng(token) And &HFFFF&
    Else
        cmpResolveValue16 = 0
    End If
End Function
Public Sub cmpRaiseAsmError(ByVal wsCPU As Worksheet, ByVal msg As String, ByVal row As Range)
    wsCPU.Range("Error").value = 1
    wsCPU.Range("errMessage").value = "ASM ERROR: " & msg & " @ " & row.address(0, 0)
End Sub
' =============================================================================
' DB string literal only (for now)
' =============================================================================
Public Function cmpStringToBytesVariant(ByVal s As String) As Variant
    Dim out() As Variant, i As Long
    If Len(s) = 0 Then
        cmpStringToBytesVariant = Empty
        Exit Function
    End If
    ReDim out(0 To Len(s))
    For i = 1 To Len(s)
        out(i - 1) = Asc(Mid$(s, i, 1)) And &HFF&
    Next i
    out(Len(s)) = 0
    cmpStringToBytesVariant = out
End Function

'================================================================================
' Sub:          RefreshMemoryTable
' Purpose:      Reads the global gMemory object and writes its contents into
'               the CPU worksheet's memory display table.
'
' Table layout (anchored at named range "MemoryTable"):
'   Col offset  0  = Hex bytes 0-7  (8 cells, one per byte)
'   Col offset -2  = Address (decimal) written into "MemoryTableAddress" column
'   Col offset -1  = ASCII  preview  (8 chars: printable or ".")
'
' Named ranges used:
'   MemoryTable        - top-left byte cell of the 8-column hex byte area
'   MemoryTableAddress - column that holds the row base address (decimal)
'   MemStart           - hex string of first memory address (e.g. "0100")
'   MemEnd             - hex string of last  memory address (e.g. "FFFF")
'                        OR MemSize (number of bytes) is used if MemEnd absent
'
' The ASCII column sits between MemoryTableAddress and MemoryTable byte columns.
' Bytes 0x20-0x7E are displayed as their character; everything else becomes ".".
'
' Call after Assemble8080_ToMachine or after the emulator modifies gMemory so
' the display reflects the live memory state.
'================================================================================
'================================================================================
' Sub:          RefreshMemoryTable
' Purpose:      Reads gMemory and writes the memory display table on the CPU
'               worksheet in a single bulk array assignment for maximum speed.
'
' Strategy:
'   1. Allocate a 2-D Variant array sized (totalRows x totalCols).
'   2. Fill every cell value in VBA memory (no sheet I/O in the loop).
'   3. Write the entire array to the sheet in ONE Range.Value assignment.
'   4. Clear only the exact range that was written (no over-clearing).
'
' Column layout written (left to right):
'   col 1  = Address  (decimal base address for the row)
'   col 2  = ASCII    (8-char preview: printable or ".")
'   col 3..10 = Hex bytes 0-7  (e.g. "3E", "00", "41" ...)
'
' Named ranges consumed:
'   MemoryTableAddress  - address column anchor cell (used for row/col position)
'   MemoryTable         - 8-column hex byte area (must start 2 cols right of above)
'   MemStart            - hex string first address  (e.g. "0100")
'   MemEnd              - hex string last  address  (e.g. "01FF")
'                         Falls back to MemStart + MemSize - 1 if MemEnd absent.
'================================================================================
'================================================================================
' Sub:          RefreshMemoryTable
' Purpose:      Reads gMemory and writes the memory display table on the CPU
'               worksheet using bulk array assignments for maximum speed.
'
' Strategy:
'   - Builds two separate arrays (address col, byte cols) and writes each
'     in a single Range.Value call.  The ASCII column is left completely
'     untouched so any formula there continues to work.
'   - The write range is anchored at the first DATA row of MemoryTable /
'     MemoryTableAddress, so the header row above is never touched.
'
' Named ranges consumed:
'   MemoryTableAddress  - first DATA cell of the address column (row 1 = data)
'   MemoryTable         - first DATA cell of the 8-column hex byte area
'   MemStart            - hex string first address  (e.g. "0100")
'   MemEnd              - hex string last  address  (e.g. "01FF")
'                         Falls back to MemStart + MemSize - 1 if MemEnd absent.
'================================================================================
Public Sub RefreshMemoryTable()

    Const BYTES_PER_ROW As Long = 8

    ' 1. Worksheet & anchors
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU")

    ' These named ranges must point to the FIRST DATA ROW (below any header)
    Dim addrAnchor As Range   ' first data cell of the address column
    Dim memAnchor  As Range   ' first data cell of MemoryTable (byte col 0)
    Set addrAnchor = ws.Range("MemoryTableAddress")
    Set memAnchor = ws.Range("MemoryTable")

    ' 2. Memory window
    Dim memStart As Long
    Dim memEnd   As Long
    memStart = usrHexToDec(CStr(ws.Range("MemStart").value))

    On Error Resume Next
    Dim memEndRng As Range
    Set memEndRng = ws.Range("MemEnd")
    On Error GoTo 0
    If Not memEndRng Is Nothing Then
        memEnd = usrHexToDec(CStr(memEndRng.value))
    Else
        memEnd = memStart + usrHexToDec(CStr(ws.Range("MemSize").value)) - 1
    End If

    ' Cap at the physical table row count
    Dim totalRows As Long
    totalRows = ((memEnd - memStart) \ BYTES_PER_ROW) + 1
    If totalRows > memAnchor.Rows.Count Then totalRows = memAnchor.Rows.Count

    ' 3. Pre-build hex lookup: 0-255 -> "00".."FF"
    Dim hexLookup(0 To 255) As String
    Dim h As Integer
    For h = 0 To 255
        hexLookup(h) = Right$("00" & Hex$(h), 2)
    Next h

    ' 4. Allocate arrays
    Dim addrArr() As Variant
    Dim byteArr() As Variant
    ReDim addrArr(1 To totalRows, 1 To 1)
    ReDim byteArr(1 To totalRows, 1 To BYTES_PER_ROW)

    ' 5. Fill arrays
    '    Cells beyond gMemHighWater are left as "" (blank) so that only
    '    bytes actually emitted by the compiler are displayed — identical
    '    to the 8080 behaviour where trailing zero-memory rows are hidden.
    Dim rowIdx  As Long
    Dim colByte As Long
    Dim rowAddr As Long
    Dim curAddr As Long
    Dim b       As Long

    rowAddr = memStart

    For rowIdx = 1 To totalRows

        ' Address column: blank the row if it starts beyond the high-water mark
        If gMemHighWater > 0 And rowAddr > gMemHighWater Then
            addrArr(rowIdx, 1) = ""
        Else
            addrArr(rowIdx, 1) = rowAddr
        End If

        For colByte = 0 To BYTES_PER_ROW - 1
            curAddr = rowAddr + colByte
            If curAddr > memEnd Then
                byteArr(rowIdx, colByte + 1) = ""
            ElseIf gMemHighWater > 0 And curAddr > gMemHighWater Then
                byteArr(rowIdx, colByte + 1) = ""   ' beyond last compiled byte
            Else
                b = CLng(gMemory.addr(curAddr)) And &HFF&
                byteArr(rowIdx, colByte + 1) = hexLookup(b)
            End If
        Next colByte

        rowAddr = rowAddr + BYTES_PER_ROW
    Next rowIdx

    ' 6. Two bulk writes — address col, then byte cols
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False

    addrAnchor.Resize(totalRows, 1).value = addrArr
    memAnchor.Resize(totalRows, BYTES_PER_ROW).value = byteArr

    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

End Sub

'================================================================================
' Module:       modGlobals
'================================================================================


''' Component: clsDecRegisterState
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsDecRegisterState
' Purpose:      Lightweight record for decimal based stack entries:
'               - MemoryAddress: long
'               - Value:        dec as pushed
'               - RegisterName: label for provenance (e.g., "CALL X", "B", "Flags")
'
' Notes:        No logic; public fields used by clsStack and clsCPU.
' Source:       Stable snapshot (2026-02-12 18:38)
'================================================================================

Public MemoryAddress As Long
Public value As Long
Public RegisterName As String

'================================================================================
' Class:        clsDecRegisterState
'================================================================================



''' Component: clsDecStack
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsDecStack
' Purpose:      Simple LIFO stack of clsRegisterState items for the emulator.
'               - PUSH/POP/PEEK operations over an internal dynamic array
'               - ShowStack renders the visible stack view on the CPU sheet
'
'================================================================================

Private m_Items() As clsDecRegisterState
Private m_Count As Long

Private Sub Class_Initialize()
    m_Count = 0
    ReDim m_Items(0)
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' ShowStack
' Renders the current stack (top at row 1) into named ranges on the CPU sheet.
' Skips redraw during headless runs unless force=True.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function ShowStack(Optional ByVal refresh As Boolean = False) As Boolean
    If Not refresh Then
        ShowStack = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    Dim i As Long, detail As Long
    Range("StackDetails").ClearContents

    If m_Count > 0 Then
        For i = 1 To m_Count
            detail = m_Count - i + 1
            Range("stackView").offset(i - 1, 1).value = usrDecToHexString(m_Items(detail).MemoryAddress)
            Range("stackView").offset(i - 1, 2).value = Right$("00" & usrDecToHexString(m_Items(detail).value), 2) & "H"
            Range("stackView").offset(i - 1, 3).value = m_Items(detail).RegisterName
        Next
    End If
    ShowStack = True
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' clsPUSH
' Pushes a new item with (address, value, register name) onto the stack.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Sub clsPUSH(ByVal addr As Long, ByVal val As Long, ByVal Reg As String)
    Dim newItem As clsDecRegisterState
    Set newItem = New clsDecRegisterState
    Dim memory As clsMemory
    
    Set memory = gMemory
    memory.addr(addr) = val
    
    newItem.MemoryAddress = addr
    newItem.value = val
    newItem.RegisterName = Reg
    
    m_Count = m_Count + 1
    If m_Count = 1 Then
        ReDim m_Items(1 To 1)
    Else
        ReDim Preserve m_Items(1 To m_Count)
    End If

    Set m_Items(m_Count) = newItem
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' clsPOP
' Pops the top item. Raises a descriptive error if underflow occurs.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function clsPOP() As clsDecRegisterState
    If m_Count > 0 Then
        Set clsPOP = m_Items(m_Count)
        m_Count = m_Count - 1
        If m_Count > 0 Then
            ReDim Preserve m_Items(1 To m_Count)
        Else
            ReDim m_Items(0)
        End If
    Else
        Err.Raise vbObjectError + 513, "clsStack", "Stack Underflow: No items to pop."
    End If
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' clsPeek
' Returns the top item without removing it. Nothing if empty.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function clsPeek() As clsDecRegisterState
    If m_Count > 0 Then
        Set clsPeek = m_Items(m_Count)
    Else
        Set clsPeek = Nothing
    End If
End Function

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Count
' Returns the number of items on the stack.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Property Get Count() As Long
    Count = m_Count
End Property

'================================================================================
' Class:        clsDecStack
'================================================================================



''' Component: decExecute8080
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Module:       decAssemble
' Purpose:      Execution harness for the Excel/VBA Intel 8080 emulator.
'               - Initializes/rehydrates CPU and memory
'               - Selection-free, headless-aware main loop
'               - Routes opcodes to clsCPU
'               - Console helpers (modeless output form)
'
' Notes:        This is documentation/reformat only. No functional changes.
' Source:       Stable snapshot (2026-02-12 18:38)  ? Export reference.
'================================================================================
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Execute
' Entry point for a run. Honours "reset" and "Step" (headless) flags on the CPU
' sheet. Bulk-reads instruction columns to arrays for performance. Routes each
' opcode to RunOpcode (which dispatches into clsCPU).
'
' Sheet bindings (named ranges expected on "CPU"):
'   Start_pc_dec, pc_dec, reset, Error, errMessage
'   MemStart, MemSize, MemEnd
'   ofs_opcode, ofs_op1, ofs_op2, ofs_rowstat, ofs_label
'   Line0_dec (decimal first row of memory/instruction grid), StackStart, StackDetails,
'   consoleOut, Step
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Sub Execute8080()
    Dim pc_dec As Long
    Dim opcode As String
    Dim op1 As String, op2 As String, label As String
    Dim ofs_opcode As Long, ofs_op1 As Long, ofs_op2 As Long, ofs_rowstat As Long, ofs_label As Long
    Dim reset As Long, errcode As Long
    Dim rowStat As String
    Dim memStart As Long, memEnd As Long
    Dim myCpu As clsDecCPU
    Dim headless As Boolean
    Dim prevCalc As XlCalculation
    Dim debugMode As Boolean
    Dim stepMode As Boolean
    Dim stepTaken As Boolean
    Dim executedThisIter As Boolean
    Dim endedByEnd As Boolean
    Dim skipBreaks As Boolean
    Dim traceReads As Boolean
    Dim maxIters As Long
    Dim stopRunning As Boolean

    ' --- Cached arrays mapped into locals for the run ---
    Dim base As Range, line0_dec As Long
    Dim countRows As Long
    Dim arrOpcode As Variant, arrRowStat As Variant, arrOp1 As Variant, arrOp2 As Variant, arrLabel As Variant
    Dim ubRows_Opcode As Long

    Dim rowIdx As Long

    Dim memAddrDec As Long
    Dim memBefore As String, memAfter As String, memAddrHex As String, memNote As String
    Dim memTrackLen As Long
    Dim preHL As Long, preSP As Long
    Dim b0 As Long, b1 As Long, a0 As Long, a1 As Long
    ' ========= Initialization =========
    InitHexTable

    ofs_opcode = Range("ofs_opcode").value
    ofs_op1 = Range("ofs_op1").value
    ofs_op2 = Range("ofs_op2").value
    ofs_rowstat = Range("ofs_rowstat").value
    ofs_label = Range("ofs_label").value

    debugMode = (Range("Debug").value = 1)
    stepMode = (Range("Step").value = 1)
    reset = Range("Reset").value
    skipBreaks = Range("SkipBreaks") = 1
    traceReads = TraceMemReads()
    maxIters = Range("Max_Iters").value
    Range("Stop").value = 0
    
    Dim atEnd As Boolean: atEnd = CLng(Range("AtEnd").value) = 1
    'if at end of program auto reset
    If atEnd Then
        reset = 1
        Range("AtEnd").value = 0
    End If

    errcode = 0
    endedByEnd = False
    stepTaken = False

    ' Clear sheet error/message each call (keeps step UI clean)
    Range("Error").value = 0
    Range("errMessage").value = ""

    ' check first and only first line for an org opcode to set global memory location
    If Range("Line0").offset(0, ofs_opcode) = "ORG" And reset = 1 Then
        op1 = Range("Line0").offset(0, ofs_op1).value
        If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
            Range("MemStart").value = op1
            Application.Calculate
        End If
    End If
    
    memStart = usrHexToDec(Range("MemStart").value)
    memEnd = memStart + usrHexToDec(Range("MemSize").value)

    Set myCpu = gDecCPU                                         ' persistent CPU instance

    ' ========= Reset / continuation =========
    If reset = 1 Then
        ' Fresh run / Step Start: reset CPU and rebuild cache
        If TraceEnabled() Then TraceClear
        ForceCompile (False)
        ResetAddressList
        ResetDecCPU
        Set myCpu = gDecCPU
        InvalidateExecCache
        gBreak = False
        gCurrentIter = 0

        mConsoleOpen = False
        pc_dec = CLng(Range("Line0_dec").value)
        myCpu.SetPC pc_dec
        myCpu.SetReg "SP", memEnd

        Range("StackStart").value = usrDecToHexString(myCpu.Reg("SP"))
        Range("StackDetails").ClearContents
        If stepMode Then
            RefreshFlags myCpu
            RefreshRegisters myCpu
            myCpu.RefreshStack True
            Application.Calculate
        End If
    Else
        ' Continue run / Step: pull PC from persistent CPU object
        pc_dec = CLng(myCpu.Reg("PC"))
    End If
    
    ' ========= Headless toggle =========
    headless = Not stepMode                                      ' stepMode implies interactive paints
    If headless Then
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        prevCalc = Application.Calculation
        Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
    End If

    ' ========= Build/refresh cached arrays ONLY when needed =========
    Set base = Range("Line0_dec")
    line0_dec = CLng(base.value)

    countRows = (memEnd - memStart) + 1
    If countRows < 1 Then countRows = 1

    ' Rebuild cache only when Reset=1 or cache invalid or layout changed
    If (Not gCacheValid) _
       Or (gCacheCountRows <> countRows) _
       Or (gCacheLine0Dec <> line0_dec) _
       Or (gCacheMemStart <> memStart) _
       Or (gCacheMemEnd <> memEnd) _
       Or (gCacheOfsOpcode <> ofs_opcode) _
       Or (gCacheOfsOp1 <> ofs_op1) _
       Or (gCacheOfsOp2 <> ofs_op2) _
       Or (gCacheOfsRowStat <> ofs_rowstat) _
       Or (gCacheOfsLabel <> ofs_label) Then

        gCacheLine0Dec = line0_dec
        gCacheCountRows = countRows
        gCacheMemStart = memStart
        gCacheMemEnd = memEnd
        gCacheOfsOpcode = ofs_opcode
        gCacheOfsOp1 = ofs_op1
        gCacheOfsOp2 = ofs_op2
        gCacheOfsRowStat = ofs_rowstat
        gCacheOfsLabel = ofs_label

        gArrOpcode = base.offset(0, ofs_opcode).Resize(countRows, 1).value
        gArrRowStat = base.offset(0, ofs_rowstat).Resize(countRows, 1).value
        gArrOp1 = base.offset(0, ofs_op1).Resize(countRows, 1).value
        gArrOp2 = base.offset(0, ofs_op2).Resize(countRows, 1).value
        gArrLabel = base.offset(0, ofs_label).Resize(countRows, 1).value

        ' Normalize once (same intent as your existing loop)
        Dim idxN As Long
        For idxN = 1 To countRows
            If Not IsEmpty(gArrOpcode(idxN, 1)) Then gArrOpcode(idxN, 1) = Trim$(UCase$(CStr(gArrOpcode(idxN, 1))))
            If Not IsEmpty(gArrRowStat(idxN, 1)) Then gArrRowStat(idxN, 1) = Trim$(UCase$(CStr(gArrRowStat(idxN, 1))))
            If Not IsEmpty(gArrOp1(idxN, 1)) Then gArrOp1(idxN, 1) = Trim$(UCase$(CStr(gArrOp1(idxN, 1))))
            If Not IsEmpty(gArrOp2(idxN, 1)) Then gArrOp2(idxN, 1) = Trim$(CStr(gArrOp2(idxN, 1))) ' preserve string case for literals
            If Not IsEmpty(gArrLabel(idxN, 1)) Then gArrLabel(idxN, 1) = Trim$(UCase$(CStr(gArrLabel(idxN, 1))))
        Next idxN

        gCacheValid = True
    End If

    ' Use cached arrays for execution
    arrOpcode = gArrOpcode
    arrRowStat = gArrRowStat
    arrOp1 = gArrOp1
    arrOp2 = gArrOp2
    arrLabel = gArrLabel

    ubRows_Opcode = UBound(arrOpcode, 1)

    ' ========= Establish starting row index =========
    rowIdx = myCpu.GetCurrentIdx

    If rowIdx < 0 Or rowIdx >= ubRows_Opcode Then
        GoTo ExecFinalize
    End If

    opcode = CStr(arrOpcode(rowIdx + 1, 1))

    ' ========= Main loop =========
    Do While errcode = 0 And pc_dec <= memEnd And (Not stepMode Or (stepMode And Not stepTaken))

        gCurrentIter = gCurrentIter + 1
        
        op1 = CStr(arrOp1(rowIdx + 1, 1))
        op2 = CStr(arrOp2(rowIdx + 1, 1))
        label = CStr(arrLabel(rowIdx + 1, 1))

        ' keep op2 uppercase for most uses except EQU literal semantics
        If UCase$(op2) <> "EQU" Then op2 = UCase$(op2)

        rowStat = CStr(arrRowStat(rowIdx + 1, 1))
        ' Check for code breaks; override in testrunner to have no breaks
        If rowStat = "B" And Not stepMode And Not skipBreaks Then
            If gBreak Then
                gBreak = False
            Else
                gBreak = True
                Exit Do
            End If
        End If

        executedThisIter = False

        ' Execute only if not compiled and opcode exists
        If rowStat <> "C" And opcode <> "" Then

            ' --- Trace memory sampling (before) ---
            memAddrHex = "": memBefore = "": memAfter = "": memNote = ""
            memTrackLen = 0
            memAddrDec = 0
            
            If TraceEnabled() Then
                ' Snapshot pre-state for address calculations
                preHL = ((myCpu.Reg("H") And 255) * 256&) + (myCpu.Reg("L") And 255)
                preSP = (myCpu.Reg("SP") And &HFFFF&)
            
                Select Case opcode
            
                    ' ===== M-operand writes (HL indirect) =====
                    Case "MOV"
                        If UCase$(op1) = "M" Then
                            memAddrDec = preHL
                            memTrackLen = 1
                        End If
            
                    Case "MVI", "INR", "DCR"
                        If UCase$(op1) = "M" Then
                            memAddrDec = preHL
                            memTrackLen = 1
                        End If
            
                    ' ===== Direct memory writes =====
                    Case "STA"
                        If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
                            memAddrDec = usrHexToDec(op1) And &HFFFF&
                            memTrackLen = 1
                        Else
                            memNote = "STA addr token=" & op1
                        End If
            
                    Case "SHLD"
                        If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
                            memAddrDec = usrHexToDec(op1) And &HFFFF&
                            memTrackLen = 2
                        Else
                            memNote = "SHLD addr token=" & op1
                        End If
            
                    ' ===== Stack writes =====
                    Case "PUSH"
                        memAddrDec = (preSP - 2) And &HFFFF&
                        memTrackLen = 2
                        memNote = "PUSH writes SP-2..SP-1"
            
                    Case "CALL", "CC", "CNC", "CNZ", "CZ", "CP", "CM", "CPE", "CPO"
                        ' Conditional calls only write if taken; we’ll detect by before/after diff
                        memAddrDec = (preSP - 2) And &HFFFF&
                        memTrackLen = 2
                        memNote = "CALL writes SP-2..SP-1 (if taken)"
            
                    ' ===== XTHL swaps stack top =====
                    Case "XTHL"
                        memAddrDec = preSP
                        memTrackLen = 2
                        memNote = "XTHL swaps (SP),(SP+1)"
            
                End Select
                
                ' ===== Memory reads (optional) =====
                If memTrackLen = 0 And traceReads Then
                
                    Select Case opcode
