                        ' MOV r, M  (read from (HL))
                        Case "MOV"
                            If UCase$(op2) = "M" Then
                                memAddrDec = preHL
                                memTrackLen = 1
                                memNote = "READ (HL)"
                            End If
                
                        ' ALU/LOGIC using M (read from (HL))
                        Case "ADD", "ADC", "SUB", "SBB", "ANA", "XRA", "ORA", "CMP"
                            If UCase$(op1) = "M" Then
                                memAddrDec = preHL
                                memTrackLen = 1
                                memNote = "READ (HL)"
                            End If
                
                        ' Direct reads
                        Case "LDA"
                            If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
                                memAddrDec = usrHexToDec(op1) And &HFFFF&
                                memTrackLen = 1
                                memNote = "READ (addr)"
                            Else
                                memNote = "READ LDA addr token=" & op1
                            End If
                
                        Case "LHLD"
                            If usrValIsHexString(op1) Then
                                memAddrDec = usrHexToDec(op1) And &HFFFF&
                                memTrackLen = 2
                                memNote = "READ16 (addr)"
                            Else
                                memNote = "READ LHLD addr token=" & op1
                            End If
                
                        ' Indirect reads via BC/DE
                        Case "LDAX"
                            If UCase$(op1) = "B" Then
                                memAddrDec = ((myCpu.Reg("B") And 255) * 256&) + (myCpu.Reg("C") And 255)
                                memTrackLen = 1
                                memNote = "READ (BC)"
                            ElseIf UCase$(op1) = "D" Then
                                memAddrDec = ((myCpu.Reg("D") And 255) * 256&) + (myCpu.Reg("E") And 255)
                                memTrackLen = 1
                                memNote = "READ (DE)"
                            End If
                
                        ' Stack reads
                        Case "POP"
                            memAddrDec = preSP
                            memTrackLen = 2
                            memNote = "READ16 (SP) POP"
                
                        Case "RET", "RNZ", "RZ", "RC", "RNC", "RP", "RM", "RPE", "RPO"
                            memAddrDec = preSP
                            memTrackLen = 2
                            memNote = "READ16 (SP) RET* (if taken)"
                    End Select
                
                End If
            
                ' Read BEFORE bytes if we have an address
                If memTrackLen = 1 Then
                    b0 = gMemory.addr(memAddrDec) And 255
                    memBefore = Right$("00" & Hex$(b0), 2)
                    memAddrHex = Right$("0000" & Hex$(memAddrDec), 4)
                ElseIf memTrackLen = 2 Then
                    b0 = gMemory.addr(memAddrDec) And 255
                    b1 = gMemory.addr((memAddrDec + 1) And &HFFFF&) And 255
                    memBefore = Right$("00" & Hex$(b0), 2) & " " & Right$("00" & Hex$(b1), 2)
                    memAddrHex = Right$("0000" & Hex$(memAddrDec), 4)
                End If
            End If
            
            If debugMode Then
                RefreshFlags myCpu
                RefreshRegisters myCpu
                myCpu.RefreshStack True
                Application.Calculate
                Debug.Assert Not debugMode
            End If

            errcode = myCpu.RunOpcode(opcode, op1, op2, label)
            executedThisIter = True
            
            If TraceEnabled() Then
                ' Read AFTER bytes for tracked address and include only if changed
                Dim isRead As Boolean
                If memTrackLen = 1 Then
                    a0 = gMemory.addr(memAddrDec) And 255
                    memAfter = Right$("00" & Hex$(a0), 2)
            
                    isRead = (Left$(memNote, 4) = "READ")
                    
                    If isRead Then
                        ' Reads don't change memory; keep the read value visible.
                        memAfter = ""
                    Else
                        ' Writes: hide if no change
                        If memBefore = memAfter Then
                            memAddrHex = "": memBefore = "": memAfter = "": memNote = ""
                        End If
                    End If
                ElseIf memTrackLen = 2 Then
                    a0 = gMemory.addr(memAddrDec) And 255
                    a1 = gMemory.addr((memAddrDec + 1) And &HFFFF&) And 255
                    memAfter = Right$("00" & Hex$(a0), 2) & " " & Right$("00" & Hex$(a1), 2)
            
                    isRead = (Left$(memNote, 4) = "READ")
                    
                    If isRead Then
                        ' Reads don't change memory; keep the read value visible.
                        memAfter = ""
                    Else
                        ' Writes: hide if no change
                        If memBefore = memAfter Then
                            memAddrHex = "": memBefore = "": memAfter = "": memNote = ""
                        End If
                    End If
                End If
            
                ' Append trace row (post-state + optional memory delta)
                TraceAppend myCpu, pc_dec, opcode, op1, op2, errcode, memAddrHex, memBefore, memAfter, memNote
            
                If stepMode And TraceLive() Then TraceFlush
            End If

            If errcode = ERR_EXEC_END Then
                endedByEnd = True
                Exit Do
            End If

            If errcode = ERR_BAD_OPCODE Then
                Range("Error").value = errcode
                Range("errMessage").value = "Error: Invalid OpCode: " & opcode & " at Line " & pc_dec
                Exit Do
            End If
            
            If gCurrentIter >= maxIters Then
                errcode = ERR_MAX_ITERS
                Range("Error").value = errcode
                Range("errMessage").value = "Error: Max Iterations Limit: " & gCurrentIter & " at Line " & pc_dec
                Exit Do
            End If

        End If

        ' Advance PC only after processing this row (consistent with your existing design)
        If errcode = 0 Then
            pc_dec = myCpu.IncPC()
        End If

        ' Update row index for next fetch
        rowIdx = myCpu.GetCurrentIdx
        If rowIdx < 0 Or rowIdx >= ubRows_Opcode Then Exit Do

        opcode = CStr(arrOpcode(rowIdx + 1, 1))

        ' In step mode, only count the step if an instruction executed
        If stepMode And executedThisIter Then
            stepTaken = True
        End If

        ' Paint UI in step mode
        If stepMode And errcode = 0 Then
            'advance to next non-blank row
            Do While opcode = "" And pc_dec <= memEnd
                pc_dec = myCpu.IncPC()
                rowIdx = pc_dec - line0_dec
                opcode = CStr(arrOpcode(rowIdx + 1, 1))
            Loop
            
            If myCpu.RegistersDirty Then
                RefreshRegisters myCpu
                myCpu.RegistersDirty = False
            End If
            If myCpu.FlagsDirty Then
                RefreshFlags myCpu
                myCpu.FlagsDirty = False
            End If
            If myCpu.StackDirty Then
                myCpu.RefreshStack True
                myCpu.StackDirty = False
            End If
        End If
        
        If Range("Stop").value = 1 Then
            errcode = ERR_STOP
            Range("Error").value = errcode
            Range("errMessage").value = "Error: Execution Stopped. Iteration: " & gCurrentIter & " at Line " & pc_dec
            Exit Do
        End If
    Loop

ExecFinalize:
    ' ========= Finalization =========
    If headless Or stepMode Or gBreak Then
        Application.Calculation = prevCalc
        Application.EnableEvents = True
        Application.ScreenUpdating = True

        If Not stepMode Then
            RefreshRegisters myCpu
            RefreshFlags myCpu
            myCpu.RefreshStack True
        Else
            Range("PC").value = usrDecToHexString(myCpu.Reg("PC"))
        End If

        Application.StatusBar = False
        Range("consoleText") = usrForm.tbConsole.value
    End If

    If TraceEnabled() Then TraceFlush
    
    ' Show "Execution Complete" ONLY when END was encountered
    If gBreak Then
        Range("errMessage") = "Break at Line " & pc_dec
        Range("Reset").value = 0
    ElseIf endedByEnd Then
        Range("AtEnd").value = 1
        Range("errMessage") = "Execution Complete"
    End If
End Sub

' UI updates
Public Function RefreshRegisters(ByRef myCpu As clsDecCPU) As Integer
    Dim key As Variant
    Dim rangeName As String
    For Each key In myCpu.Registers
        If InStr("ABCDEFHLApBpCpDpEpFpHpLpIXIYR", key) Then
            rangeName = "R_"
        Else
            rangeName = ""
        End If
        rangeName = rangeName & CStr(key)
        Range(rangeName).value = usrDecToHexString(myCpu.Reg(key))
    Next
    myCpu.RegistersDirty = False
End Function
Public Function RefreshFlags(ByRef myCpu As clsDecCPU) As Integer
    Dim key As Variant
    Dim rangeName As String
    For Each key In myCpu.Flags
        Range(CStr(key)).value = myCpu.Flag(key)
    Next
    myCpu.FlagsDirty = False
End Function


'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' ReSetRegisters
' Clears sheet register display cells (not CPU object) for A..L, PC, SP view.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Sub ReSetRegisters()
    Dim i As Integer
    For i = 0 To 8
        Range("Registers").offset(i, 2).value = 0
    Next i
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' Button Macros
' '------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Public Sub BTN_Run()
    With Sheets("CPU")
        .Range("Step").value = 0
    End With
    SelectEngine
End Sub

Public Sub BTN_Restart()
    Application.Calculation = xlAutomatic
    
    With Sheets("CPU")
        .Range("Step").value = 1
        .Range("Reset").value = 1
        .Range("PC").value = Range("MemStart").value
    End With
End Sub

Public Sub BTN_Step()
    With Sheets("CPU")
        .Range("Step").value = 1
        SelectEngine
        .Range("Reset").value = 0
    End With
End Sub
Public Sub ForceCompile(Optional ByVal compile As Boolean = False)
    Dim base As Range
    Dim ofs_opcode As Long
    Dim memSize As Long
    Dim arrOpcode As Variant
    Dim EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT As Long: EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT = 8
    Dim emptyRuns As Long
    Dim opcode As String
    
    If compile Then
        AssembleForCPUMode
        Exit Sub
    End If
    ofs_opcode = Range("ofs_opcode").value
    Set base = Range("Line0").offset(0, ofs_opcode)
    memSize = usrHexToDec(Range("MemSize").value)
    arrOpcode = base.Resize(memSize, 1).value
    
    Dim i As Long
    i = 1
    emptyRuns = 0
    Do While i <= memSize And Not compile And (emptyRuns < EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT)
        opcode = arrOpcode(i, 1)
        'If opcode = "DB" Or opcode = "DS" Then
        If opcode = "DB" Then
            compile = True
        End If
        If opcode = "" Then
            emptyRuns = emptyRuns + 1
        Else
            emptyRuns = 0
        End If
        i = i + 1
    Loop
    If compile Then
        AssembleForCPUMode
    End If
End Sub
'================================================================================
' Module:       decAssemble
'================================================================================







''' Component: Sheet3
''' [No code]

''' Component: Compiler8080
Option Explicit

' --- Compile gating / caching ---
Private gCompileEnabled As Boolean
Private gCompiledValid As Boolean
Private gCompiledForResetStamp As Double   ' optional: timestamp of last reset compile
Private gLastCodeSignature As String       ' optional: detect edits without reset
' MemoryTable is 8 bytes wide: AB..AI
Private Const BYTES_PER_MEMROW As Long = 8
Private Const EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT As Long = 8
Private gMemTableCol As Long
Private pLabels As New clsLabels
' =============================================================================
' Assemble8080_ToMachine
' Compiles CPU listing into 8080 machine bytes and writes to:
'   - Column Z: base address for each 8-byte row
'   - MemoryTable (AB..AI): hex bytes
' Optionally writes "AA BB CC" into the listing Mem column and marks RowStat="C".
' =============================================================================
Public Sub Assemble8080_ToMachine()

    Dim wsCPU As Worksheet, wsOp As Worksheet
    Set wsCPU = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU")
    Set wsOp = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("8080 Op to Hex") ' opcode mapping table
    Dim myMemory As clsMemory
    Dim lbl As clsLabelRecord
    
    usrMemReset
    ResetAddressList
    Set myMemory = gMemory
    ' Offsets into the CPU program grid (named ranges)
    Dim ofsLabel As Long, ofsOpcode As Long, ofsOp1 As Long, ofsOp2 As Long

    ofsLabel = CLng(wsCPU.Range("ofs_label").value)
    ofsOpcode = CLng(wsCPU.Range("ofs_opcode").value)
    ofsOp1 = CLng(wsCPU.Range("ofs_op1").value)
    ofsOp2 = CLng(wsCPU.Range("ofs_op2").value)
    gMemTableCol = CLng(wsCPU.Range("MemoryTableAddress").Column)
    

    ' Memory window
    Dim memStartDec As Long, memSize As Long
    memStartDec = usrHexToDec(CStr(wsCPU.Range("MemStart").value))
    memSize = usrHexToDec(CStr(wsCPU.Range("MemSize").value))

    ' Build opcode lookup dictionary from "8080 Op to Hex"
    Dim opMap As Object
    Set opMap = BuildOpcodeMap(wsOp)

    ' Labels/EQU/DB metadata (your existing class)
    Dim lbls As clsLabels
    Set lbls = New clsLabels

    ' MemoryTable byte cells (AB..AI) named range
    Dim rngMem As Range
    Set rngMem = wsCPU.Range("MemoryTable")

    Application.Calculate
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False

    ' Clear prior compiled bytes (only AB..AI)
    rngMem.ClearContents

    ' Also clear address column Z for the memory rows we might touch (overwrite is OK per you)
    wsCPU.Range(wsCPU.Cells(rngMem.row, gMemTableCol), _
                wsCPU.Cells(rngMem.row + rngMem.Rows.Count - 1, gMemTableCol)).ClearContents

    Dim base As Range
    Set base = wsCPU.Range("Line0") ' start of listing grid

    Dim pc As Long
    pc = memStartDec

    Dim r As Long, emptyRun As Long
    emptyRun = 0

    ' Walk listing rows (cap at memSize rows for safety)
    For r = 0 To memSize

        Dim cur As Range
        Set cur = base.offset(r, 0)

        Dim labelName As String, opcode As String, op1 As String, op2 As String
        labelName = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsLabel).value)))
        opcode = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsOpcode).value)))
        op1 = StripComment(Trim$(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsOp1).value)))
        op2 = StripComment(Trim$(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsOp2).value)))

        ' stop condition: consecutive empty program rows
        If (labelName = ";") Then
            GoTo NextRow
        End If
        
        If (labelName = "") And (opcode = "") And (op1 = "") And (op2 = "") Then
            emptyRun = emptyRun + 1
            If emptyRun >= EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT Then Exit For
            GoTo NextRow
        Else
            emptyRun = 0
        End If

        Set lbl = pLabels.GetLabel(op1)
        If Not lbl Is Nothing Then
            op1 = lbl.clsAddressHex ' use the label's hex value/address
        End If

        Dim bytesOut As Variant
        bytesOut = Empty

        Select Case opcode
            Case ""
                GoTo NextRow

            Case "ORG"
                If op1 = "" Then
                    cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, "ORG missing operand", cur
                    Exit Sub
                End If
                pc = cmpResolveValue16(lbls, UCase$(op1))
                GoTo NextRow

            Case "EQU"
                ' In your model, EQU constants are captured during label parsing already.
                GoTo NextRow

            Case "DB"
                ' String literal only for now (raw OP1)
                If Len(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsOp1).value)) = 0 Then
                    cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, "DB missing string", cur
                    Exit Sub
                End If
                bytesOut = cmpStringToBytesVariant(CStr(cur.offset(0, ofsOp1).value))

            Case "DS"
                Dim ds As Long
                Dim i As Long
                If Not usrValIsHexString(cur.offset(0, ofsOp1).value) Then
                     cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, "DS Invalid DS Length", cur
                    Exit Sub
                End If
                ds = usrHexToDec(cur.offset(0, ofsOp1).value)
                Dim out() As Variant
                ReDim out(0 To ds - 1)
                For i = 1 To ds
                    out(i - 1) = 255
                Next i
                bytesOut = out
                    
            Case Else
                ' Normal instruction: lookup + encode (1/2/3 bytes)
                Dim info As Variant
                info = HlpFindOpcode(opMap, opcode, UCase$(op1), UCase$(op2))
                If IsEmpty(info) Then
                    cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, "Unknown instruction form: " & opcode & " " & op1 & " " & op2, cur
                    Exit Sub
                End If

                bytesOut = HlpEncodeInstruction(lbls, CByte(info(0)), CLng(info(1)), _
                                             CStr(info(2)), CStr(info(3)), _
                                             UCase$(op1), UCase$(op2), opcode, cur, wsCPU)
        End Select

        ' Emit compiled bytes to MemoryTable using PC-based mapping (Z + AB..AI)
        If Not IsEmpty(bytesOut) Then
            EmitBytesToMemoryTable wsCPU, rngMem, memStartDec, pc, bytesOut, myMemory


            pc = pc + (UBound(bytesOut) - LBound(bytesOut) + 1)
        End If


NextRow:
    Next r
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True

    wsCPU.Range("errMessage").value = "Assemble complete"

End Sub

' =============================================================================
' Memory emit: PC -> row/col within AB..AI and base address into column Z
' =============================================================================
Public Sub EmitBytesToMemoryTable(ByVal wsCPU As Worksheet, _
 ByVal rngMem As Range, _
 ByVal memStartDec As Long, _
 ByVal startAddrDec As Long, _
 ByVal bytesOut As Variant, _
 ByRef myMem As clsMemory, _
 Optional ByVal addrCol As Long = 0)

    Dim i As Long
    Dim baseAddr As Long
    Dim lastTargetRow As Long

    lastTargetRow = 0
    baseAddr = memStartDec

    For i = LBound(bytesOut) To UBound(bytesOut)

        Dim addr As Long
        addr = startAddrDec + (i - LBound(bytesOut))

        Dim offset As Long
        offset = addr - memStartDec
        If offset < 0 Then Exit Sub

        Dim rowIndex As Long, colIndex As Long
        rowIndex = offset \ BYTES_PER_MEMROW
        colIndex = offset Mod BYTES_PER_MEMROW

        Dim targetRow As Long, targetCol As Long
        targetRow = 1 + rowIndex
        targetCol = 1 + colIndex

        If targetRow > rngMem.Rows.Count Then Exit Sub
        If targetCol > rngMem.Columns.Count Then Exit Sub

        rngMem.Cells(targetRow, targetCol).value = Right$("00" & Hex$(CLng(bytesOut(i)) And &HFF&), 2)
        myMem.addr(addr) = CLng(bytesOut(i)) And &HFF&

        ' Track the highest address written so RefreshMemoryTable can blank the rest
        If addr > gMemHighWater Then gMemHighWater = addr

        baseAddr = memStartDec + (rowIndex * BYTES_PER_MEMROW)
        lastTargetRow = targetRow
    Next i

    If lastTargetRow > 0 Then
        Dim col As Long: col = IIf(addrCol > 0, addrCol, gMemTableCol)
        wsCPU.Cells(rngMem.row + (lastTargetRow - 1), col).value = baseAddr
    End If

End Sub
' =============================================================================
' Opcode map from "8080 Op to Hex" table: key = MNEMONIC|OP1SPEC|OP2SPEC
' =============================================================================
Public Function BuildOpcodeMap(ByVal wsOp As Worksheet) As Object
    Dim dict As Object: Set dict = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    dict.CompareMode = vbTextCompare

    Dim lastRow As Long
    lastRow = wsOp.Cells(wsOp.Rows.Count, 1).End(xlUp).row

    Dim r As Long, emptyRun As Long
    emptyRun = 0

    ' Columns in your sheet:
    ' A Opcode, B Hex, D OP1, E OP2, F Bytes
    For r = 2 To lastRow
        Dim mnem As String
        mnem = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(wsOp.Cells(r, 1).value)))
        If mnem = "" Then
            emptyRun = emptyRun + 1
            If emptyRun >= 10 Then Exit For
            GoTo ContinueRow
        Else
            emptyRun = 0
        End If

        Dim hexTxt As String: hexTxt = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(wsOp.Cells(r, 2).value)))
        Dim spec1 As String: spec1 = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(wsOp.Cells(r, 4).value)))
        Dim spec2 As String: spec2 = UCase$(Trim$(CStr(wsOp.Cells(r, 5).value)))
        Dim bytes As Long: bytes = CLng(wsOp.Cells(r, 6).value)

        If hexTxt = "" Or bytes < 1 Then GoTo ContinueRow

        Dim opByte As Long
        opByte = usrHexToDec(hexTxt) And &HFF&

        Dim key As String
        key = mnem & "|" & spec1 & "|" & spec2

        If Not dict.Exists(key) Then
            dict.ADD key, Array(opByte, bytes, spec1, spec2)
        End If

ContinueRow:
    Next r

    Set BuildOpcodeMap = dict
End Function

Private Function HlpFindOpcode(ByVal opMap As Object, ByVal mnem As String, ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As Variant
    Dim key As String

    key = mnem & "|" & op1 & "|" & op2
    If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function

    key = mnem & "|" & op1 & "|"
    If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function

    Dim p As Variant
    For Each p In Array("BYTE", "WORD", "PORT")
        key = mnem & "|" & op1 & "|" & CStr(p)
        If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function
    Next p

    For Each p In Array("BYTE", "WORD", "PORT")
        key = mnem & "|" & CStr(p) & "|" & op2
        If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function
        key = mnem & "|" & CStr(p) & "|"
        If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function
        key = mnem & "|" & CStr(p) & "|" & CStr(p)
        If opMap.Exists(key) Then HlpFindOpcode = opMap(key): Exit Function
    Next p

    HlpFindOpcode = Empty
End Function

' =============================================================================
' Encode instruction bytes (1/2/3 bytes), using label/EQU resolution via clsLabels
' =============================================================================
Private Function HlpEncodeInstruction(ByVal lbls As clsLabels, ByVal opByte As Byte, ByVal nBytes As Long, _
                                   ByVal spec1 As String, ByVal spec2 As String, _
                                   ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String, _
                                   ByVal opname As String, ByVal curRow As Range, ByVal wsCPU As Worksheet) As Variant

    Dim out() As Variant

    Select Case nBytes
        Case 1
            ReDim out(0 To 0)
            out(0) = opByte

        Case 2
            ReDim out(0 To 1)
            out(0) = opByte

            Dim imm8 As Long
            imm8 = ResolveValue8(lbls, HlpPickImmediateToken(spec1, spec2, op1, op2), opname, wsCPU, curRow)
            out(1) = CByte(imm8 And &HFF&)

        Case 3
            ReDim out(0 To 2)
            out(0) = opByte

            Dim imm16 As Long
            imm16 = cmpResolveValue16(lbls, HlpPickImmediateToken(spec1, spec2, op1, op2))

            ' 8080 immediates are little-endian: low byte then high byte
            out(1) = CByte(imm16 And &HFF&)
            out(2) = CByte((imm16 \ 256) And &HFF&)

        Case Else
            cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, "Unsupported instruction length: " & nBytes & " for " & opname, curRow
            HlpEncodeInstruction = Empty
            Exit Function
    End Select

    HlpEncodeInstruction = out
End Function

Private Function HlpPickImmediateToken(ByVal spec1 As String, ByVal spec2 As String, ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String) As String
    If HlpIsPlaceholder(spec1) Then
        HlpPickImmediateToken = op1
    ElseIf HlpIsPlaceholder(spec2) Then
        HlpPickImmediateToken = op2
    Else
        If Len(op2) > 0 Then HlpPickImmediateToken = op2 Else HlpPickImmediateToken = op1
    End If
End Function

Private Function HlpIsPlaceholder(ByVal s As String) As Boolean
    s = UCase$(Trim$(s))
    HlpIsPlaceholder = (s = "BYTE" Or s = "ADDRESS" Or s = "PORT" Or s = "DATA")
End Function

' =============================================================================
' Operand resolution
' =============================================================================
Private Function ResolveValue8(ByVal lbls As clsLabels, ByVal token As String, _
                               ByVal opname As String, ByVal wsCPU As Worksheet, ByVal curRow As Range) As Long
    token = UCase$(Trim$(token))
    If token = "" Then
        cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, opname & " missing 8-bit immediate", curRow
        ResolveValue8 = 0
        Exit Function
    End If

    Dim rec As clsLabelRecord
    Set rec = lbls.GetLabel(token)
    If Not rec Is Nothing Then
        ResolveValue8 = (rec.clsAddress And &HFF&)
        Exit Function
    End If

    If usrValIsHexString(token) Then
        ResolveValue8 = usrHexToDec(token) And &HFF&
    ElseIf IsNumeric(token) Then
        ResolveValue8 = CLng(token) And &HFF&
    Else
        cmpRaiseAsmError wsCPU, opname & " invalid imm8: " & token, curRow
        ResolveValue8 = 0
    End If
End Function

Private Function BytesToHexString(ByVal bytesOut As Variant) As String
    Dim i As Long, s As String
    s = ""
    For i = LBound(bytesOut) To UBound(bytesOut)
        s = s & IIf(Len(s) > 0, " ", "") & Right$("00" & Hex$(CLng(bytesOut(i)) And &HFF&), 2)
    Next i
    BytesToHexString = s
End Function

' =============================================================================
' Helpers / safety wrappers
' =============================================================================
Public Function StripComment(ByVal s As String) As String
    Dim p As Long
    p = InStr(1, s, ";", vbBinaryCompare)
    If p > 0 Then StripComment = Trim$(Left$(s, p - 1)) Else StripComment = Trim$(s)
End Function



Public Sub Compile_SetEnabled(ByVal enabled As Boolean)
    gCompileEnabled = enabled
End Sub

Public Function Compile_IsEnabled() As Boolean
    ' default enabled if never set
    If gCompileEnabled = False And gCompiledForResetStamp = 0 Then
        gCompileEnabled = True
    End If
    Compile_IsEnabled = gCompileEnabled
End Function

Public Sub Compile_Invalidate()
    gCompiledValid = False
    gLastCodeSignature = vbNullString
End Sub
Public Sub CompileIfNeeded(ByVal wsCPU As Worksheet)
    ' If disabled, do nothing
    If Not Compile_IsEnabled() Then Exit Sub

    Dim doReset As Boolean
    doReset = (CLng(wsCPU.Range("Reset").value) = 1)

    ' Only compile on Reset, unless cache invalidated
    If doReset Then
        gCompiledValid = False
    End If

    If gCompiledValid Then Exit Sub

    ' Optional: cheap signature check to avoid compiling if nothing changed even on Reset
    ' (you can comment this out initially)
    'Dim sig As String
    'sig = ComputeCodeSignature(wsCPU)
    'If sig = gLastCodeSignature And doReset = False Then
    '    gCompiledValid = True
    '    Exit Sub
    'End If

    ' Call your actual compiler
    AssembleForCPUMode

    ' Mark cache valid
    gCompiledValid = True
    gCompiledForResetStamp = Timer
    'gLastCodeSignature = sig
End Sub



''' Component: tests
Public Sub myTests()
    Dim pNodes As clsAddrList
    Dim pNodeRec As clsAddrRecord
    Set pNodes = New clsAddrList
    Dim i As Long
    Dim c As Long
    c = pNodes.size
    Dim startAddr As Long
    startAddr = CLng(Range("line0").value)
    For i = startAddr To c + startAddr - 1
        Set pNodeRec = pNodes.GetAddr(i)
        Debug.Print i, pNodeRec.clsAddress, pNodeRec.clsAddressLast, pNodeRec.clsAddressNext
    Next i
End Sub
Public Function tstHlpGetInstructionSize(ByVal opcode As String, Optional ByVal op1 As String = "", Optional ByVal op2 As String = "") As Integer
    Dim byteCount As Integer
    Debug.Assert opcode = ""
    byteCount = HlpGetInstructionSize(opcode, op1, op2)
    tstHlpGetInstructionSize = byteCount
End Function

''' Component: clsMemory
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsMemory
' Purpose:      Memory representation

'================================================================================
Private pStartAddress As Long
Private pMemSize As Long
Private pInitialized As Boolean
Private pMemory() As Byte
Private pMemError As Boolean

Private Sub Class_Initialize()
    Dim wsCPU As Worksheet
    Set wsCPU = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU")
    pStartAddress = usrHexToDec(CStr(wsCPU.Range("MemStart").value))
    pMemSize = usrHexToDec(CStr(wsCPU.Range("MemSize").value))
    ReDim pMemory(0 To pMemSize)
    pInitialized = True
    pMemError = False
End Sub

Public Function IsInitialized() As Boolean
    IsInitialized = pInitialized
End Function

Public Property Get addr(ByVal memAddr As Long) As Byte
    Dim offset As Long
    offset = memAddr - pStartAddress
    If offset < 0 Or offset > pMemSize Then
        addr = 0
        pMemError = True
    Else
        addr = pMemory(offset)
        pMemError = False
    End If
End Property

Public Property Let addr(ByVal memAddr As Long, ByVal value As Byte)
    Dim offset As Long
    offset = memAddr - pStartAddress
    If offset < 0 Or offset > pMemSize Then
        Debug.Print "Invalid Address: " & offset & " non in range (0," & pMemSize & ")"
        pMemError = False
        Exit Property
    End If
    pMemError = False
    pMemory(offset) = value
End Property

Public Function StartAddress() As Long
    StartAddress = pStartAddress
End Function

Public Function MemorySize() As Long
    MemorySize = pMemSize
End Function
Public Property Get MemError() As Boolean
    MemError = pMemError
End Property


''' Component: clsAddrRecord
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsAddrRecord
' Purpose:      Node in a double linked list used for memory addressing
'================================================================================
Public clsAddress As Long
Public clsAddressHex As String
Public clsAddressLast As Long
Public clsAddressNext As Long
Public clsIndex As Long

''' Component: clsAddrList
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        clsAddrList
'================================================================================

Private pNodes As Object
Private wsCPU As Worksheet

Private Sub Class_Initialize()
    Set wsCPU = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU")
    Set pNodes = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    ParseAddresses
End Sub

Public Sub ParseAddresses()
    Dim data As Variant
    Dim r As Long
    Dim nodeRec As clsAddrRecord
    Dim line0 As Range
    Dim maxRows As Long
    Dim addr_hex As String
    Dim addr_dec As Long
    Dim addr_previous As Long
    Dim emptyRun As Long
    Dim ofs_opcode As Long
    Dim ofs_label As Long
    Dim opcode As String
    Const EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT As Long = 8   ' stop after 8 consecutive empty rows
  
    pNodes.RemoveAll


    Set line0 = wsCPU.Range("Line0")
    ofs_opcode = wsCPU.Range("ofs_opcode").value
    ofs_label = wsCPU.Range("ofs_label").value
    addr_previous = 0
    emptyRun = 0

    ' Offsets into the CPU grid
    ' Upper bound so we don't scan forever: MemSize + 1 is perfect
    ' (Your grid is MemStart..MemEnd; MemSize is in hex on CPU sheet.)
    maxRows = CLng(usrHexToDec(CStr(wsCPU.Range("MemSize").value))) + 1
    If maxRows < 1 Then maxRows = 1
    If maxRows > 5000 Then maxRows = 5000 ' hard safety cap

    ' Pull a block once for speed: from column 1 through ofs_ops2
    data = line0.offset(0, 0).Resize(maxRows, ofs_opcode + 1).value
    For r = 1 To UBound(data, 1)
        ' Read the program fields from the array (1-based array)
        addr_dec = CLng(data(r, 1))
        opcode = CStr(data(r, ofs_opcode + 1))
        'skip comments
        If data(r, ofs_label + 1) = ";" Then
            GoTo NextRow
        End If
        
        ' Determine whether this row is "program-empty"
        If data(r, 1) = "" Or addr_dec = addr_previous Or opcode = "" Then
            emptyRun = emptyRun + 1
            If emptyRun >= EMPTY_RUN_LIMIT Then Exit For
            GoTo NextRow
        Else
            emptyRun = 0
        End If
        
        If opcode = "EQU" Or opcode = "ORG" Then
            GoTo NextRow
        End If
        
        If data(r, 1) = "" Or addr_dec = 0 Then
            Exit For
        End If
        Set nodeRec = New clsAddrRecord
        nodeRec.clsAddress = addr_dec
        nodeRec.clsAddressHex = usrDecToHexString(addr_dec)
        If r = 1 Then
            nodeRec.clsAddressLast = 0
        Else
            nodeRec.clsAddressLast = addr_previous
        End If
        If r = maxRows Then
            nodeRec.clsAddressNext = 0
        Else
            nodeRec.clsAddressNext = CLng(data(r + 1, 1))
        End If
        nodeRec.clsIndex = r - 1
        pNodes.ADD addr_dec, nodeRec
        addr_previous = addr_dec

NextRow:
    Next r
End Sub

'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' GetLabel
' Returns the label record if found, else Nothing.
'------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Public Function GetAddr(ByVal addr As Long) As clsAddrRecord
    If pNodes.Exists(addr) Then
        Set GetAddr = pNodes(addr)
    Else
        Set GetAddr = Nothing
    End If
End Function

Public Function size() As Long
    size = pNodes.Count
End Function



''' Component: Sheet7
''' [No code]

''' Component: Trace
Option Explicit

'=========================
' Trace mode (buffered)
'=========================
Private Const TRACE_BATCH As Long = 500          ' grow buffer in chunks
Private Const TRACE_MAX_ROWS As Long = 20000     ' hard cap safety

Private gTraceArr() As Variant                  ' 2D array buffer
Private gTraceCount As Long                     ' total entries captured
Private gTraceWritten As Long                   ' how many entries flushed to sheet
Private gHeadersWritten As Boolean

' Columns (fixed order)
'  1 Step#
'  2 PC
'  3 Op
'  4 OP1
'  5 OP2
'  6 A
'  7 B
'  8 C
'  9 D
' 10 E
' 11 H
' 12 L
' 13 SP
' 14 S
' 15 Z
' 16 P
' 17 CY
' 18 AC
' 19 Err
'20 memAddr
'21 MemBefore
'22 MemAfter
'23 MemNote
Private Const TRACE_COLS As Long = 23

Public Function TraceEnabled() As Boolean
    ' Controlled by CPU!Trace (named range). Missing range => False.
    On Error Resume Next
    TraceEnabled = (CLng(ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU").Range("Trace").value) = 1)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then TraceEnabled = False
    On Error GoTo 0
End Function

Public Function TraceLive() As Boolean
    ' Optional CPU!TraceLive (named range). Missing => False.
    On Error Resume Next
    TraceLive = (CLng(ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU").Range("TraceLive").value) = 1)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then TraceLive = False
    On Error GoTo 0
End Function
Public Function TraceMemReads() As Boolean
    On Error Resume Next
    TraceMemReads = (CLng(ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("CPU").Range("TraceMemReads").value) = 1)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then TraceMemReads = False
    On Error GoTo 0
End Function
Public Sub TraceClear()
    gTraceCount = 0
    gTraceWritten = 0
    gHeadersWritten = False
    Erase gTraceArr

    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Set ws = TraceGetSheet(True)
    ws.Cells.Clear
End Sub

Private Function TraceGetSheet(Optional ByVal createIfMissing As Boolean = True) As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set TraceGetSheet = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("Trace")
    On Error GoTo 0

    If TraceGetSheet Is Nothing And createIfMissing Then
        Set TraceGetSheet = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets.ADD(After:=ThisWorkbook.Sheets(ThisWorkbook.Sheets.Count))
        TraceGetSheet.name = "Trace"
    End If
End Function

Private Sub TraceEnsureHeaders()
    If gHeadersWritten Then Exit Sub

    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Set ws = TraceGetSheet(True)

    Dim headers As Variant
    headers = Array("Step", "PC", "Op", "OP1", "OP2", _
                    "A", "B", "C", "D", "E", "H", "L", "SP", _
                    "S", "Z", "P", "CY", "AC", "Err", _
                    "MemAddr", "MemBefore", "MemAfter", "MemNote")

    ws.Range("A1").Resize(1, UBound(headers) + 1).value = headers
    ws.Rows(1).Font.Bold = True

    ws.Columns("A").ColumnWidth = 8
    ws.Columns("B").ColumnWidth = 6
    ws.Columns("C").ColumnWidth = 8
    ws.Columns("D:E").ColumnWidth = 10
    ws.Columns("F:M").ColumnWidth = 4
    ws.Columns("N:S").ColumnWidth = 4
    ws.Columns("T").ColumnWidth = 8   ' MemAddr
    ws.Columns("U:V").ColumnWidth = 10 ' before/after
    ws.Columns("W").ColumnWidth = 28  ' note
    ws.Columns("T:W").NumberFormat = "@"
    
    ' Keep hex-looking fields as text (prevents Excel auto-formatting)
    ws.Columns("B").NumberFormat = "@"
    ws.Columns("F:M").NumberFormat = "@"

    gHeadersWritten = True
End Sub

Private Sub TraceEnsureCapacity(ByVal neededRow As Long)
    Dim curRows As Long

    ' If the array is not allocated yet, UBound will error.
    On Error Resume Next
    curRows = UBound(gTraceArr, 1)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then
        Err.Clear
        ReDim gTraceArr(1 To TRACE_BATCH, 1 To TRACE_COLS)
        Exit Sub
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0

    If neededRow <= curRows Then Exit Sub

    ReDim Preserve gTraceArr(1 To (curRows + TRACE_BATCH), 1 To TRACE_COLS)
End Sub

Private Function Hex2(ByVal v As Long) As String
    Hex2 = Right$("00" & Hex$(v And 255), 2)
End Function

Private Function Hex4(ByVal v As Long) As String
    Hex4 = Right$("0000" & Hex$(v And &HFFFF&), 4)
End Function

Public Sub TraceAppend(ByRef cpu As clsDecCPU, _
                       ByVal pc_dec As Long, _
                       ByVal opcode As String, _
                       ByVal op1 As String, _
                       ByVal op2 As String, _
                       ByVal errcode As Long, _
                       Optional ByVal memAddr As String = "", _
                       Optional ByVal memBefore As String = "", _
                       Optional ByVal memAfter As String = "", _
                       Optional ByVal memNote As String = "")
                       
    If Not TraceEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If gTraceCount >= TRACE_MAX_ROWS Then Exit Sub

    TraceEnsureHeaders

    gTraceCount = gTraceCount + 1
    TraceEnsureCapacity gTraceCount

    Dim r As Long: r = gTraceCount

    gTraceArr(r, 1) = r
    gTraceArr(r, 2) = Hex4(pc_dec)
    gTraceArr(r, 3) = opcode
    gTraceArr(r, 4) = op1
    gTraceArr(r, 5) = op2

    gTraceArr(r, 6) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("A"))
    gTraceArr(r, 7) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("B"))
    gTraceArr(r, 8) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("C"))
    gTraceArr(r, 9) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("D"))
    gTraceArr(r, 10) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("E"))
    gTraceArr(r, 11) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("H"))
    gTraceArr(r, 12) = Hex2(cpu.Reg("L"))
    gTraceArr(r, 13) = Hex4(cpu.Reg("SP"))

    gTraceArr(r, 14) = cpu.Flag("Sign")
    gTraceArr(r, 15) = cpu.Flag("Zero")
    gTraceArr(r, 16) = cpu.Flag("Parity")
    gTraceArr(r, 17) = cpu.Flag("Carry")
    gTraceArr(r, 18) = cpu.Flag("AC")

    gTraceArr(r, 19) = errcode
    
    gTraceArr(r, 20) = memAddr
    gTraceArr(r, 21) = memBefore
    gTraceArr(r, 22) = memAfter
    gTraceArr(r, 23) = memNote
End Sub
'================================================================================
'  Private gTraceArr, gTraceCount, TRACE_MAX_ROWS, TraceEnsureHeaders,
'  and TraceEnsureCapacity, which is why it must live there not here)
'
' Register columns:  A->col6, X->col7, Y->col8, cols 9-12 blank, SP->col13
' Flag columns:      N->col14(S), Z->col15, V->col16(P), C->col17(CY), I->col18(AC)
'================================================================================
'
Public Sub TraceAppend6510(ByRef cpu As cls6510cpu, _
                           ByVal pc_dec As Long, _
                           ByVal opcode As String, _
                           ByVal op1 As String, _
                           ByVal op2 As String, _
                           ByVal errcode As Long, _
                           Optional ByVal memAddr As String = "", _
                           Optional ByVal memBefore As String = "", _
                           Optional ByVal memAfter As String = "", _
                           Optional ByVal memNote As String = "")

    If Not TraceEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If gTraceCount >= TRACE_MAX_ROWS Then Exit Sub
    TraceEnsureHeaders
    gTraceCount = gTraceCount + 1
    TraceEnsureCapacity gTraceCount
    Dim r As Long: r = gTraceCount
    gTraceArr(r, 1) = r
    gTraceArr(r, 2) = Right$("0000" & Hex$(pc_dec And &HFFFF&), 4)
    gTraceArr(r, 3) = opcode
    gTraceArr(r, 4) = op1
    gTraceArr(r, 5) = op2
    gTraceArr(r, 6) = Right$("00" & Hex$(cpu.Reg("A") And 255), 2)
    gTraceArr(r, 7) = Right$("00" & Hex$(cpu.Reg("X") And 255), 2)
    gTraceArr(r, 8) = Right$("00" & Hex$(cpu.Reg("Y") And 255), 2)
    gTraceArr(r, 9) = ""    ' no D
    gTraceArr(r, 10) = ""   ' no E
    gTraceArr(r, 11) = ""   ' no H
    gTraceArr(r, 12) = ""   ' no L
    gTraceArr(r, 13) = Right$("00" & Hex$(cpu.Reg("SP") And 255), 2)
    gTraceArr(r, 14) = cpu.Flag("N")   ' S  col = Negative
    gTraceArr(r, 15) = cpu.Flag("Z")   ' Z  col = Zero
    gTraceArr(r, 16) = cpu.Flag("V")   ' P  col = oVerflow
    gTraceArr(r, 17) = cpu.Flag("C")   ' CY col = Carry
    gTraceArr(r, 18) = cpu.Flag("I")   ' AC col = Interrupt (repurposed)
    gTraceArr(r, 19) = errcode
    gTraceArr(r, 20) = memAddr
    gTraceArr(r, 21) = memBefore
    gTraceArr(r, 22) = memAfter
    gTraceArr(r, 23) = memNote
End Sub


Public Sub TraceFlush(Optional ByVal forceAll As Boolean = False)
    If Not TraceEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If gTraceCount = 0 Then Exit Sub

    TraceEnsureHeaders

    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Set ws = TraceGetSheet(True)

    Dim startRow As Long, rowsToWrite As Long
    If forceAll Then
        gTraceWritten = 0
    End If

    rowsToWrite = gTraceCount - gTraceWritten
    If rowsToWrite <= 0 Then Exit Sub

    startRow = 2 + gTraceWritten

    ws.Range("A" & startRow).Resize(rowsToWrite, TRACE_COLS).value = _
        wsParentSlice(gTraceArr, gTraceWritten + 1, gTraceCount, TRACE_COLS)

    gTraceWritten = gTraceCount
End Sub

' Helper: slice a 2D array [r1..r2, 1..cols] into a new 2D array
Private Function wsParentSlice(ByRef src As Variant, ByVal r1 As Long, ByVal r2 As Long, ByVal cols As Long) As Variant
    Dim out As Variant
    Dim rr As Long, cc As Long, rOut As Long
    ReDim out(1 To (r2 - r1 + 1), 1 To cols)
    rOut = 0
    For rr = r1 To r2
        rOut = rOut + 1
        For cc = 1 To cols
            out(rOut, cc) = src(rr, cc)
        Next cc
    Next rr
    wsParentSlice = out
End Function

' Convenience button macros
Public Sub BTN_ClearTrace()
    TraceClear
End Sub

Public Sub BTN_FlushTrace()
    TraceFlush True
End Sub


''' Component: Sheet6
''' [No code]

''' Component: Sheet9
''' [No code]

''' Component: VBATests
Option Explicit
' ==============================================================================
' Test Helper Functions
' ==============================================================================

Private pTestHeader As String
Private pHeadersPrinted As Boolean
Private pTestError As Boolean
Private pTestCount As Long
Private pTestFailureCount As Long
Private Function CreateTestCPU() As clsDecCPU
    ' Create fresh CPU instance - auto-initializes via Class_Initialize
    Set CreateTestCPU = New clsDecCPU
End Function
Public Sub VBARunAllTests()
    VBAResetCounts
    VBAClaudeSetOne
    VBAClaudeSetTwo
    VBA6510RunAllTests
End Sub
Public Function VBATestCount() As Long
    VBATestCount = pTestCount + VBA6510TestCount()
End Function
Public Function VBAFailureCount() As Long
    VBAFailureCount = pTestFailureCount + VBA6510FailureCount()
End Function
Public Function VBAPassed() As Boolean
    VBAPassed = Not pTestError And VBA6510Passed()
End Function
Private Sub VBAResetCounts()
    pHeadersPrinted = False
    pTestError = False
    pTestError = 0
    pTestCount = 0
    pTestFailureCount = 0
End Sub

Private Sub AssertEquals(expected As Long, actual As Long, testName As String)
    If pHeadersPrinted Then
        TestHeader pTestHeader
    Else
        pHeadersPrinted = False
    End If

    If expected = actual Then
        'Debug.Print "  ? " & testName & " (expected=" & expected & ")"
    Else
        Debug.Print "  ? FAIL: " & testName & " (expected=" & expected & ", got=" & actual & ")"
        pTestFailureCount = pTestFailureCount + 1
        pTestError = True
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub AssertTrue(condition As Boolean, testName As String)
    If condition Then
        'Debug.Print "  ? " & testName
    Else
        Debug.Print "  ? FAIL: " & testName
    End If
End Sub

Private Sub TestHeader(category As String)
    Debug.Print ""
    Debug.Print "-------------------------------------------------------------------"
    Debug.Print "Testing: " & pTestHeader
    Debug.Print "-------------------------------------------------------------------"
End Sub

Sub Test_ADD()
    pTestHeader = "ADD (Add Register to A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic addition without overflow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80         ' 0x50 in hex
    cpu.SetReg "B", 48         ' 0x30 in hex
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 80 + 48 = 128 (0x80)"
    
    ' Test 2: Addition with carry/overflow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255        ' 0xFF in hex
    cpu.SetReg "B", 1          ' 0x01 in hex
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 255 + 1 = 0 (overflow, wraps)"
    
    ' Test 3: Auxiliary carry (AC flag)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 15         ' 0x0F in hex
    cpu.SetReg "B", 1          ' 0x01 in hex
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 16, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 15 + 1 = 16 (0x10)"
    
    ' Test 4: Sign flag
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 112        ' 0x70 in hex
    cpu.SetReg "B", 32         ' 0x20 in hex
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 144, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 112 + 32 = 144 (0x90, sign set)"
    
    ' Test 5: ADD with same register (A = A + A, double A)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 64         ' 0x40 in hex
    cpu.ADD "A"
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 64 + 64 = 128 (double)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_ADI()
    pTestHeader = "ADI (Add Immediate to A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic addition - pass hex string WITHOUT & prefix
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.ADI "30"             ' Pass as hex digits only: 30 hex = 48 decimal
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADI: 80 + 48 = 128 (using hex string 30)"
    
    ' Test 2: With overflow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255
    cpu.ADI "02"             ' 02 hex = 2 decimal
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADI: 255 + 2 = 1 (overflow)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_ADC()
    pTestHeader = "ADC (Add Register with Carry to A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Add with carry clear (requires carry flag manipulation)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SetReg "B", 48
    cpu.ADC "B"
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADC: 80 + 48 = 128 (no carry input)"
    
    ' Test 2: Add with carry set (would be 81 if carry is properly included)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SetReg "B", 48
    cpu.ADC "B"
    ' Result depends on initial carry flag state
    
End Sub

Sub Test_SUB()
    pTestHeader = "SUB (Subtract Register from A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic subtraction
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SetReg "B", 48
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals 32, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 80 - 48 = 32 (0x20)"
    
    ' Test 2: Subtraction with borrow (A < B)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 48
    cpu.SetReg "B", 80
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals 224, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 48 - 80 = 224 (0xE0, wraps with borrow)"
    
    ' Test 3: Subtract from itself (result = 0)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SUB_ "A"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 80 - 80 = 0"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_SUI()
    pTestHeader = "SUI (Subtract Immediate from A)"

    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SUI "30"             ' 30 hex = 48 decimal
    AssertEquals 32, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUI: 80 - 48 = 32"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_ANA()
    pTestHeader = "ANA (AND Register with A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic AND
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255        ' 0xFF
    cpu.SetReg "B", 15         ' 0x0F
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals 15, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: 255 AND 15 = 15 (0x0F)"
    
    ' Test 2: AND with 0
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: 255 AND 0 = 0"
    
    ' Test 3: AND with itself
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 165        ' 0xA5
    cpu.ANA "A"
    AssertEquals 165, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: 165 AND 165 = 165 (identity)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_ANI()
    pTestHeader = "ANI (AND Immediate with A)"

    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 245        ' 0xF5
    cpu.ANI "0F"             ' Hex 0F = 15 decimal, mask
    AssertEquals 5, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANI: 245 AND 15 = 5 (0xF5 AND 0x0F = 0x05)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_ORI()
    pTestHeader = "ORI (OR Immediate with A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Set bit 7 using OR
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 0
    cpu.ORI "80"             ' 80 hex = 128 decimal, which is bit 7
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "ORI: 0 OR 128 = 128 (0x80, bit 7 set)"
    
    ' Test 2: Combine patterns
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 240        ' 0xF0
    cpu.ORI "0F"             ' 0x0F
    AssertEquals 255, cpu.Reg("A"), "ORI: 240 OR 15 = 255 (0xFF)"
    
End Sub

    cpu.SetReg "B", 0

Sub Test_CMP()
    pTestHeader = "CMP (Compare Register with A)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: A = B (equal)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.SetReg "B", 80
    cpu.CMP "B"
    AssertEquals 80, cpu.Reg("A"), "CMP: A unchanged (80)"
    
    ' Test 2: A > B
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 128
    cpu.SetReg "B", 64
    cpu.CMP "B"
    AssertEquals 128, cpu.Reg("A"), "CMP: A unchanged (128)"
    
    ' Test 3: A < B
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 64
    cpu.SetReg "B", 128
    cpu.CMP "B"
    AssertEquals 64, cpu.Reg("A"), "CMP: A unchanged (64)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_INR()
    pTestHeader = "INR (Increment Register)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic increment
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.INR "A"
    AssertEquals 81, cpu.Reg("A"), "INR: 80 + 1 = 81"
    
    ' Test 2: Increment with overflow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255
    cpu.INR "A"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "INR: 255 + 1 = 0 (wrap around)"
    
    ' Test 3: AC flag on half-carry
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 15         ' 0x0F
    cpu.INR "A"
    AssertEquals 16, cpu.Reg("A"), "INR: 15 + 1 = 16 (half-carry)"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_DCR()
    pTestHeader = "DCR (Decrement Register)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic decrement
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 80
    cpu.DCR "A"
    AssertEquals 79, cpu.Reg("A"), "DCR: 80 - 1 = 79"
    
    ' Test 2: Decrement from 0
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 0
    cpu.DCR "A"
    AssertEquals 255, cpu.Reg("A"), "DCR: 0 - 1 = 255 (wrap around)"
    
    ' Test 3: Decrement to 0
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 1
    cpu.DCR "A"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "DCR: 1 - 1 = 0"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_INX()
    pTestHeader = "INX (Increment Register Pair)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Increment BC
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "B", 16         ' 0x10
    cpu.SetReg "C", 0
    cpu.INX "B"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Reg("C"), "INX: C remains 0 when not at 255"
    
    ' Test 2: Increment with carry
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "B", 16
    cpu.SetReg "C", 255
    cpu.INX "B"
    AssertEquals 17, cpu.Reg("B"), "INX: B incremented from 16 to 17 when C overflows"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("C"), "INX: C wrapped from 255 to 0"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_DCX()
    pTestHeader = "DCX (Decrement Register Pair)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Decrement BC
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "B", 16
    cpu.SetReg "C", 1
    cpu.DCX "B"
    AssertEquals 16, cpu.Reg("B"), "DCX: B unchanged when C not at 0"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("C"), "DCX: C decremented"
    
    ' Test 2: Decrement with borrow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "B", 16
    cpu.SetReg "C", 0
    cpu.DCX "B"
    AssertEquals 15, cpu.Reg("B"), "DCX: B decremented when C at 0"
    AssertEquals 255, cpu.Reg("C"), "DCX: C wrapped to 255"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_DAD()
    pTestHeader = "DAD (Double Add - HL += regpair)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Add BC to HL
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "H", 16         ' HL = 0x1000 = 4096
    cpu.SetReg "L", 0
    cpu.SetReg "B", 32         ' BC = 0x2000 = 8192
    cpu.SetReg "C", 0
    cpu.DAD "B"
    AssertEquals 48, cpu.Reg("H"), "DAD: H = 16 + 32 = 48 (HL += BC)"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("L"), "DAD: L unchanged"
    
End Sub

Sub Test_ADD_EdgeCases()
    pTestHeader = "ADD - Edge Cases"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Zero + Zero
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 0
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 0 + 0 = 0"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "ADD: Zero flag set"
    
    ' Test 2: Max + Max = overflow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255
    cpu.SetReg "B", 255
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 254, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 255 + 255 = 254 (wrap, carry set)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "ADD: Carry flag set on overflow"
    
    ' Test 3: Half-carry boundary (0x0F + 0x01)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HF
    cpu.SetReg "B", 1
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals &H10, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: Half-carry detected at 4-bit boundary"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("AC"), "ADD: AC (Auxiliary Carry) flag set"
    
    ' Test 4: Parity - 7 bits set (odd parity)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H7F   ' 0111 1111
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals &H7F, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADD: 127 unchanged"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Parity"), "ADD: Parity flag clear (odd)"
    
    ' Test 5: Parity - 8 bits set (even parity)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HFF   ' 1111 1111
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.ADD "B"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Parity"), "ADD: Parity flag set (even)"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_ADC_WithCarry()
    pTestHeader = "ADC - Add with Carry"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: ADC without carry-in
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 50
    cpu.SetReg "B", 30
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 0
    cpu.ADC "B"
    AssertEquals 80, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADC: 50 + 30 + 0 = 80"
    
    ' Test 2: ADC with carry-in (adds 1)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 50
    cpu.SetReg "B", 30
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.ADC "B"
    AssertEquals 81, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADC: 50 + 30 + 1(carry) = 81"
    
    ' Test 3: ADC causing carry-out
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 255
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.ADC "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADC: 255 + 0 + 1 = 0 (overflow, carry set)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "ADC: Carry flag set on overflow"
    
    ' Test 4: ADC with half-carry from Carry bit
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HF
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.ADC "B"
    AssertEquals &H10, cpu.Reg("A"), "ADC: 15 + 0 + 1(C) = 16 (half-carry)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("AC"), "ADC: AC flag set"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_SUB_BorrowCases()
    pTestHeader = "SUB - Subtract with Borrow"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Simple subtraction
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 100
    cpu.SetReg "B", 30
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals 70, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 100 - 30 = 70"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "SUB: No borrow (Carry clear)"
    
    ' Test 2: Subtraction requiring borrow
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 30
    cpu.SetReg "B", 100
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals 186, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 30 - 100 = -70 (wrap to 186)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "SUB: Borrow required (Carry set)"
    
    ' Test 3: Subtract from zero
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 0
    cpu.SetReg "B", 1
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals 255, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 0 - 1 = 255 (underflow wrap)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "SUB: Carry set (borrow)"
    
    ' Test 4: Half-carry borrow (crossing nibble boundary)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H10
    cpu.SetReg "B", 1
    cpu.SUB_ "B"
    AssertEquals &HF, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: 16 - 1 = 15"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("AC"), "SUB: AC flag set (half-borrow)"
    
    ' Test 5: Subtract self (clear A)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 42
    cpu.SUB_ "A"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "SUB: A - A = 0"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "SUB: Zero flag set"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "SUB: No carry on zero result"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_ANA_LogicalAND()
    pTestHeader = "ANA - Logical AND"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic AND
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HFF   ' 1111 1111
    cpu.SetReg "B", &HF    ' 0000 1111
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals &HF, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: FF AND 0F = 0F"
    
    ' Test 2: AND with zero (clears A)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HFF
    cpu.SetReg "B", &H0
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: FF AND 00 = 00"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "ANA: Zero flag set"
    
    ' Test 3: AND of alternating bits
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HAA   ' 1010 1010
    cpu.SetReg "B", &H55   ' 0101 0101
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "ANA: AA AND 55 = 00"
    
    ' Test 4: AND clears carry (per 8080 spec)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HFF
    cpu.SetReg "B", &HFF
    cpu.ANA "B"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "ANA: Clears Carry flag"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_ORA_LogicalOR()
    pTestHeader = "ORA - Logical OR"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic OR
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HF    ' 0000 1111
    cpu.SetReg "B", &HF0   ' 1111 0000
    cpu.ORA "B"
    AssertEquals &HFF, cpu.Reg("A"), "ORA: 0F OR F0 = FF"
    
    ' Test 2: OR with zero (no change)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H42
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.ORA "B"
    AssertEquals &H42, cpu.Reg("A"), "ORA: 42 OR 00 = 42"
    
    ' Test 3: OR of same register
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H55
    cpu.ORA "A"
    AssertEquals &H55, cpu.Reg("A"), "ORA: 55 OR 55 = 55"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "ORA: Clears Carry"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_XRA_LogicalXOR()
    pTestHeader = "XRA - Logical XOR"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: XOR of different patterns
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HF0   ' 1111 0000
    cpu.SetReg "B", &HF    ' 0000 1111
    cpu.XRA "B"
    AssertEquals &HFF, cpu.Reg("A"), "XRA: F0 XOR 0F = FF"
    
    ' Test 2: XOR with self (clears A) - common trick to zero register
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H55
    cpu.XRA "A"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "XRA: 55 XOR 55 = 00 (common zero trick)"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "XRA: Zero flag set"
    
    ' Test 3: XOR with zero (no change)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HAA
    cpu.SetReg "B", 0
    cpu.XRA "B"
    AssertEquals &HAA, cpu.Reg("A"), "XRA: AA XOR 00 = AA"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_RLC_RotateLeftCircular()
    pTestHeader = "RLC - Rotate Left Circular (no carry)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic left rotate (bit 7 -> bit 0)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H80   ' 1000 0000
    cpu.RLC
    AssertEquals &H1, cpu.Reg("A"), "RLC: 80 rotated left = 01"
    
    ' Test 2: Rotate with carry propagation
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &HC0   ' 1100 0000
    cpu.RLC
    AssertEquals &H81, cpu.Reg("A"), "RLC: C0 rotated left = 81"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "RLC: Carry set from bit 7"
    
    ' Test 3: Rotate zero
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 0
    cpu.RLC
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("A"), "RLC: 00 rotated = 00"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_RRC_RotateRightCircular()
    pTestHeader = "RRC - Rotate Right Circular"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Basic right rotate (bit 0 -> bit 7)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H1    ' 0000 0001
    cpu.RRC
    AssertEquals &H80, cpu.Reg("A"), "RRC: 01 rotated right = 80"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "RRC: Carry set from bit 0"
    
    ' Test 2: Rotate with multiple bits
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H3    ' 0000 0011
    cpu.RRC
    AssertEquals &H81, cpu.Reg("A"), "RRC: 03 rotated right = 81"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_RAL_RotateLeftArithmetic()
    pTestHeader = "RAL - Rotate Left through Carry"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: RAL with Carry clear
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H80   ' 1000 0000
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 0
    cpu.RAL
    AssertEquals &H0, cpu.Reg("A"), "RAL: 80 << with C=0 = 00"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "RAL: Carry gets bit 7"
    
    ' Test 2: RAL with Carry set (chaining)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H0
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.RAL
    AssertEquals &H1, cpu.Reg("A"), "RAL: 00 << with C=1 = 01"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_RAR_RotateRightArithmetic()
    pTestHeader = "RAR - Rotate Right through Carry"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: RAR with Carry clear
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H1    ' 0000 0001
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 0
    cpu.RAR
    AssertEquals &H0, cpu.Reg("A"), "RAR: 01 >> with C=0 = 00"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "RAR: Carry gets bit 0"
    
    ' Test 2: RAR with Carry set (chaining)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", &H0
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.RAR
    AssertEquals &H80, cpu.Reg("A"), "RAR: 00 >> with C=1 = 80"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_CPI_CompareImmediate()
    pTestHeader = "CPI - Compare Immediate"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Equal (Zero flag set)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 42
    cpu.CPI "2A"  ' 42 hex
    AssertEquals 42, cpu.Reg("A"), "CPI: A unchanged"
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "CPI: Zero flag set when A == operand"
    
    ' Test 2: A > operand
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 100
    cpu.CPI "32"  ' 50
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "CPI: Zero flag clear when A != operand"
    
    ' Test 3: A < operand
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "A", 50
    cpu.CPI "64"  ' 100
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "CPI: Carry set when A < operand"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_LHLD_LoadMemoryToHL()
    pTestHeader = "LHLD - Load Memory to HL"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    ' Assume memory at address 0x1000: [0x42, 0x99]
    ' LHLD should load L from 0x1000, H from 0x1001
    
    cpu.LHLD "1000"
    AssertTrue (cpu.Reg("H") >= 0 And cpu.Reg("H") <= 255), _
        "LHLD: H register set from memory"
    AssertTrue (cpu.Reg("L") >= 0 And cpu.Reg("L") <= 255), _
        "LHLD: L register set from memory"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_SHLD_StoreHLToMemory()
    pTestHeader = "SHLD - Store HL to Memory"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "H", 85
    cpu.SetReg "L", 170
    cpu.SHLD "1000"
    
    ' Verify memory was written (depends on memory implementation)
    AssertTrue True, "SHLD: Store completed without error"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_FlagAndCheckFlag()
    pTestHeader = "Flag Manipulation"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    
    ' Test all flag types
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Carry"), "Flag: Carry set"
    
    cpu.SetFlag "Zero", 1
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Zero"), "Flag: Zero set"
    
    cpu.SetFlag "Sign", 1
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Sign"), "Flag: Sign set"
    
    cpu.SetFlag "Parity", 1
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("Parity"), "Flag: Parity set"
    
    cpu.SetFlag "AC", 1
    AssertEquals 1, cpu.Flag("AC"), "Flag: AC set"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_JC_JumpIfCarry()
    pTestHeader = "JC - Jump If Carry"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Jump when carry set
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 1
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JC "0100"
    AssertEquals &H100, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JC: Jumped to 0100 (Carry=1)"
    
    ' Test 2: No jump when carry clear
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Carry", 0
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JC "0100"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JC: No jump (Carry=0)"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_JNZ_JumpIfNotZero()
    pTestHeader = "JNZ - Jump If Not Zero"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Jump when zero flag clear
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Zero", 0
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JNZ "0200"
    AssertEquals &H200, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JNZ: Jumped to 0200 (Zero=0)"
    
    ' Test 2: No jump when zero flag set
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Zero", 0
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JNZ "0200"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JNZ: No jump (Zero=1)"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_JM_JumpIfMinus()
    pTestHeader = "JM - Jump If Minus (Sign=1)"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    ' Test 1: Jump when negative (Sign=1)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Sign", 1
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JM "0300"
    AssertEquals &H300, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JM: Jumped to 0300 (Sign=1)"
    
    ' Test 2: No jump when positive (Sign=0)
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetFlag "Sign", 0
    cpu.SetReg "PC", 0
    cpu.JM "0300"
    AssertEquals 0, cpu.Reg("PC"), "JM: No jump (Sign=0)"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_MOV_AllRegisterPairs()
    pTestHeader = "MOV - All Register Pair Combinations"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    Dim regs() As String: regs = Split("A,B,C,D,E,H,L", ",")
    Dim i As Long, j As Long
    
    For i = 0 To UBound(regs)
        For j = 0 To UBound(regs)
            If i <> j Then
                Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
                cpu.SetReg regs(i), 50 + i
                cpu.MOV regs(j), regs(i)
                AssertEquals 50 + i, cpu.Reg(regs(j)), _
                    "MOV: " & regs(j) & " <- " & regs(i)
            End If
        Next j
    Next i
    
End Sub
Sub Test_MVI_AllRegisters()
    pTestHeader = "MVI - Move Immediate to All Registers"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    Dim regs() As String: regs = Split("A,B,C,D,E,H,L", ",")
    Dim i As Long
    
    For i = 0 To UBound(regs)
        Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
        cpu.MVI regs(i), "55"  ' Load 0x55 = 85
        AssertEquals &H55, cpu.Reg(regs(i)), _
            "MVI: " & regs(i) & " loaded with 55"
    Next i
    
End Sub
Sub Test_PUSH_POP_StackBalance()
    pTestHeader = "PUSH/POP - Stack Balance"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    Dim initialSP As Long: initialSP = cpu.Reg("SP")
    
    ' PUSH BC
    cpu.SetReg "B", 18
    cpu.SetReg "C", 52
    cpu.PUSH "B"
    AssertEquals initialSP - 2, cpu.Reg("SP"), "PUSH: SP decremented by 2"
    
    ' POP BC into D/E
    cpu.POP "D"
    AssertEquals 18, cpu.Reg("D"), "POP: D loaded from stack"
    AssertEquals 52, cpu.Reg("E"), "POP: E loaded from stack"
    AssertEquals initialSP, cpu.Reg("SP"), "POP: SP restored"
    
End Sub
Sub Test_CALL_RET_BasicFlow()
    pTestHeader = "CALL/RET - Subroutine Flow"
    Dim cpu As clsDecCPU
    
    Set cpu = CreateTestCPU
    cpu.SetReg "PC", &H100
    Dim returnSP As Long: returnSP = cpu.Reg("SP")
    
    cpu.CALL_ "0200"
    AssertEquals &H200, cpu.Reg("PC"), "CALL: Jumped to 0200"
    'AssertNotEquals returnSP, cpu.Reg("SP"), "CALL: Return address pushed to stack"
    
End Sub

''' Component: Sheet8
''' [No code]

''' Component: Sheet10
''' [No code]

''' Component: cls6510cpu
Option Explicit
'================================================================================
' Class:        cls6510CPU
' Purpose:      CPU core for the Excel/VBA MOS 6510 emulator.
'               Mirrors the architecture of clsDecCPU exactly:
'               - Register & flag storage (Dictionary-based, same pattern)
'               - Stack helper (reuses clsDecStack unchanged)
'               - Label helper (reuses clsLabels unchanged)
'               - Memory helper (reuses clsMemory unchanged)
'               - All 56 6510 mnemonics implemented as Public Functions
'               - RunOpcode dispatcher (drop-in compatible with decExecute)
'               - UI deferral (RegistersDirty / FlagsDirty / StackDirty)
'               - HlpFlagPack / HlpFlagUnpack for Trace sheet SR column
'
' 6510 Registers (vs 8080):
'   A            - 8-bit accumulator          (same)
'   X, Y         - 8-bit index registers      (replaces B,C,D,E,H,L pairs)
'   PC           - 16-bit program counter     (same)
'   SP           - 8-bit stack pointer        (fixed page $01: $0100-$01FF)
'   SR / P       - 8-bit status register      (replaces pFlags dictionary,
'                                              but we keep the same Dict pattern)
'
' 6510 Flags (SR bit layout):  N V - B D I Z C
'   Bit 7  N  Negative   (replaces Sign)
'   Bit 6  V  oVerflow   (new; no 8080 equivalent)
'   Bit 5  -  Unused     (always 1 in hardware; we ignore)
'   Bit 4  B  Break      (set by BRK; software interrupt marker)
'   Bit 3  D  Decimal    (BCD mode; ADC/SBC behave differently when D=1)
'   Bit 2  I  Interrupt  (IRQ disable)
'   Bit 1  Z  Zero       (same)
'   Bit 0  C  Carry      (same; NOTE: borrow sense is INVERTED vs 8080)
'
' Key differences from 8080 you need to keep in mind:
'   - No register pairs (no BC/DE/HL).  Zero-page ($00-$FF) is used for
'     16-bit pointer storage via indirect addressing modes.
'   - Carry flag for SBC is inverted: C=1 means NO borrow (set CLC before SBC).
'   - All branches are relative (-128..+127 from next instruction).
'   - Stack is ALWAYS page $01 ($0100-$01FF).  SP wraps in that page.
'   - JSR pushes PC-1 (address of last byte of JSR); RTS pops and adds 1.
'   - BRK pushes PC+1 (one past the padding byte) then SR with B=1.
'
' Addressing Modes encoded in op1/op2 columns (mirrors your existing model):
'   IMM      #nn          op1 = hex literal e.g. "4A"
'   ZP       nn           op1 = 1-2 hex digit address e.g. "42"
'   ZP,X     nn,X         op1 = "42,X"
'   ZP,Y     nn,Y         op1 = "42,Y"
'   ABS      nnnn         op1 = 4-digit hex address e.g. "C000"
'   ABS,X    nnnn,X       op1 = "C000,X"
'   ABS,Y    nnnn,Y       op1 = "C000,Y"
'   IND      (nnnn)       op1 = "(C000)"  (JMP only)
'   (ZP,X)   (nn,X)       op1 = "(42,X)"
'   (ZP),Y   (nn),Y       op1 = "(42),Y"
'   IMP/ACC  (no operand) op1 = "" or "A"
'
' Notes:
'   - clsDecStack, clsLabels, clsMemory, clsAddrList, clsAddrRecord are
'     shared unchanged with the 8080/Z80 model.
'   - modGlobals: add  Public gDecCPU6510 As cls6510CPU  (same singleton
'     pattern as gDecCPU).
'   - decExecute: add a SelectEngine branch that calls Execute6510 instead
'     of Execute when the CPU sheet has a "6510" radio/cell selected.
'   - Trace sheet columns are identical; SR replaces the 8080 F register.
'
' Source:       Initial build (2026-03-22) - based on clsDecCPU v2.08
'================================================================================

'--- State ---
Private pRegs   As Object          ' Dictionary: A, X, Y, PC, SP (decimal Long)
Private pFlags  As Object          ' Dictionary: N, V, B, D, I, Z, C (0/1 ints)
Private pStack  As New clsDecStack
Private pLabels As New clsLabels
Private pMemory As clsMemory
Private pAddressList As clsAddrList

'--- UI deferral (headless runs) ---
Private mUIRegsDirty  As Boolean
Private mUIFlagsDirty As Boolean
Private mUIStackDirty As Boolean

'--- Error state (mirrors clsDecCPU.SetError / Err pattern) ---
Private pLastErrCode As Long
Private pLastErrMsg  As String

'================================================================================
' Class_Initialize
'================================================================================
Private Sub Class_Initialize()
    Set pRegs = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    pRegs.ADD "A", 0
    pRegs.ADD "X", 0
    pRegs.ADD "Y", 0
    pRegs.ADD "PC", 0
    pRegs.ADD "SP", &HFF         ' points to top of stack page; wraps in $01xx

    ' excel does not like 1 character range names so register names are written out and reused from 8080 GUI
    Set pFlags = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    pFlags.ADD "N", 0            ' Negative (N)
    pFlags.ADD "V", 0            ' oVerflow (V)
    pFlags.ADD "B", 0            ' Break (B)
    pFlags.ADD "D", 0            ' Decimal (D)
    pFlags.ADD "I", 1            ' Interrupt disable (set on reset) (I)
    pFlags.ADD "Z", 0            ' Zero (Z)
    pFlags.ADD "C", 0            ' Carry (C)

    Set pAddressList = gAddressList
    Set pMemory = gMemory
End Sub
' --- Class_Initialize ---

'================================================================================
' RunOpcode
' Drop-in replacement for clsDecCPU.RunOpcode.
' Called by decExecute (or a new Execute6510 module) with the same signature.
' Returns 0 on success; ERR_EXEC_END / ERR_BAD_OPCODE / negative on halt/error.
'================================================================================
Public Function RunOpcode(ByVal opcode As String, _
    ByVal op1 As String, ByVal op2 As String, _
    Optional ByVal label As String = "") As Long

    Dim result As Long
    result = 0

    Select Case opcode
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Load / Store
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "LDA": result = Me.LDA(op1)
        Case "LDX": result = Me.LDX(op1)
        Case "LDY": result = Me.LDY(op1)
        Case "STA": result = Me.STA(op1)
        Case "STX": result = Me.STX(op1)
        Case "STY": result = Me.STY(op1)

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Register transfers
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "TAX": result = Me.TAX()
        Case "TAY": result = Me.TAY()
        Case "TXA": result = Me.TXA()
        Case "TYA": result = Me.TYA()
        Case "TSX": result = Me.TSX()
        Case "TXS": result = Me.TXS()

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Stack
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "PHA": result = Me.PHA()
        Case "PHP": result = Me.PHP()
        Case "PLA": result = Me.PLA()
        Case "PLP": result = Me.PLP()

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Arithmetic
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "ADC": result = Me.ADC(op1)
        Case "SBC": result = Me.SBC(op1)
        Case "INC": result = Me.INC(op1)
        Case "INX": result = Me.INX()
        Case "INY": result = Me.INY()
        Case "DEC": result = Me.DEC(op1)
        Case "DEX": result = Me.DEX()
        Case "DEY": result = Me.DEY()

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Logical
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "AND": result = Me.AND_(op1)
        Case "ORA": result = Me.ORA(op1)
        Case "EOR": result = Me.EOR(op1)
        Case "BIT": result = Me.BIT(op1)

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Shifts & Rotates
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "ASL": result = Me.ASL(op1)
        Case "LSR": result = Me.LSR(op1)
        Case "ROL": result = Me.ROL(op1)
        Case "ROR": result = Me.ROR(op1)

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Compare
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "CMP": result = Me.CMP(op1)
        Case "CPX": result = Me.CPX(op1)
        Case "CPY": result = Me.CPY(op1)

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Branches (all relative; op1 = target label or hex offset)
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "BCC": result = Me.BCC(op1)
        Case "BCS": result = Me.BCS(op1)
        Case "BEQ": result = Me.BEQ(op1)
        Case "BMI": result = Me.BMI(op1)
        Case "BNE": result = Me.BNE(op1)
        Case "BPL": result = Me.BPL(op1)
        Case "BVC": result = Me.BVC(op1)
        Case "BVS": result = Me.BVS(op1)

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Jumps & Subroutines
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "JMP": result = Me.JMP(op1)
        Case "JSR": result = Me.JSR(op1)
        Case "RTS": result = Me.RTS()
        Case "RTI": result = Me.RTI()
        Case "BRK": result = Me.BRK()

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Flag operations
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "CLC": result = Me.CLC()
        Case "CLD": result = Me.CLD()
        Case "CLI": result = Me.CLI()
        Case "CLV": result = Me.CLV()
        Case "SEC": result = Me.SEC()
        Case "SED": result = Me.SED()
        Case "SEI": result = Me.SEI()

        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        ' Misc / pseudo-ops
        '----------------------------------------------------------------------
        Case "NOP":             result = Me.NOP()
        Case "ORG", "DB", "DS": result = 0          ' assembler directives
        Case "EQU":             result = Me.EQU_(op1, label)
        Case "END":             result = ERR_EXEC_END
        Case "HLT", "STP":     result = Me.HLT()   ' unofficial/WDC stop

        Case Else
            SetError ERR_BAD_OPCODE, "6510 RunOpcode: Unknown opcode: " & opcode
            result = ERR_BAD_OPCODE
    End Select

    RunOpcode = result
End Function
' --- RunOpcode ---
